 Brittene igland is ehta hund mila lang. &amp; twa hund brad. &amp; her sind on &t;is iglande fif ge&t;eode. Englisc. &amp; Brittisc. &amp; Wilsc. &amp; Scyttisc. &amp; Pyhtisc. &amp; Boc Leden. 
 Erest weron bugend &t;ises landes Brittes. &t;a coman of Armenia. &amp; ges&ae;tan su&d;ewearde Bryttene &ae;rost. 
 &T;a gelamp hit &t;&ae;t Pyhtas coman su&t;an of Scithian. mid langum scipum na manegum. &amp; &t;a coman &ae;rost on nor&t; Ybernian up. &amp; &t;&ae;r b&ae;don Scottas &t;&ae;t hi &d;er moston wunian. 
 Ac hi noldan heom lyfan. for&d;an hi cw&ae;don &t;&ae;t hi ne mihton ealle &ae;tg&ae;dere gewunian &t;&ae;r. &amp; &t;a cw&ae;don &t;a Scottas. we eow magon &t;eah hwa&d;ere r&ae;d gel&ae;ron. 
 We witan o&t;er egland her be easton. &t;er ge magon eardian gif ge willa&d;. &amp; gif hwa eow wi&d;stent. we eow fultumia&d;. &t;&ae;t ge hit magon gegangan. 
 &D;a ferdon &t;a Pihtas. &amp; geferdon &t;is land nor&t;anweard. &amp; su&t;anweard hit hefdon Brittas. swa we &ae;r cwedon. 
 And &t;a Pyhtas heom ab&ae;don wif &ae;t Scottum. on &t;a gerad &t;&ae;t hi gecuron heora kyne cinn aa on &t;a wifhealfa. &t;&ae;t hi heoldon swa lange sy&d;&d;an. 
 &amp; &t;a gelamp hit imbe geara rina. &t;&ae;t Scotta sum d&ae;l gewat of Ybernian on Brittene. &amp; &t;es landes sum d&ae;l geeodon. &amp; wes heora heratoga Reoda gehaten. from &t;am heo sind genemnode D&ae;l Reodi. 
 Sixtigum wintrum &ae;r &t;am &t;e Crist were acenned. Gaius Iulius Romana Kasere mid hundehtatigum scipum gesohte Brytene. 
 &T;er he wes &ae;rost geswenced mid grimmum gefeohte. &amp; micelne d&ae;l his heres forl&ae;dde. 
 &amp; &t;a he forlet his here abidan mid Scottum. &amp; gewat into Galwalum. &amp; &t;er gegadorode six hund scipa. mid &t;am he gewat eft in to Brytene. 
 &amp; &t;a hi &ae;rost togedore ger&ae;sdon. &t;a man ofsloh &d;es Caseres gerefan. se wes Labienus gehaten. 
 &D;a genamon &t;a Walas. &amp; adrifon sumre ea ford ealne mid scearpum pilum greatum innan &t;am wetere. sy ea hatte Temese. 
 &T;a &t;&ae;t onfundon &d;a Romani. &t;a noldon hi faron ofer &t;one ford. 
 &T;a flugon &t;a Bryt Walas to &t;am wuduf&ae;stenum. &amp; se Kasere geeode wel manega hehburh mid mycelum gewinne. &amp; eft gewat into Galwalum.

 Her Iustus arcebiscop gehalgode Paulinum to biscope on xii kalend&ae; Augusti. Hic ciclus Dionisii quinque deconnouenalibus constans  hoc est xcv annis. sumitque exordium a xxx anno Incarnationis Domini  et desinit in dc xxvi anno. Hic ordo decennouenalis quem Gr&ae;ci Ennia kai&d; Iohannes papa Kaderida uocat  a Sanctis patribus in Nicea Sinodo fuit constitutus  in quo xiiii luna Paschalis omni anno sine ulla dubitatione. 
 Her com Eomer fram Cwichelme West Seaxna cininge. &t;ohte &t;&ae;t he wolde ofstingan Eadwine cininge. ac he ofstang Lillan his &d;egn. &amp; For&d;here. &amp; &t;one cining gewundode.

 Cwe&d; &t;a &t;et he wolde hit wur&d;minten &amp; arwur&d;en be his bro&d;re r&ae;d &ae;&d;elred &amp; Merwala. &amp; be his swustre red Kyneburges &amp; Kyneswi&d;es. &amp; be se &ae;rcebiscopes r&ae;d se w&ae;s gehaten Deusdedit. &amp; be al his gewiten r&ae;d l&ae;red &amp; lawed &t;e on his kynerice w&ae;ron. &amp; he swa dide.

 &D;a cw&ae;d se kyning to &t;an abbode. La leof S&ae;xulf ic haue geseond &ae;fter &t;e for mine saule &t;urfe. &amp; ic hit wile &t;e w&ae;l secgon for hwi.

 Ic Wulfere gife to d&ae;i Sancte Petre &amp; &t;one abbode Saxulf &amp; &t;a munecas of &t;e mynstre &t;as landes &amp; &t;as wateres &amp; meres &amp; fennes &amp; weres &amp; ealle &t;a landes &t;a &t;&ae;r abuton ligge&d; &d;a of mine kynerice sindon freolice. swa &d;et nan man na haue &t;&ae;r nan onsting buton seo abbot &amp; se muneces. 
 &D;as is se gife: fram Medeshamstede to Nor&d;burh  &amp; to &d;et stede &t;et man cleope&d; Folies. &amp; swa &ae;l se feon riht to Esendic. &amp; fra Esendic to &t;&ae;t steode &t;e man cleope&d; Fe&d;ermude. &amp; swa &t;&ae;t rihte weie x mile lang to Cuggedic. &amp; swa to Raggewilh. 
 &amp; fra Raggewilh v mile to &t;e rihte &ae; &t;e ga&d; to &AE;lm &amp; to Wisebece. &amp; swa abutan iii mile to &T;rokonholt. &amp; fra &T;rokonholt riht &t;urh al &d;e fen to Fereuorde &t;&ae;t is xx mile lang. &amp; swa to Gr&ae;tecros.

 &amp; &t;as meres &amp; laces. Sc&ae;lfremere &amp; Witlesmere &amp; &ae;lle &t;a o&t;re &t;&ae;t &t;ar abutan liggan mid land &amp; mid huses &t;a sindon on &ae;sthalfe Sc&ae;lfremere. &amp; &t;eonen &ae;lle &t;a feonnon to Medeshamstede. 
 &amp; fra Medeshamstede al to Welmes forde. &amp; fra Welmes forde to Cliue. and &t;eonen to &AE;stune. &amp; fra &AE;stune to Stanford. &amp; fra Stanford swa swa &t;&ae;t w&ae;ter renne&d; to seo forensprecone Nor&d;burh. 
 &D;is sindon &t;a landes &amp; &d;a feonnes &t;e seo kyning gef into Sancte Petres mynstre. 
 &D;a cw&ae;&d; seo kyning. Hit is litel &t;eos gife. ac ic wille &t;&ae;t hi hit h&ae;lden swa kynelice &amp; swa freolice. &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;r ne benumen of na geld na gaule. buton to &t;a munecan ane. 
 &D;us ic wille freon &t;is mynstre &t;et hit ne be under&t;ed buton Rome ane. &amp; hider ic wille &t;&ae;t we secan Sancte Petre. ealle &t;a &t;a to Rome na magen faren.

 Her Oswiu &amp; Ecbriht sendon Wigheard preost to Rome. &t;&ae;t hine man scolde halgian to &ae;rcebiscope. ac he for&d;ferde sona swa he &t;ider com. 
 Her Uitalianus se papa gehadode Theodorus to arcebiscop. &amp; sende hine to Brytene. 
 Her Egbriht cining sealde Basse preost Raculf  mynster to tymbrianne. 
 Her Oswiu for&d;ferde Nor&d;anhymbra cining on xv kalend&ae; Marcii &amp; Ecfer&d; his sunu rixade &ae;fter him. &amp; Hlothere feng to biscopdome ofer Weast Seaxum &AE;glbrihtes biscopes nefa. &amp; heold vii gear. &amp; &t;eodorus biscop hine halgode. 
 Her w&ae;s &t;&ae;t mycele fugla well. 
 Her for&d;ferde Cenwalh. &amp; Sexburh an gear rixade his cwen &ae;fter him. 
 Her &AE;gbriht Cantwara cining for&d;ferde. &amp; Theodorus &ae;rcebiscop gesomnode sino&d; &ae;t Heortforde. &amp; Sancte &AE;&d;eldri&t; ongan &t;&ae;t mynster &ae;t Helige.

 Her Wulfhere Pending &amp; &AE;scwine Cenfusing gefuhton &ae;t Bedan heafde. 
 &amp; &t;a ilcan geare Wulfhere for&d;ferde. &amp; &ae;&d;elred feng to rice. 
 On his time &t;a seonde he to Rome Wilfrid biscop to &t;am pape &t;e &t;a wes. Agatho he w&ae;s gehaten. &amp; cydde him mid writ &amp; mid worde. hu his bre&d;re Peada &amp; Wulfhere &amp; se abbot Saxulf heafden wroht an minstre Medeshamstede w&ae;s gehaten. &amp; &t;&ae;t hi hit heafden gefreod wi&d; kyning &amp; wi&d; biscop of ealle &t;ewdom. &amp; bed him &t;&ae;t he scolde &t;&ae;t geten mid his writ &amp; mid his bletsunge. 
 And seo papa seonde &t;a his gewrite to Englalande &t;us cwe&d;ende. Ic Agatho papa of Rome grete wel seo wur&d;fulle &ae;&d;elred Myrcene kyning &amp; se &ae;rcebiscop Theodorum of Cantwarbyrig. &amp; seo Myrcene biscop Saxulf seo &ae;r w&ae;s abbot. &amp; alle &t;a abbotes &t;a sindon on Englalande Godes gretinge &amp; minre bletsunge. 
 Ic haue geheord seo kyninges &ae;&d;elredes geornunge &amp; &t;es &ae;rcebiscopes Theodorus. &amp; &t;es biscopes Saxulfes. &amp; &t;es abbotes Cuthbaldes. &amp; ic hit wille &t;&ae;t hit on &ae;lle wise beo. swaswa ge hit sprecon hauen. 
 And ic bebeode of Godes half &amp; Sancte Petres. &amp; ealra halgan. &amp; ealre hadode heafde. &t;et ne kyning ne biscop ne eorl. ne nan man ne haue nan onsting. ne gafle ne geold ne feording ne nanes cinnes &d;eudom ne nime man of &t;&ae;t abbotrice of Medeshamstede. 
 Ic beode &ae;c &t;&ae;t &t;e scyrbiscop ne seo swa dyrstlece &t;&ae;t he ne hading ne haleging ne do on &t;is abbotrice buton seo abbot hit him bidde. ne biscopwite ne sina&d; ne nanes kinnes &t;ing na haue &t;&ae;r nan onsting. 
 &amp; ic wille &t;&ae;t seo abbot beo gehealden for legat of Rome ofer eal &t;&ae;t iglande. &amp; hwilc abbot &t;e be&t; &t;&ae;r coren of &t;e munecan &t;&ae;t he beo gebletsad of &t;an &ae;rcebiscop of Cantwarbyrig. 
 Ic wille &amp; ty&d;e &t;&ae;t whilc man swa haued behaten to faren to Rome  and he ne muge hit for&d;ian. ou&d;er for untrumnisse  ou&d;er for lauerdes neode. ou&d;er for haueleste. ou&d;er for hwilces cinnes o&d;er neod he ne muge &t;&ae;r cumon. beo he of Englelande ou&d;er of hwilc o&d;er igland beo he. cume to &t;&ae;t mynstre on Medeshamstede. &amp; haue &t;&ae;t ilce forgiuenesse of Criste &amp; Sancte Peter. &amp; of &t;onne abbot &amp; of &t;one muneca &t;&ae;t he scolde hauen gif he to Rome fore. 
 Nu bidde ic &t;e bro&d;er Theodorus &t;&ae;t &t;u lete bedon geond &ae;l Englelande &t;et seo sina&d; wur&d;e gegaderod. &amp; &t;is write wur&d;e geredd &amp; gehealdon. 
 Alswa ic beode &t;e Saxulf biscop &t;&ae;t swa swa &t;u hit geornest. &t;&ae;t seo mynstre beo freo. swa ic forbeode &t;e &amp; ealle &t;e biscopas &t;e &ae;fter &d;e cumon of Criste &amp; of ealle his halgan &t;&ae;t ge nan onsting ne hauen of &t;&ae;t mynstre buton swa micel swa &t;one abbot wile. 
 Nu wille ic hit segge mid worde &t;&ae;t hwa swa halt &t;is write &amp; &t;is bode. &t;a wur&d;e he efre wuniende mid God &ae;lmihti on heuenrice. &amp; hwa swa hit tobrece&d;. &t;a wur&d;e he amansumed &amp; ani&d;rod mid Iudas &amp; mid ealle deofle on helle buton he cume to dedbote. AMEN. 
 &D;as writ seonde seo papa Agatho &amp; an hundred &amp; fif &amp; twenti biscopes bi Wilfrid &ae;rcebiscop of Eoferwic to Englalande. 
 &T;is w&ae;s gedon &ae;fter ure Drihtnes acennednesse dc lxxx &t;es kininges vi gear &ae;&d;elredes. 
 &D;a heot seo kining &t;one &ae;rcebiscop Theodorus &t;&ae;t he scolde setton ealle gewitenemot &ae;t &t;one stede &t;&ae;t man cleope&d; Heatfelde. 
 &D;a hi w&ae;ron &t;&ae;r gegaderod. &t;a leot he r&ae;don &t;a gewrite &t;e seo papa &t;ider seonde. &amp; ealle hit getton &amp; fulfeostnodon. 
 &D;a seide se kyning  Ealle &t;a &t;ing &t;e min bro&d;er Peada. &amp; min bro&d;er Wulfere. &amp; mine swuster Kineburh &amp; Kynesuith geafon &amp; getton Sancte Peter &amp; &t;one abbot &t;a wile ic &t;&ae;t stande. &amp; ic wile on min d&ae;i hit &ae;con for here sawle. &amp; for minre sawle. 
 Nu gife ic Sancte Peter tod&ae;i into his minstre Medeshamstede &t;as landes. &amp; eal &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;r to ligge&d;. &t;et is Bredune. Hrepingas. Cedenac. Swinesh&ae;fed. Heanbyrig. Lodeshac. Scuffanhalch. Costesford. Stretford. W&ae;ttelleburne. Lufgeard. &AE;&t;elhuniglond. Bar&t;anig. 
 &D;as landes ic gife Sancte Peter ealswa freolice swa ic seolf hit ahte. &amp; swa &t;&ae;t nan min &ae;ftergengles &t;&ae;r nan &t;ing of ne nime. 
 Gif hwa hit do&d;. &t;es papa curs of Rome &amp; ealre biscope curs he habbe. &amp; here ealre &t;e her be gewitnesse. &amp; &t;is ic festnie mid Cristes tacne. 
 Ic Theodorus &ae;rcebiscop of Cantwarbyrig am witnesse of &t;as gewrite of Medeshamstede. &amp; ic festnie mid min gewrite. &amp; ic amansumie ealle &t;a &t;&ae;r ani&t;ing ofbreke. &amp; ic bletsie ealle &t;a &t;e hit healden. 
 Ic Wilfrid &ae;rcebiscop of &AE;ferwic ic eam witnesse of &t;as gewrite. &amp; ic g&ae;te &t;&ae;s ilce curs. 
 Ic Saxulf &t;e w&ae;s first abbot &amp; nu eam biscop ic gife hi min curs &amp; ealle min &ae;ftergengle &t;e &t;is tobreket. 
 Ic Ostri&d;e &ae;&d;elredes cwen hit ty&d;e. 
 Ic Adrianus legat hit iete. 
 Ic Putta biscop of Rofecestre ic hit write. 
 Ic Waldhere biscop of Lundene hit festnie. 
 Ic Cu&d;bald abbot hit geate swa &t;et hwa swa hit breket. ealre biscope cursunge &amp; eal Cristene foces he hafe. Amen. 
 Her &AE;scwine for&d;ferde. &amp; Hedde feng to biscopdome. &amp; Centwine feng to West Seaxna rice. &amp; &AE;&d;elred Myrcena cining oferhergode Centland. 
 Her ateowede cometa se steorra on Auguste. &amp; scan iii mon&d;as &ae;lce morgen swilce sunne beam. 
 &amp; Wilfer&d; biscop w&ae;s adrifen of his biscopdome fram Ecfer&d;e cininge. &amp; man gehalgode ii biscopas on his stal. Bosan to Derum. &amp; Eatan to Beornicum. &amp; man gehalgode Lindiswarum to biscope Eadhed. se w&ae;s on Lindissi &ae;rost biscopa. 
 Her man ofsloh &AE;lfwine be Trentan &t;&ae;r &d;&ae;r Egfer&d; &amp; &AE;&d;elred gefuhton. &amp; her for&d;ferde sancte &AE;&d;eldri&d;. &amp; Coludes burh forbarn mid godcundum fyre. 
 Her geset Theodorus &ae;rcebiscopes sino&d; on H&ae;&d;felda. for&t;an &t;e he wolde &t;one Cristes gel&ae;fan gerihtan. &amp; &t;y geare Hild abbo&d;essa on Streonesheale for&d;ferde.

 Her h&ae;t Ecgfer&d; cining gehalgian Cu&d;berht to biscope. &amp; Theodorus archiepiscopus hine gehalgode on Eoferwic &t;am forman Eastord&ae;ge to biscope to Hagustaldesham. for &t;am Trumbriht w&ae;s adon of &d;am biscopdome. 
 &amp; &d;y ilcan geare man ofsloh Ecgfer&d; cining be nor&d;an s&ae;. &amp; mycelne here mid him on xiii kalend&ae; Iunii. 
 He w&ae;s xv winter cining. &amp; Aldfri&d; his bro&d;or feng &ae;fter him to rice. 
 &amp; her ongan Ceadwala winnan &ae;fter rice. 
 &amp; &t;y ilcan geare Lo&d;ere Cantwara cining for&d;ferde. &amp; man gehalgode Iohannes on Augusti to biscope. &amp; he &t;&ae;r w&ae;s o&d;&d;e Wilfri&t; incom.

 &T;a w&ae;s Wilfer&d; his preost sy&d;&d;an gehalgod Ceastre to biscope. &amp; for to his mynstre on Derawuda. 
 Her Ceadwala &amp; Mul his bro&d;or forhergodan Cent &amp; Wiht. 
 &T;&ae;s C&ae;dwala gef into sancte Petres minstre Medeshamstede Hoge. &t;&ae;t is in an igland Heabureahg hatte. 
 &T;a w&ae;s abbot on &t;&ae;re minstre Egbalth w&ae;s gehaten. heo w&ae;s se &t;ridde abbot &ae;fter Saxulfe. &t;a w&ae;s Theodorus &ae;rcebiscop on Cent. 
 Her Mul w&ae;r&d; on Cent b&ae;rned. &amp; o&d;re xii men mid him. &amp; &t;y geara Ceadwala eft forhergode Cent. 
 Her for Ceadwala cining to Rome. &amp; onfeng fulluht &ae;t Sergium &t;am papan. &amp; he him scop Petrum to name. &amp; he sy&d;&d;an ymbe vii niht for&d;ferde on xii kalend&ae; Mai under Cristes cla&d;um. &amp; he w&ae;s gebyrged innan Sancte Petres cyrican.

 &amp; se &ae;&d;eling gehwilcan feoh. &amp; feorh bead  &amp; heo n&ae;nig &t;icgan noldan. ac heo symle feohtende w&ae;ron. o&t; hig ealle ofslagene w&ae;ron. buton anum Brytwyliscum gisle. &amp; se swy&d;e gewundod w&ae;s. 
 &T;a on morgen gehyrdon &t;&ae;t &t;es ciniges &t;egnas &t;e him b&ae;fton w&ae;ron &t;&ae;t se cining ofslagen w&ae;s. &t;a ridon hi &t;ider &amp; his ealdorman Osric. &amp; Wifer&d; his &t;egn. &amp; &t;a men &t;e he him be&ae;fton l&ae;fde &ae;r. &amp; &t;one &ae;&d;eling on &t;&ae;re byrig gemetton &t;&ae;r se cining ofslagen l&ae;g. 
 &amp; heo &t;a gatu heom to belocen h&ae;fdon. &amp; &d;a &d;er toeodon.

 &amp; &t;a cwe&d;on hig. &t;&ae;t heom n&ae;nig m&ae;g leofra n&ae;re &t;one heora hlaford. &amp; heo n&ae;fre his banan folgian noldon.

 On &t;es ilca Offa d&ae;i. w&ae;s an ealdorman Brordan w&ae;s gehaten. he geornde at se kyning. &t;&ae;t he scolde for his luuen freon his ane mynstre Wocingas het. for &t;i &d;et he hit wolde giuen into Medeshamstede. &amp; Sancte Peter. &amp; &t;one abbote &t;e &t;a was. he was Pusa gehaten;

 Karolus in Hispanias intrauit. Karolus Saxoniam uenit. Karolus Pampileniam urbem destruxit  atque Cesar Augustam. exercitum suum coniunxit  et acceptis obsidibus  subiugatis Sarracenis  per Narbonam Wasconiam Franciam rediit.

 Karolus rex imperator factus est  et a Romanis appellatus Augustus; qui illos qui Leonem papam dehonestauerant morte damnauit  sed precibus pap&ae; morte indulta exilio retrusit. Ipse enim papa Leo imperatorem eum sacrauerat.

 Her Ceorl ealdorman gefeaht wi&d; he&d;ene men mid Defenescire &ae;t Wicgeanbeorge. &amp; &t;&ae;r mycel w&ae;l geslogon. &amp; sige namon. 
 &amp; h&ae;&d;ene men on Tenet ofer winter ges&ae;ton. 
 &amp; &t;y ilcan geare com feor&t;e healfhund scipa on Temesemu&t;an. &amp; br&ae;con Cantwareburh. &amp; geflymdon Brihtwulf Myrcena cining mid his fyrde. &amp; foran &t;a su&d; ofer Temese on Su&d;rige. &amp; him gefeaht wi&d; &AE;&d;elwulf cining. &amp; &AE;&d;elbald his sunu &ae;t Aclea mid W&ae;st S&ae;xna fyrde. 
 &amp; &t;&ae;r &t;&ae;t m&ae;ste w&ae;l geslogon on h&ae;&d;ene here &t;e we &ae;fre gesecgan herdon. &amp; &t;&ae;r sige namon. 
 And &t;y ilcan geare &AE;&d;elstan cining. and Ealhere dux gefuhton on scipum. &amp; mycelne here ofslogon &ae;t Sandwic. &amp; ix scipu gefengon &amp; &t;a o&d;re geflymdon. 
 Her on &t;is tima leot Ceolred abbod of Medeshamstede &amp; &t;a munecas Wulfrede to hande &t;et land of Sempigaham  to &t;&ae;t forewearde &t;&ae;t &ae;fter his d&ae;i scolde &t;&ae;t land into &t;e minstre. &amp; Wulfred scolde gifen &t;&ae;t land of Sliowaforda into Medeshamstede. 
 &amp; he scolde gife ilca gear into &t;e minstre sixtiga fo&d;ra wuda. &amp; tw&ae;lf fo&d;ur gr&ae;fan. &amp; sex fo&d;ur gearda. &amp; twa tunnan fulle hlutres alo&d;. &amp; twa sl&ae;gn&ae;t. &amp; sex hund hlafes. &amp; ten mittan W&ae;lsces alo&d;. &amp; ilca gear an hors &amp; &t;rittiga scillinga. &amp; ane n&ae;ht gefeormige. 
 Her w&ae;s wi&d; se cining Burhred. &amp; Ceolred &ae;rcebiscop. and Tunberht biscop. &amp; Cenred biscop. &amp; Alhhun biscop. &amp; Berhtred biscop. &amp; Wihtred abbod. &amp; Werhtherd abbod. &AE;&d;elheard ealdorman. Hunberht ealdorman. &amp; feola o&d;re. 
 Her Burhred Myrcene cyning under&d;eodde him Nor&d; Wealas mid &AE;&t;elwulfes cininge fultume. 
 &amp; &t;y ilcan geare Ealhhere mid Cantwarum. &amp; Huda mid Su&d;rigum gefuhton on Tenet wi&d; h&ae;&d;ene here. &amp; &t;&ae;r w&ae;ron feala ofsl&ae;gene. &amp; adruncen on &ae;g&d;re hand. &amp; &t;a ealdormen bege d&ae;de. 
 &amp; Burhred Myrcene cining feng to &AE;&d;elwulfes dohtor West Seaxna cininges. 
 Her h&ae;&t;ene men &ae;rest on Sceapege ofer winter s&ae;ton. 
 &amp; &t;y ilcan geare gebocade &AE;&d;elwulf cining teo&d;an d&ae;l his landes ofer eal his rice Gode to lofe. &amp; him selfum ecre h&ae;le. 
 And &t;y ilcan geare ferde to Rome mid mycclum wur&d;scipe. &amp; &t;&ae;r wunade xii mona&d;. &amp; he feng to Karles dohter Francna cining &t;a he hamweard w&ae;s. &amp; gesund ham com. 
 &amp; &t;&ae;s ymbe ii gear for&d;ferde. &amp; his lic li&d; on Wintanceastre. &amp; he rixade ix gear. 
 He w&ae;s Ecgbrihting. &amp; &t;a fengon his ii sunu to rice. &AE;&d;elbald to West Seaxna rice. and to Su&d;rigean. &amp; he rixade v gear. 
 Her &AE;&d;elbald cining for&d;ferde. &amp; his lic li&d; &ae;t Scireburnan. &amp; feng &AE;&d;elbriht to eallum &t;am rice his bro&d;or. 
 &amp; on his d&ae;ge com mycel sciphere up. &amp; abr&ae;con Wintanceastre. &amp; wi&d; &t;one here fuhton Osric ealdorman mid Hamtunescire. &amp; &AE;&d;elwulf ealdorman mid Barrucscire  &amp; &t;one here geflymdon. &amp; w&ae;lstowe geweald ahton. 
 &amp; se &AE;&d;elbriht rixade v gear. &amp; his lic li&d; &ae;t Scirburnan. 
 Her s&ae;t se h&ae;&d;ene here on Tenet  &amp; genam fri&d; wi&d; Cantwarum. &amp; Cantware heom feoh beheton wi&d; &d;am fri&d;e. &amp; on &t;am feohbehate se here hine on niht up best&ae;l. &amp; oferhergode ealle Cent eastewarde. 
 Her feng &AE;&d;elred &AE;&d;elbrihtes bro&d;or to West Seaxna rice. And &t;y ilcan geare com mycel h&ae;&d;en here on Angelcynnes land. &amp; wintersetle namon &ae;t East Englum. &amp; &t;&ae;r gehorsade wurdon. &amp; hi heom wi&d; fri&d; genamon. 
 Her for se here of East Englum ofer Hymbre mu&d;an. to Eoferwicceastre on Nor&d;anhumbre. 
 &amp; &t;&ae;r w&ae;s mycel un&d;w&ae;rnesse &d;ere &t;eode betwux heom sylfum. &amp; hi h&ae;fdon heora cining aworpene Osbriht. &amp; ungecynde cining underfengon &AE;llan.

 &amp; &t;a ceastre br&ae;con. &amp; hi sume inne wurdon. &amp; &t;&ae;r w&ae;s ungemet w&ae;l gesl&ae;gen Nor&d;anhymbra  sume binnan  sume butan. &amp; &t;a ciningas b&ae;gen ofsl&ae;gene. &amp; seo lafe wi&d; &t;one here fry&d; nam.

 Her for se ilca here innan Myrce to Snotingham &amp; &t;&ae;r wintersetle namon. 
 And Burhcred Myrcena cining and his witan b&ae;don &ae;&d;elred West Seaxna cining &amp; &ae;lfred his bro&d;or &t;et hi him fultumedon. &t;&ae;t hi wi&d; &t;one here gefuhton.

 Her rad se here to Readingum on Westseaxe. &amp; &t;es ymb iii niht ridon twegen eorlas up. &t;a gemette &AE;&d;elwulf ealdorman hie on Englafelda. &amp; heom &t;&ae;r wi&d; gefeaht &amp; sige nam. &amp; wear&d; &t;&ae;r se o&t;er ofsl&ae;gen. &t;&ae;s nama w&ae;s Sidrac.

 &amp; &t;&ae;r w&ae;s mycel w&ae;l gesl&ae;gen on gehwa&d;ere hand. &amp; &AE;&d;elwulf ealdorman wear&d; ofsl&ae;gen. &amp; &t;a Deniscan ahton w&ae;lstowe geweald. 
 And ymb iiii niht gefeaht &AE;&d;ered cining. &amp; &AE;lfred his bro&d;or wi&d; ealne &d;one here on &AE;scesdune. 
 &amp; hi w&ae;ron on twam gefylcum. on o&d;rum wes Basecg &amp; Halfdene &d;a h&ae;&d;ene ciningas. &amp; on o&d;rum w&ae;ron &t;a eorlas. 
 &amp; &t;a feaht se cining &AE;&d;ered wi&d; &d;ara cininga getruman. &amp; &t;&ae;r wear&d; se cining Bagsecg ofsl&ae;gen. &amp; &AE;lfred his bro&d;or wi&d; &t;ara eorla getruman  &amp; &t;&ae;r wear&d; Sidrac eorl ofsl&ae;gen se ealda. &amp; Sidrac se geonga  &amp; Osbearn eorl. &amp; Fr&ae;na eorl. &amp; Harold eorl.

 &amp; &ae;fter &t;isum gefeohte com mycel sumerlida to Readingum. &amp; &t;&ae;s &ae;fter Eastron gefor &AE;&d;ered cining. &amp; he rixade v gear. &amp; his lic li&d; &ae;t Winburnan mynster. 
 &D;a feng &AE;lfred &AE;&d;elwulfing his bro&d;or to West Seaxna rice. 
 &amp; &t;&ae;s ymb i mona&d; gefeaht &ae;lfred cining wi&d; ealne &t;one here litle werede &ae;t Wiltune. &amp; hine lange on d&ae;g geflymde. &amp; &t;a Deniscan ahton w&ae;lstowe geweald. 
 &amp; &t;es geares wurdon ix folcgefeoht gefohten wi&d; &t;one here on &t;am cinerice besu&d;an Temese. butan &t;am &t;e him &AE;lfred &t;es cinges bro&d;er. &amp; ealdormen. &amp; ciningas &t;&ae;gnas oft rada on riden &t;e man na ne rimde  &amp; &t;&ae;s geares w&ae;ron ofslagene ix eorlas. &amp; an cyning.

 Her for se here to Lundenbyrig fram Redingum. &amp; &t;&ae;r nam wintersetle. &amp; &t;a naman Myrce fri&d; wi&d; &t;one here.

 Her for se here of Lindesse to Hreopedune. &amp; &t;&ae;r wintersetle nam. &amp; &t;one cining Burgred ofer s&ae; adrefdon ymb xxii wintra &t;&ae;s &t;e he rice h&ae;fde. &amp; &t;et land eall geeodan. 
 &amp; he for to Rome &amp; &t;&ae;r s&ae;t. &amp; his lic li&d; on sancta Marian cyrican on Angelcynnes scole.

 &amp; he him a&d;as swor &amp; gislas sealde. &t;et hit him georo w&ae;re swa hwilce d&ae;ge swa hi hit habban woldon. &amp; he geare w&ae;re mid him sylfum. &amp; mid eallum &t;am &t;e him gel&ae;stan wolden to &t;&ae;s heres &t;&ae;rfe. 
 Her for se here fram Hreopedune. &amp; Healfdene for mid sumum &t;am here on Nor&d;anhymbre. &amp; nam wintersetle be Tinan &t;&ae;re ea. 
 &amp; se here &t;et land geeode. &amp; oft gehergode on Pehtas. &amp; on Str&ae;tl&ae;d Wealas.

 Her hine best&ae;l se here into W&ae;rham West Seaxna fyrde. 
 &amp; si&d;&d;an wi&d; &t;one here se cyning fri&d; nam. &amp; him &t;a gislas sealdon &t;e on &t;am here weor&t;uste w&ae;ron to &t;am cyninge. &amp; him &t;a a&d;as sworon on &t;am halgan beage  &t;e hi &ae;r nanre &t;eode don noldon &t;et hi hredlice of his rice foron.

 Rollo cum suis Normaniam penetrauit et regnauit annis liii. 
 Her com se here to Exanceastre fram Werham. 
 &amp; se sciphere seglode west ymbutan. &amp; &t;a gemette hi mycel yst on s&ae;. &amp; &t;ear forwear&d; cxx scipa &ae;t Swanawic.

 &amp; hi him &t;ar foregislas sealdon swa feala swa he habban wolde. &amp; mycele a&d;as sworon. &amp; &t;a godne fri&d; heoldan. 
 &amp; &t;a on herfeste gefor se here on Myrcenaland. &amp; hit ged&ae;ldon sum. and sum Ceolwulfe sealdon. 
 Her hine best&ae;l se here on midne winter ofer twelftan niht to Cippanhamme. &amp; geridan West Seaxna land &amp; gesetton. &amp; mycel &t;&ae;s folces ofer s&ae; adr&ae;fdon. &amp; &t;&ae;s o&d;res &t;one m&ae;stan d&ae;l hi geridon butan &t;am cynge &AE;lfrede litle werede uny&d;elice &ae;fter wudum for. &amp; on morfestenum. 
 &amp; &t;es ilcan wintra w&ae;s Iweres bro&d;or &amp; Healfdenes on West Sexum on Defenanscire. &amp; hine mon &t;&ae;r sloh. &amp; dccc manna mid him. &amp; xl manna his heres. &amp; &t;ar w&ae;s se gu&d;fana genumen &t;e hi r&ae;fen heton.

 &amp; he for ymb ane niht of &t;am wicum to &AE;glea. &amp; &t;&ae;s ymb ane niht to e&d;andune. &amp; &t;&ae;r gefeaht wi&d; ealne here &amp; hine geflymde. &amp; him &ae;fter rad o&d; &t;et geweorc. &amp; &t;&ae;r s&ae;t xiiii niht. 
 &amp; &t;a sealde se here him gislas. and mycele a&d;as. &t;et hi of his rice woldon. &amp; him eac geheton &t;et heora cyng fulwihte onfon wolde. &amp; hi &t;&ae;t gel&ae;ston. 
 &amp; &t;&ae;s ymb iii wucan com se cyng Godrum. &t;rittigum sum. &t;ara manna &t;e in &t;am here weor&d;uste w&ae;ron &ae;t Alre. &amp; &t;&ae;t is wi&d; &ae;&d;elinga ige. 
 &amp; his se cyng onfeng &t;&ae;r &ae;t fulwihte. &amp; his crismlysing w&ae;s &ae;t Wedmor. &amp; he wes xii niht mid &t;am cynge. &amp; he hine mycclum &amp; his geferan mid feo weor&d;ode. 
 Her for se here to Cirenceastre of Cippanhamme. &amp; s&ae;t &t;&ae;r an winter. &t;y geare gegaderodon an hlo&d; wicinga. &amp; ges&ae;t &ae;t Fullanhamme be Temese. &amp; &t;y ilcan geare a&t;ystrode seo sunne an tid d&ae;ges. 
 Her for se here of Cirenceastre on East Engle. &amp; ges&ae;t &t;&ae;t land &amp; ged&ae;lde. &amp; &t;y ilcan geare for se here ofer s&ae; &t;e on Fullanhamme s&ae;t on Frangland to Gent. &amp; s&ae;t &t;&ae;r an gear. 
 Her for se here ufor on Frangland. &amp; &t;a Francan him wi&d; gefuhton. &amp; &t;&ae;r &t;a war&d; se here horsad &ae;fter &t;am gefeohte.

 &amp; hi &t;&ae;r Godes &t;ances swy&d;e bentig&d;e w&ae;ron &ae;fter &t;am gehatum.

 &amp; hi &t;eah &t;a ceastre aweredan o&d;&d;et &ae;lfred cyng com uton mid fyrde.

 Her for se here up &t;urh &d;a brycge &ae;t Paris. &amp; &t;a up andlang Sigene o&d; M&ae;terne. &amp; &t;a up on M&ae;terne o&d; Caziei. &amp; &t;a s&ae;ton &t;ar innan Ionan twa winter on &d;am twam stedum. 
 &amp; &t;y ilcan geare for&d;ferde Carl Francena cyng. &amp; Earnulf his bro&d;orsunu hine vi wucan &ae;r he for&d;ferde ber&ae;dde &ae;t &t;am rice. 
 &amp; &t;a wear&d; &t;et rice tod&ae;led on v &amp; fif cyningas to gehalgode. &t;et weas &t;&ae;h mid Earnulfes &t;afunge. 
 &amp; hi cw&ae;&d;on &t;&ae;t hi him &t;et to handa healdan scoldan. for&d;an &t;et heora nan n&ae;s of f&ae;drenhalfe geboren butan him anum. 
 Earnulf wunode on &t;am lande be &ae;stan Rine. &amp; Hro&d;ulf &t;a feng to &t;am middelrice. &amp; O&t;a &t;a to &t;am weastd&ae;le. &amp; Beorngar &amp; Wi&d;a to Langbeardnalande. &amp; to &t;am landum on &t;a healfe muntes. 
 &amp; &t;et heoldan mid mycel unsibbe. &amp; twa folcgefeoht gefuhton. &amp; &t;&ae;t land oft &amp; gelome forhergodon. &amp; &ae;ghwe&d;er o&d;erne oft r&ae;dlice utadr&ae;fde. 
 &amp; &t;y ilcan geare &t;e se here for for&d; up ofer &t;a brycge &ae;t Paris. &AE;&d;elhelm ealdorman l&ae;dde Weast Seaxna &ae;lmessan &amp; &AE;lfredes cyninges to Rome. 
 Her l&ae;dde Beocca ealdorman West Seaxna &ae;lmessan &amp; &AE;lfredes cyninges to Rome. &amp; &AE;&d;elswi&d; cw&ae;n seo w&ae;s &AE;lfredes swustor cyninges. &amp; heo for&d;ferde. &amp; hire lic li&d; &ae;t Pauian.

 Hic Plegemundus archiepiscopus a Deo et omni populo electus est. 
 Her for se myccla here &t;e we gefyrn &ae;r ymbspr&ae;con eft of &t;am eastrice weastward to Bunan. &amp; &t;&ae;r wurdon gescipode swa &t;&ae;t hi as&ae;tton hi on &ae;nne si&d; ofer mid horsum mid ealle.

 He wear&d; wide  geond &t;eodland  swi&d;e geweor&d;ad  for&t;am &t;e he weor&d;ode Godes naman georne  &amp; Godes lage smeade  oft &amp; gelome  &amp; Godes lof r&ae;rde  wide &amp; side  &amp; wislice r&ae;dde  oftost a simle for Gode &amp; for worulde  eall his &t;eode. 
 Ane misd&ae;da he dyde &t;eah to swi&d;e  &t;&ae;t he &ae;l&t;eodige unsida lufode &amp; h&ae;&d;ene &t;eawas innan &t;ysan lande gebrohte to f&ae;ste  &amp; utl&ae;ndisce hider in tihte  &amp; deoriende leoda bespeon to &t;ysan earde.

 Com &t;a to &t;e cyng  &amp; leot him locon &t;a gewrite &t;e &ae;r w&ae;ron gefunden. 
 And se kyng andswerode &t;a &amp; cwed. Ic &AE;dgar geate &amp; gife tod&ae;i toforen Gode &amp; toforen &t;one &ae;rcebiscop Dunstan freodom Sancte Petres mynstre Medeshamstede of kyng  &amp; of biscop. &amp; ealle &t;a &t;orpes &t;e &d;&ae;rto lin. &t;&ae;t is &AE;stfeld. &amp; Dodesthorp. &amp; Ege. &amp; Pastun. 
 &amp; swa ic hit freo &t;et nan biscop ne haue &t;&ae;r nane h&ae;se  buton se abbot of &t;one minstre. 
 And ic gife &t;one tun &t;e man cleopa&d; Vndela  mid eall &t;et &t;&ae;r to li&d;  &t;&ae;t is &t;et man cleope&d; Eahte hundred. &amp; market &amp; toll  swa freolice &t;&ae;t ne king ne biscop ne eorl ne scyrreue ne haue &t;&ae;r nane h&ae;se. ne nan man buton se abbot ane  &amp; &t;am &t;e he &t;&ae;rto s&ae;t. 
 And ic gife Crist &amp; Sancte Peter  &amp; &t;urh &t;es biscop bene A&d;elwold. &t;as land. &t;&ae;t is Barwe. Wermigtun. &AE;sctun. Ketering. Castra. Egleswur&d;e. Waltun. Wi&d;ringtun. Ege. Thorp. &amp; an myneter in Stanfor&d;. 
 &D;as land &amp; ealla &t;a o&d;re &t;e lin into &t;e mynstre &t;a cwede ic scyr. &t;&ae;t is saca &amp; socne. toll &amp; team &amp; infangen&t;ef. 
 &T;as rihting &amp; ealle o&d;re &d;a cwe&d;e ic scyr Crist &amp; Sancte Peter.

 &D;a andswerade se arcebiscop Dunstan of Cantwarbyrig &amp; s&ae;ide. Ic ty&d;e &t;&ae;t ealle &t;a &t;ing &t;e her is gifen &amp; sprecon. &amp; ealle &t;a &t;ing &t;e &t;in forgengles &amp; min geatton. &t;a wille ic &t;&ae;t hit stande. 
 &amp; swahwaswa hit tobreco&d;. &t;a gife ic him Godes curs &amp; ealra halgan &amp; eallre hadede heafde &amp; min. buton he cume to d&ae;dbote.

 Her w&ae;s &AE;lfstan biscop. A&t;ulf biscop. &amp; Escwi abbot. &amp; Osgar abbot. &amp; &AE;&t;elgar abbot. &amp; &AE;lfere ealdorman. &AE;&d;elwine ealdorman. Brihtno&t;. Oslac ealdorman. &amp; feola o&d;re rice men. &amp; ealle hit geatton. &amp; ealle hit writen mid Cristes m&ae;l.

 &amp; &t;a on &t;ere nihte &d;e hi on &d;one d&ae;i tog&ae;dere cumon sceoldon. &d;a sceoc he on niht fram &t;&ae;re fyrde him sylfum to mycclum bismore. &amp; se here &t;a &ae;tb&ae;rst  buton an scip &t;&ae;r man ofsloh. 
 &amp; &t;a gem&ae;tte se here &d;a scipu of East Englum &amp; of Lunden. &amp; hi &d;&ae;r ofslogon mycel w&ae;l. &amp; &t;&ae;t scip genamon eall gew&ae;pnod &amp; gew&ae;dod &t;e se ealdorman on w&ae;s. 
 &amp; &d;a &ae;fter Oswaldes arcebiscop for&d;si&d;e. feng Ealdulf abbot of Burch to Eoferwicstole and to Wigeraceastre. &amp; Kenulf to &t;am abbotrice &ae;t Burch. 
 Her on &d;issum geare w&ae;s B&ae;bbanburh tobrocon. &amp; mycel herehu&d;e &t;&ae;r genumen  &amp; &ae;fter &t;am com to Humbranmu&d;e se here. &amp; &t;&ae;r mycel yfel gewrohtan &ae;g&d;er ge on Lindesige ge on Nor&d;hymbran. 
 &T;a gegaderode man swi&d;e mycele fyrde. &amp; &t;a hi tog&ae;dere gan sceoldan. &t;a onstealdon &t;a heretogan &ae;rest &t;one fleam. &t;&ae;t w&ae;s Fr&ae;na. &amp; Godwine. &amp; Fri&d;egist. 
 On &t;ysum ilcan geare het se cyng ablendan &AE;lfgar &AE;lfrices sunu ealdormannes. 
 Her on &t;isum geare com Anlaf &amp; Swegen to Lundenbyrig on Nativitas sancte Marie mid iiii &amp; hundnigontigum scipum. 
 &amp; hi &d;a on &d;a burh festlice feohtende w&ae;ron. &amp; eac hi mid fyre ontendan woldon. ac hi &t;ar gefeordon maran hearm &amp; yfel &t;onne hi &ae;fre wendon. &t;&ae;t heom &ae;nig burhwaru gedon sceolde. 
 Ac se halige Godes modor on &d;am hire mildheortnisse &t;&ae;re burhware gecy&d;de. &amp; hi ahredde wi&d; heora feondum. 
 &amp; hi &t;anon ferdon. &amp; wrohton &t;&ae;t m&ae;ste yfel &t;e &ae;fre &ae;nig here don mihte on b&ae;rnette &amp; hergunge &amp; on manslihtum &ae;g&d;er be &d;am s&ae;riman on East Seaxum  &amp; on Centlande. &amp; on Su&d;Seaxum. &amp; on Hamtunscire. 
 &amp; &ae;t nyxtan naman heom hors. &amp; ridon swa wide swa hi woldon. &amp; unasecgendlice yfel wircende w&ae;ron. 
 &T;a ger&ae;dde se cyng &amp; his witan &t;&ae;t him man to sende. &amp; him gafol behete &amp; metsunge wi&d; &t;on &t;e hi &t;&ae;re hergunge geswicon. 
 &amp; hi &t;a &t;et underfengon. &amp; com &t;a eall se here to Hamtune. &amp; &t;&ae;r wintersetle namon. 
 &amp; hi man &t;&ae;r f&ae;dde geond eall West Seaxna rice. &amp; him man geald xvi &t;usend punda. 
 &T;a sende se cyng &ae;fter Anlafe cyninge  &AE;lfeach biscop &amp; &AE;&d;elward ealdorman &amp; man gislade &t;a hwile in to &t;am scipum. 
 &amp; hi &t;a l&ae;ddan Anlaf mid mycclum wur&d;scipe to &t;am cynge to Andeferan. &amp; se cyng &ae;&d;elred his anfeng &ae;t biscopes handa. &amp; him cynelice gifode. &amp; him &t;a Anlaf behet swa he hit eac gel&ae;ste. &t;&ae;t he n&ae;fre eft to Angelcynne mid unfri&d;e cumon nolde. 
 Hic Ricardus uetus obiit. et Ricardus filius eius suscepit regnum. et regnauit xxxi annos. 
 Her on &t;issum geare &ae;teowde cometa se steorra. &amp; Siric arcebiscop for&d;ferde. 
 Her on &t;issum geare w&ae;s &ae;lfric gehalgod to arcebiscope to Cristes cyrcean. 
 Her on &t;issum geare ferde se here abutan Defnanscire into S&ae;fernmu&d;on. &amp; &t;&ae;r gehergodon &ae;g&d;er on Cornwealum ge on Nor&d;walum. &amp; on Defenan. &amp; eodon him &t;a up &ae;t Wecedport. 
 &amp; &t;&ae;r mycel yfel wrohtan on b&ae;rnette. &amp; on manslihtum. &amp; &ae;fter &t;am wendon eft abutan Penwiht steort on &d;a su&d;healfe. and wendon &t;a in to Tamermu&d;an. &amp; eodon &t;a up o&d; &t;&ae;t hi comon to Hlidaforda. 
 &amp; &ae;lc &t;ing b&ae;rndon &amp; slogon &t;&ae;t hi gemetton. &amp; Ordulfes mynster &ae;t Tefingstoce forb&ae;rndon. &amp; unasecgendlice herehu&d;e mid him to scipa brohtan. 
 Her gewende se here eft eastweard into Frommu&d;an. &amp; &t;&ae;r &ae;ghw&ae;r up eodon swa wide swa hi woldon into Dors&ae;tan. 
 &amp; man oft fyrde ongean hi gegaderode. ac sona swa hi tog&ae;dere gan sceoldan. &t;onne wear&d; &t;&ae;r &ae;fre &t;urh sum &t;ing fleam astiht. &amp; &ae;fre hi &ae;t ende sige ahton. 
 &amp; &t;onne o&d;re hwile lagen heom on Wihtlande. &amp; eoton heom &t;a hwile of Hamtunscire. &amp; of Su&d;seaxum. 
 Her com se here eft abuton into Temese. &amp; wendon &t;a up andlang Medew&ae;gan to Hrofeceastre. 
 &amp; com &t;a seo Centisce fyrde &t;&ae;r ongean. &amp; hi &t;&ae;r f&ae;ste togedere fengon. ac wala &t;&ae;t hi to hra&d;e bugon. &amp; flugon. for&t;am &t;e hi n&ae;fdon fultum &t;e hi habban sceoldan. 
 &T;a ahton &t;a D&ae;niscan w&ae;lstowe geweald &amp; naman &t;a hors. &amp; ridan swa wide swa hi woldon sylf. &amp; forn&ae;h ealle Weast Centingas fordydon. &amp; forhergodan. 
 &D;a r&ae;dde se cyng wi&d; his witan &t;&ae;t man sceolde mid scipfyrde. &amp; eac mid landfyrde him ongean faran. ac &d;a &t;a scipu gearwe w&ae;ron. &t;a elkede man fram d&ae;ge to d&ae;ge. &amp; swencte &t;&ae;t earme folc &t;e on &d;am scipon lagon. 
 &amp; a swa hit for&d;wearde beon scolde. swa hit l&ae;tre w&ae;s fram anre tyde to o&d;re. &amp; a hi leton heora feonda w&ae;rod wexan. &amp; a man rymde fram &t;&ae;re s&ae;. &amp; hi ferdon &ae;fre for&d; &ae;fter. 
 &amp; &t;onne &ae;t &t;am ende ne beheold hit nan &t;ing seo scipfyrding. buton folces geswinc. &amp; feos spilling. &amp; heora feonda for&d;bylding. 
 Her on &d;issum geare se cyng ferde in to Cumerlande. &amp; hit swi&d;e neah eall forhergode. 
 &amp; his scipu wendon ut abuton Legceastre. and sceoldan cumon ongean hine. ac hi ne mihton. &t;a gehergodon hi M&ae;nige. 
 &amp; seo unfri&d;flota w&ae;s &t;&ae;s sumeres gewend to Ricardesrice. 
 Her com se here to Exanmu&d;an. &amp; up &d;a eodan to &d;ere byrig. &amp; &t;&ae;r f&ae;stlice feohtende w&ae;ron. ac him man swy&d;e f&ae;stlice wi&d; stod. &amp; heardlice. 
 &D;a gewendon hi geond &t;&ae;t land. &amp; dydon eall swa hi bewuna w&ae;ron. slogon &amp; beorndon. 
 &T;a gesomnode man &t;&ae;r orm&ae;te fyrde of Defenisces folces. &amp; Sumors&ae;tisces. &amp; hi &d;a tosomne comon &ae;t Peonnho. 
 &amp; sona swa hi tog&ae;dere fengon. &t;a beah seo Englisce fyrd. &amp; hi &t;&ae;r mycel w&ae;l ofslogon. &amp; ridan &t;a ofer &t;&ae;t land. &amp; w&ae;s &ae;fre heora &ae;ftra sy&d; wyrse &t;onne se &ae;rra. 
 &amp; mid him &t;a mycele herehu&d;e to scipon brohton. &amp; &t;anon wendon in Wihtland. &amp; &t;&ae;r him ferdon on buton swa swa hi sylf woldon. &amp; him nan &t;ing ne wi&d;stod. 
 Ne him to ne dorste sciphere on s&ae;. ne landfyrd. ne eodon hi swa feor up. 
 W&ae;s hit &t;a on &ae;lce wisan hefig tyma. for&d;am &t;e hi n&ae;fre heora yfeles geswicon. 
 Her on &t;issum geare se cyng ger&ae;dde &amp; his witan. &t;&ae;t man sceolde gafol gyldon &t;am flotan. &amp; fri&d; wi&d; hi geniman wi&d; &t;on &t;e hi heora yfeles geswican sceoldan. 
 &D;a sende se cyng to &t;am flotan Leofsig ealdorman. &amp; he &t;a &t;&ae;s cynges worde &amp; his witena gri&d; wi&d; hi ges&ae;tte. &amp; &t;et hi to metsunge fengon &amp; to gafle. 
 &amp; hi &t;a &t;&ae;t underfengon. &amp; him man &t;a geald xxiiii &t;usend punda. 
 &D;a on gemang &t;ysum ofsloh Leofsig ealdorman &AE;fic &t;&ae;s cynges heahgerefan. &amp; se cyng hine &d;a geutode of earde. 
 And &t;a on &t;am ilcan lengtene com seo hl&ae;fdige Ricardes dohtor hider to lande. 
 On &d;am ilcan sumera Ealdulf arcebiscop for&d;ferde. 
 &amp; on &d;am geare se cyng het ofslean ealle &d;a Deniscan men &t;e on Angelcynne w&ae;ron on Bricius messed&ae;g. for&t;on &t;am cynge w&ae;s gecydd &t;&ae;t hi woldon hine besyrewian &ae;t his life. &amp; sy&d;&d;an ealle his witan. &amp; habban sy&t;&d;an his rice. 
 Her w&ae;s Eaxeceaster abrocen &t;urh &t;one Frenciscan ceorl Hugon &t;e seo hlefdige heafde hire gesett to gerefan. &amp; se here &t;a burh mid ealle fordyde. &amp; mycele here hu&d;e &t;&ae;r genamen. 
 &D;a gegaderode man swi&d;e mycele fyrde of Wiltunscire &amp; of Hamtunscire. &amp; swi&d;e anr&ae;dlice wi&d; &t;&ae;s heres weard w&ae;ron. 
 &D;a sceolde se ealdorman &ae;lfric l&ae;dan &t;a fyrde. ac he teah for&d; &t;a his ealdan wrenceas. 
 Sona swa hi w&ae;ron swa gehende &t;et &ae;g&d;er heora on o&d;er hawede. &t;a gebr&ae;d he hine seocne. &amp; ongan hine brecan to spiwenne. &amp; cwe&d; &t;et he gesiclod w&ae;re. &amp; swa &t;&ae;t folc beswac &t;&ae;t he l&ae;dan sceolde. 
 Swa hit gecwe&d;en is. &d;onne se heretoga waca&d; &t;onne bi&d; eall se here swi&d;e gehindred. 
 &D;a Swegen geseah &t;&ae;t hi anr&ae;de n&ae;ron. &amp; ealle tohwurfon. &t;a l&ae;dde he his here into Wiltune. 
 &amp; hi &d;a burh gehergodon &amp; forb&ae;rndon. &amp; eodon &t;a to Searbyrig. &amp; &t;anon eft to s&ae;. ferde &t;&ae;r he wiste his y&d;hengestas. 
 Her com Swegen mid his flotan to Nor&d;wic. &amp; &t;a burh ealle gehergade. &amp; forb&ae;rndon. 
 &T;a ger&ae;dde Ulfkytel wi&d; &t;a witan on East Englum. &t;&ae;t him b&ae;tere weron &t;&ae;t man wi&d; &t;one here fri&d;es ceapode. &ae;r hi to mycelne hearm on &t;am earde gedydon. for&t;am &t;e hi unwares comon. &amp; he fyrst n&ae;fde &t;&ae;t he his fyrde gegadrian mihte. 
 &D;a under &t;am gri&d;e &t;e heom betweonan beon sceolde. &t;a besteal se here up fram scipon. &amp; wendan heora fore to &t;eodforda. 
 &D;a Ulfcytel &t;&ae;t undergeat. &t;a seonde he &t;&ae;t man sceolde &t;a scipu toheawan. ac hi abru&d;on &t;a &d;e he to &t;ohte. &amp; he &t;a gegaderode his fyrde diglice swa he swy&d;ost muhte. 
 &amp; se here com &t;a to &t;eodforda binnon iii wuca &t;&ae;s &t;e hi &ae;r gehergodon Nor&d;wic. &amp; &t;&ae;r binnon ane niht w&ae;ron. &amp; &t;a burh hergodon &amp; forb&ae;rndon. 
 &T;a on morgen &t;a hi to scipum woldon. &t;a com Ulfcytel mid his werode. &amp; hi &t;&ae;r tog&ae;dere feastlice fengon. &amp; mycel w&ae;l &t;&ae;r on &ae;g&d;&ae;re hand gefeoll. 
 &D;&ae;r w&ae;r&d; East Engla folces seo yld ofslagen. ac gif &t;et fulle m&ae;gen &t;&ae;re w&ae;re. ne eodan hi n&ae;fre eft to scipon. swa hi sylfe s&ae;don. 
 Her on &t;yssum geare w&ae;s se mycla hungor geond Angelcynn swilce nan man &ae;r ne gemunde swa grimne. &amp; se flota &t;&ae;s geares gewende of &t;issum earde to D&ae;nemearcon. and litelne fyrst let. &t;et he eft ne com. 
 Her for&d;ferde &AE;lfric arcebiscop. &amp; &AE;lfeah biscop feng &ae;fter him to &d;am &ae;rcestole. &amp; Brihtwold biscop feng to &t;am rice on Wiltunscire. 
 &amp; Wulfgeate w&ae;s eall his are ofgenumen. &amp; Wulfeah &amp; Ufegeat w&ae;ron ablende. &amp; &AE;lfelm ealdorman wear&d; ofslagen. &amp; Kenulf biscop for&d;ferde. 
 &amp; &t;a ofer &t;one midne sumor com &t;a se Denisca flota to Sandwic. &amp; dydon eall swa hi &ae;r gewuna w&ae;ron  hergodon &amp; b&ae;rndon. &amp; slogon swa swa hi ferdon. 
 &T;a het se cyng abannan ut ealne &d;eodscipe of Westseaxum. &amp; of Myrcean. &amp; hi lagon ute &t;a ealne &t;one herfest on fyrdinge ongean &t;one here. ac hit naht ne beheold &t;e ma &t;e hit oftor &ae;r dyde. 
 Ac for eallum &t;issum se here ferde swa he sylf wolde. &amp; se fyrdinge dyde &t;&ae;re landleode &ae;lcne hearm. &t;et him na&d;or ne dohte ne innhere ne uthere. 
 &D;a hit winter leohte. &t;a ferde se fyrd ham. 
 &amp; se here com &t;a ofer Martinus messan to his fry&d;stole to Wihtlande. &amp; tilode him &t;&ae;r &ae;ghwer &t;&ae;s &d;e hi behofdan. 
 &amp; &t;a to &d;am middan wintran eodon heom to heora garwan feorme ut &t;urh Hamtunscire into Barrucscire to R&ae;dingan. and hi dydon heora gewuna  atendon heora beacna swa swa hi ferdon. 
 &amp; ferdon &t;a to Wealingaforda. &amp; &t;et eall forsweldon. &amp; w&ae;ndon him &t;a andlang &AE;scesdune to Cwicelmes hl&ae;we. 
 &amp; &t;&ae;r onbidedon beotra gylpa. for&t;on oft man cw&ae;&d;. gif hi Cwicchelmes hl&ae;we gesohton. &t;et hi n&ae;fre to s&ae; gan ne sceoldan. wendon &t;a o&d;res w&ae;ges hamweard. 
 &T;a w&ae;s &t;&ae;r fyrd gesomnod &ae;t Cynetan. &amp; hi &t;&ae;r tog&ae;dere fengon. &amp; sona &t;et w&ae;rod on fleame gebrohtan  &amp; sy&d;&d;an hyra herehu&d;e to s&ae; f&ae;redon. 
 &T;&ae;r mihton geseon Winceastre leodan rancne here. &amp; unearhne. &t;&ae;t hi be hyra gate to s&ae; eodon. &amp; m&ae;te &amp; madmas ofer L mila him fram s&ae; f&ae;ttan. 
 &T;a w&ae;s se cyng gewend ofer Temese into Scrobbesbyrigscire. &amp; nam &t;&ae;r his feorme in &t;&ae;re middewintres tide. 
 &T;a wear&d; hit swa mycel &ae;ge fram &t;am here. &t;et man ne mihte ge&t;eoncean ne asm&ae;gian hu man of earde hi gebringon sceolde. o&d;&d;e &t;isne eard wi&d; hi gehealdan. for&t;an &t;e hi h&ae;fdon &ae;lce scire on West Sexum sti&d;e gemarcod mid bryne. &amp; mid hergunge. 
 Agan se cyng georne to smeagenne wi&d; his witan hwet heom eallum r&ae;dlicost &t;uhte. &t;&ae;t man &t;isum earde gebeorgan mihte &ae;r he mid ealle fordon wur&d;e. 
 &D;a ger&ae;dde seo cyng &amp; his witan eallum &t;eodscipe to &t;earfe. &t;eah hit him eallum la&d; w&ae;re. &t;&ae;t man nyde moste &t;am here gafol gyldan. 
 &D;a sende se cyng to &t;am here. &amp; him cy&t;an het &t;&ae;t he wolde &t;&ae;t heom gri&d; betweonan beon sceolde. &amp; him man gafol and metsunge syllan sceolde. &amp; hi &d;a ealle &t;&ae;t underfengon. &amp; him man metsode geond Angelcyn. 
 Her on &d;issum geare w&ae;s &t;et gafol gel&ae;st &t;am unfri&d;e here. &t;&ae;t w&ae;s xxx &t;usend punda. 
 &amp; On &d;issum geare eac w&ae;s &AE;dric gesett to ealdorman on Myrcena rice. 
 Her bebead se cyng &t;&ae;t man sceolde ofer eall Angelcynn scipu feastlice wircean. &t;&ae;t is &t;onne of &t;rym hund hidum. &amp; of x hidon &ae;nne sceg&d;. &amp; of viii hidum helm &amp; byrnan. 
 Her on &t;issum geare gewurdon &t;a scipu gearwe &t;e we &ae;r ymbe spr&ae;con. &amp; heora w&ae;s swa feala swa n&ae;fre &ae;r &t;es &d;e us bec secga&d; on Angelcynne ne gewurdon on nanes cynges d&ae;g. 
 &amp; hi man &t;a ealle tog&ae;dere ferode to Sandwic. &amp; &t;&ae;r sceoldan licgan. &amp; &t;isne eard healdan wi&d; &ae;lcne uthere. ac we gyt n&ae;fdon &t;a gesel&d;a. ne &t;one wur&d;scipe &t;&ae;t seo scipfyrd nytt w&ae;re &d;isum earde. &t;e ma &t;e heo oftor &ae;r w&ae;s. 
 &D;a gewear&d; hit on &t;isum ilcan timan o&d;&d;e litle &ae;r &t;et Brihtric Eadrices bro&d;or ealdormannes forwregde Wulfno&d; cild &t;one Su&d;seaxscian to &t;am cyning. 
 &amp; he &t;a utgewende. &amp; him &t;a to aspeon &t;et he heafde xx scipa. &amp; he &t;a hergode &ae;ghwer be &d;am su&d;riman. &amp; &ae;lc yfel wrohton. 
 &T;a cydde man into &t;&ae;re scipfyrde. &t;et hi mann ea&d;e befaran mihte. gif man ymbe beon wolde. 
 &D;a genam se Brihtric him to hundeahtatig scipa. &amp; &t;ohte &t;&ae;t he him myceles wordes wircean sceolde. &t;&ae;t he Wulfno&d; cuconne o&d;&d;e deadne begytan sceolde. 
 Ac &t;a hi &t;yderweard w&ae;ron. &t;a com him swilc wind ongean swilce nan mann &ae;r ne gemunde. &amp; &t;a scipo &d;a ealle tobeot. &amp; to&t;r&ae;sc. &amp; on land wearp. &amp; com se Wulfno&d; sona. &amp; &d;a scipo forb&ae;rnde. 
 &D;a &t;is cu&d; w&ae;s to &d;am o&d;rum scipon &t;&ae;r se cyng w&ae;s hu &d;a o&d;re geferdon. w&ae;s &t;a swilc hit eall r&ae;dleas w&ae;re. &amp; ferde se cyng him ham. &amp; &t;a ealdormenn. &amp; &t;a heahwitan. &amp; forleton &t;a scipo &t;us leohtlice. 
 &amp; &t;et folc &t;a &t;e on &d;am scipe w&ae;ron f&ae;rcodon &d;a scipo eft to Lundene. &amp; leton ealles &d;eodscipes geswincg &t;us leohtlice forwur&d;an. &amp; n&ae;s se ege na betera &t;e eall Angelcynn tohopode. 
 &T;a &d;eos scipfyrd &d;us geendod w&ae;s. &t;a com sona &ae;fter hlammessan se ungemetlica unfri&d;here to Sandwic. &amp; sona wendon heora fore to Cantwarbyrig. &amp; &t;a burh ra&d;e geeodon. gif hi &t;e ra&d;or to him fri&d;es to ne girndon. 
 &amp; ealle East Centingas wi&d; &t;one here fri&d; genamon. &amp; him gesealdon iii &t;usend punda. 
 &amp; se here &t;a sona &ae;fter &t;am gewende abuton o&d; &t;et hi comon to Wihtlande. &amp; &t;&ae;r &ae;ghwer on Su&d;seaxum. &amp; on Hamtunscire. &amp; eac on Bearrucscire hergodon &amp; b&ae;rndon swa heora gewuna w&ae;s. 
 &T;a het se cyng abannan ut ealne &t;eodscipe &t;et mann on &ae;lce healfe wi&d; hi gehealden sceolde. ac &t;eah hwe&d;ere hi ferdon loc hu hi woldon. 
 &T;a sum si&d;e heafde se cyng hi forebegan mid ealre fyrde. &t;a hi to scipan woldon. &amp; eall folc gearu w&ae;s heom on to fonne. ac hit w&ae;s &d;a &t;urh Eadric ealdorman gelet swa hit &t;a &ae;fre w&ae;s. 
 &D;a &ae;fter sanctus Martinus m&ae;ssan. &t;a ferdon hi eft ongean to Cent. &amp; namon him wintersettl on Temesan. &amp; lifedon of East Seaxum. &amp; of &d;am scirum &t;e &t;&ae;r nyxt w&ae;ron on twam healfe Temese. &amp; oft hi on &t;a burh Lundene gefuhton. 
 Ac si Gode lof. &t;et heo gyt gesund stent. &amp; hi &t;&ae;r &ae;fre yfel geferdon. 
 &D;a &ae;fter middan wintra hi namon &t;a &ae;nne upgang ut &t;urh Ciltern. &amp; swa to Oxneforda. &amp; &t;a burh forb&ae;rndon. &amp; namon hit &t;a on twa healfe Temese to scipanweard. 
 &T;a gewarnode man hi &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;r w&ae;s fyrd &ae;t Lundene ongean. hi gewendon &t;a ofer &ae;t Stane. &amp; &t;us ferdon ealne &t;one winter  &amp; &d;one lencten w&ae;ron him on Cent. and bettan heora scipa. 
 Her on &d;issum geare com se foresprecenda here ofer Eastron to East Englum. &amp; wendon up &ae;t Gipeswic. &amp; eodon anreces &t;&ae;r hi geaxodon Ulfcytel mid his fyrde. 
 &D;is w&ae;s on &t;am d&ae;g prima ascensio Domini. 
 &amp; &t;a sona flugon East Engla. &t;a stod Grantabrycgscir f&ae;stlice ongean. 
 &T;&ae;r w&ae;s ofsl&ae;gen &AE;&d;elstan &t;es cynges a&d;um. &amp; Oswi &amp; his sunu. &amp; Wulfric Leofwines sunu. &amp; Eadwig &AE;fices bro&d;or. &amp; feala o&d;ra godra &t;egna. &amp; folces ungerim. 
 &T;one fleam &ae;rest astealde &t;urcytel Myran heafod. &amp; &t;a D&ae;niscan ahton w&ae;lstowe geweald. &amp; &t;&ae;r wurdon gehorsode. 
 &amp; sy&d;&d;on ahton East Engle geweald. &amp; &t;one eard iii mon&t;as hergodon &amp; b&ae;rndon. 
 Ge fur&d;on on &t;a wildan fennas hi ferdon. &amp; menn &amp; yrfe hi slogon. &amp; b&ae;rndon geond &t;a feonnas. &amp; &t;eodford forb&ae;rndon. &amp; Grantabrycge. 
 &amp; sy&d;&d;on wendon eft su&d;weard into Temese. &amp; ridon &t;a gehorsedan menn ongean &t;a scipo. 
 &amp; sy&d;&d;on hr&ae;dlice wendon westweard on Oxnafordscire. &amp; &t;anon to Bucinghamscire. &amp; swa andlang Usan. o&d; hi comon to Bedanforda &amp; swa for&d; o&d; Temesanford. &amp; a b&ae;rndon swa hi geferdon. 
 Wendon &t;a eft to scipon mid heora herehu&d;e. &amp; &t;one hi to scipon streddon. &t;onne sceolde fyrd ut eft ongean &t;&ae;t hi up woldon. 
 &T;onne ferde seo fyrd ham. 
 &amp; &t;onne hi w&ae;ron be easton. &t;onne heold man fyrde be westan. &amp; &t;onne hi w&ae;ron be su&d;an. &t;onne w&ae;s ure fyrd be nor&d;an. 
 &D;onne bead man ealle witan to cynge. &amp; man &t;onne r&ae;dan scolde hu man &t;isne eard werian sceolde. Ac &t;eah man hw&ae;t &t;onne r&ae;dde. &t;&ae;t ne stod fur&d;on &ae;nne mona&d;. 
 &AE;t nyxtan n&ae;s nan heafodman &t;&ae;t fyrde gaderian wolde. ac &ae;lc fleah swa he m&ae;st myhte. Ne fur&d;on nan scir nolde o&d;re gel&ae;stan &ae;t nyxtan. 
 &T;a &ae;tforan sanctus Andreas m&ae;ssan. &d;a com se here to Hamtune. &amp; &t;one port sona forb&ae;rndon. &amp; &t;&ae;r namon abuton swa mycel swa hi woldon sylfe. &amp; &t;anon wendon ofer Temese into West Seaxum. &amp; swa wi&d; Caningan m&ae;rsces. &amp; &t;&ae;t eall forb&ae;rndon. 
 &T;a hi swa feor gegan h&ae;fdon swa hi &t;a woldon. &t;a comon hi to &d;am middanwintra to scipon. 
 Her on &t;issum geare sende se cyng &amp; his witan to &d;am here. &amp; georndon fri&d;es. &amp; him gafol &amp; metsunga behetan. wi&d; &t;am &t;e hi heora hergunga geswicon. 
 Hi heafdon &t;a ofergan East Engla i and East Seaxe ii &amp; Middel Seaxe iii &amp; Oxenafordscire iiii &amp; Grantabrycgescire v &amp; Heortfordscire vi &amp; Bucingahamscire vii &amp; Bedanfordscire viii &amp; healfe Huntadunscire x &amp; be su&d;an Temese ealle Centingas. &amp; Su&d; Seaxe. &amp; H&ae;stingas. &amp; Su&d;rig. &amp; Bearrucscire. &amp; Hamtunscire. &amp; micel on Wiltunscire. 
 Ealle &t;as unges&ae;l&d;a us gelumpon &t;urh unr&ae;des. &t;&ae;t mann nolde him to timan gafol bedan. ac &t;onne hi m&ae;st to yfele gedon h&ae;fdon. &t;onne nam man gri&d;. &amp; fri&d; wi&d; hi. 
 &amp; na&d;el&ae;s for eallum &t;isum gri&d;e &amp; fri&d;e &amp; gafole. hi ferdon &ae;ghwider folcm&ae;lum. &amp; hergodon. &amp; ure earme folc r&ae;pton &amp; slogon. 
 &amp; On &t;issum geare betwix Natiuitate sancte Marie &amp; sancte Michaeles m&ae;ssan hi ymbes&ae;tan Cantwaraburh. &amp; hi &t;&ae;r into comon &t;urh syrewrenceas. for&t;on &AE;lm&ae;r hi becyrde Cantwaraburh. &t;e se arcebiscop &AE;lfeah &ae;r generede his life. 
 &amp; hi &t;&ae;r &t;a genaman &t;one arcebiscop &AE;lfeah. &amp; &AE;lfword &t;&ae;t cynges gerefan. &amp; Leofwine abbod. &amp; Godwine biscop. &amp; &AE;lm&ae;r abbod hi l&ae;tan aweg. 
 &amp; hi &t;&ae;r genaman inne ealle &t;a gehadode menn. &amp; weras. &amp; wif. &t;&ae;t w&ae;s unasecgendlic &ae;nigum menn hu mycel &t;&ae;s folces w&ae;s. 
 &amp; on &t;&ae;re byrig si&d;&d;on w&ae;ron swa lange swa hi woldon. &amp; &t;a hi h&ae;fdon &t;a burh ealle asmeade. wendon him &t;a to scipon. &amp; l&ae;ddon &t;one arcebiscop mid him; 
 W&ae;s &d;a r&ae;pling  se &t;e &ae;r w&ae;s Angelcynnes heafod &amp; Christendomes. 
 &T;&ae;r man mihte &t;a geseon earm&d;e &t;&ae;r man &ae;r geseah blisse on &t;&ae;re &ae;rman byrig  &t;anon us com &ae;rest Christendom &amp; blisse for Gode &amp; for worulde. 
 &amp; hi heafdon &t;one arcebiscop mid him swalange o&d; &t;one timan &t;e hi hine gemartyredon. 
 Her on &t;issum geare com Eadric ealdorman. &amp; ealle &t;a yldestan witan gehadode &amp; leawede Angelcynnes to Lundenbyrig toforan &t;am Eastron. 
 W&ae;s &ae;sterd&ae;g &t;a on &d;am datarum IDus Aprilis. 
 &amp; hi &t;&ae;ra &d;a swa lange w&ae;ron o&d; &t;&ae;t gafol w&ae;s eall gel&ae;st ofer Eastran. &t;&ae;t w&ae;s viii &t;usend punda. 
 &T;a on &t;one S&ae;ternesd&ae;g wear&d; swi&d;e gestired se here ongean &t;one biscop. for&t;an &t;e he nolde heom nan feoh behaten. &amp; forbead &t;&ae;t man nan &t;ing wi&d; him syllan ne moste. 
 W&ae;ron hi eac swy&d;e druncene. for&t;am &t;&ae;r w&ae;s gebroht win su&d;an. 
 Genamon &t;a &t;one biscop. leaddon hine to heora hustinga on &t;one Sunnanefen octabas Pasch&ae;. &amp; hine &t;a &t;&ae;r oftorfodon mid banum. &amp; mid hry&d;era heafdum. 
 &amp; sloh hine &t;a an heora mid anre &ae;xe yre on &t;et heafod. &t;et he mid &t;am dynte ni&d;er asah. &amp; his halige blod on &d;a eor&d;an feoll. &amp; his &t;a haligan sawle to Godes rice asende. 
 &amp; &t;a biscopas Eadno&d; &amp; &AE;lfhun. &amp; seo burhwaru underfengon haligan &t;one lichaman on mergen &amp; feredon hine to Lundene mid ealre arwur&d;nisse. &amp; hine bebyrigdon on sanctus Paulus mynstre. &amp; &t;&ae;r nu God swutela&d; &t;&ae;s halgan martires mihta. 
 &D;a &t;et gafol gelest w&ae;s. &amp; &t;a fri&d; a&d;as gesworene. &t;a toferde se here wide swa he &ae;r gegaderod w&ae;s. 
 &D;a bugon to &t;am cyninge of &t;am here xlv scipa. &amp; him beheton &t;et hi woldon &t;isne eard healdan. &amp; he hi fedan scolde &amp; scrydan. 
 On &t;am &ae;ftran geare &t;e se arcebiscop w&ae;s gemartyrod. se cyng ges&ae;tte Lifing biscop to Cantwarabyrig to &d;am arcestole. 
 &amp; on &t;am ilcan geare toforan &t;am mon&d;e Augustus com Swegen cyning mid his flotan to Sandwic. &amp; wende swy&d;e ra&d;e abutan East Englum. into Humbran mu&d;an. &amp; swa uppweard andlang Trentan &t;et he com to Gegnesburh. 
 &amp; &t;a sona abeah Uhtred eorl. &amp; eall Nor&d;hymbra to him. &amp; eall &t;&ae;t folc on Lindesige. &amp; sy&d;&d;an &t;et folc of Fifburhingan. &amp; ra&d;e &t;&ae;s eall here be nor&d;an W&ae;tlinga str&ae;te. &amp; him man sealde gislas of &ae;lcere scire. 
 Sy&d;&d;an he undergeat &t;et eall folc him to gebogen w&ae;s. &t;a bead he &t;&ae;t man sceolde his here metian &amp; horsian. 
 &amp; he &t;a gewende sy&d;&d;an su&d;weard mid fulre fyrde. &amp; bet&ae;hte his scipa &amp; &t;a gislas Cnute his sunu. 
 &amp; sy&d;&d;an he com ofer W&ae;clingastr&ae;te  hi wrohton &t;&ae;t m&ae;ste yfel &t;e &ae;nig here don mihte. 
 Wende &t;a to Oxnaforda. &amp; seo burhwaru sona abeah &amp; gislode. &amp; &t;anon to Winceastre. &amp; &t;&ae;t ilce dydon. 
 Wendon &t;a &t;anon eastward to Lundene. &amp; mycel his folces adranc on Temese. for&d;am hi nanre brycge ne cepton. 
 &D;a he to &t;&ae;re byrig com. &t;a nolde seo burhwaru abugan ac heoldan mid fullan wige ongean. for&d;an &t;&ae;r w&ae;s inne se cyning &ae;&t;elred. &amp; &t;urkil mid him. 
 &T;a wende Swegen cyning &t;anon to Wealingaforda. &amp; swa ofer Temese westweard to Ba&d;on. &amp; s&ae;t &t;&ae;r mid his fyrde. 
 &amp; com &AE;&t;elmer ealdorman &t;ider. &amp; &t;a weasternan &t;&ae;gnas mid him. &amp; bugon ealle to Swegene. &amp; gislodon. 
 &T;a he eall &t;us gefaren heafde. wende &t;a nor&d;weard to his scipon. 
 &amp; eall &t;eodscipe hine heafde for fullne cyning. 
 &amp; seo burhwaru &ae;fter &t;am on Lundene beah &amp; gislode. for&t;am hi ondreddon &t;&ae;t he hi fordon wolde. 
 Bead &t;a Swegen full gild &amp; metsunga to his here &t;one winter. &amp; &t;urcyl bead &t;&ae;t ilce to &t;am here &t;e l&ae;g on Grenawic. &amp; buton &t;am hi hergodan swa oft swa hi woldon. 
 &D;a ne duhte na&d;or &t;isse &t;eoda ne su&d;an. ne nor&d;an. 
 &T;a w&ae;s se cyng sume hwile mid &t;am flotan &t;e on Temese w&ae;ron. &amp; seo hlafdige wende &t;a ofer seo to hire bro&d;or Ricarde. &amp; &AE;lsige abbot of Burh mid hire. 
 &amp; se cyng sende &AE;lfun biscop mid &t;am &ae;&t;elinge Eadwarde. &amp; &AE;lfrede ofer se. &t;&ae;t he hi bewitan sceolde.

 &amp; &d;a hwile &t;e seo l&ae;fdige mid hire bro&t;er w&ae;s begondon s&ae;. &AE;lfsige abbot of Burh &t;e &t;&ae;r w&ae;s mid hire for to &t;one mynstre &t;e is gehaten Boneual &t;&ae;r sancte Florentines lichama l&ae;g. 
 Fand &t;&ae;r &ae;rm stede. &ae;rm abbot &amp; &ae;rme muneces  for&t;an &t;e hi forhergode w&ae;ron. 
 Bohte &t;a &t;&ae;r &ae;t &t;one abbot &amp; &ae;t &t;e muneces sancte Florentines lichaman eall buton &t;e heafod to v hundred punda. &amp; &t;a &t;e he ongean com &t;a offrede hit Crist &amp; sancte Peter. 
 Her on &t;issum geare Swegen geendode his dagas to candelm&ae;ssan iii Non&ae; Februarii. &amp; se flota eall gecuron Cnut to cyninge. 
 &D;a ger&ae;ddan &t;a witan ealle ge hadode ge l&ae;wede &t;&ae;t man &ae;fter &t;am cyninge &AE;&d;elrede sende. &amp; cw&ae;don &t;&ae;t him nan leofre hlaford n&ae;re &t;onne heora gecynde hlaford. gif he hi rihtlicor healdan wolde &t;onne he &ae;r dyde. 
 &D;a sende se cyng his sunu Eadward mid his &ae;rendracan hider. &amp; het gretan ealne his leodscipe. 
 &amp; cw&ae;&d; &t;&ae;t he heom hold hlaford beon wolde. &amp; &ae;lc &t;&ae;ra &t;inga betan &t;e hi ealle ascunedon. &amp; &ae;lc &t;&ae;ra &t;inga forgifan beon sceolde &t;e him gedon o&d;&d;e gecwe&d;en w&ae;re. wi&d; &t;am &t;e hi ealle anr&ae;dlice buton swicdome to him gecyrdon. 
 &amp; man &t;a fullne freondscipe gef&ae;stnode mid worde &amp; mid w&ae;dde on &ae;g&d;ere healfe. &amp; &ae;fre &ae;lcne Deniscne cyning utlagede of Englalande gecw&ae;don. 
 &D;a com &ae;&d;elred cyning innan &t;am lenctene ham to his agenre &d;eode. &amp; he gl&ae;dlice fram heom eallum onfangen w&ae;s. 
 &amp; &t;a sy&d;&d;on Swegen dead w&ae;s. s&ae;tt Cnut mid his here on Gegnesburh o&d; &d;a Eastron. &amp; gewear&d; him &amp; &t;am folce on Lindesige anes. &t;&ae;t hi hine horsian sceoldan. &amp; sy&d;&d;an ealle &ae;tg&ae;dere faran &amp; hergian. 
 &D;a com se cyning &ae;&d;elred mid fulre fyrde &t;ider &ae;r hi gearwe w&ae;ron to Lindesige. &amp; mann &t;a hergode. &amp; b&ae;rnde &amp; sloh eall &t;et mancynn &t;&ae;t man ar&ae;can mihte. 
 Se Cnut gewende him ut mid his flotan. &amp; wear&d; &t;et earme folc &t;us beswican &t;urh hine. 
 &amp; w&ae;nde &t;a su&d;weard o&d; &t;&ae;t he com to Sandwic. &amp; let &t;&ae;r up &t;a gislas &t;e his f&ae;der gesealde w&ae;ron. &amp; cearf of heora handa &amp; heora nosa. 
 &amp; buton eallum &t;isum yfelum se cyning het gyldan &t;am here &t;e on Grenewic l&ae;g xxi &t;usend punda. 
 &amp; on &t;issum geare on sancte Mich&ae;les m&ae;sse&ae;fan. com &t;et mycele s&ae;flod geond wide &t;isne eard. &amp; &ae;rn swa feor up swa n&ae;fre &ae;r ne dyde. &amp; adrencte feala tuna. &amp; manncynnes unarim&ae;dlice geteall. 
 On &t;issum geare w&ae;s &t;&ae;t mycele gemot on Oxonaforda. 
 &amp; &t;&ae;r Eadric ealdorman beswac Sigefer&d; &amp; Morc&ae;r &t;a yldestan &t;&ae;genas into Seofonburgum. bep&ae;hte hi into his bure. &amp; hi man &t;&ae;r inne ofsloh ungerisenlice. 
 &amp; se cyng &t;a genam eall heora &ae;hta. &amp; het nimon Sigefer&d;es lafe &amp; gebringon binnon Mealdelmes byrig. 
 &T;a &ae;fter litlum fece ferde Eadmund &ae;&d;eling to. &amp; genam &t;&ae;t wif ofer &t;es cynges willan. &amp; heafde him to wife. 
 &D;a toforan natiuitas sancte Mari&ae; ferde se &ae;&d;eling w&ae;ston nor&d; into Fifburgum. &amp; gerad sona ealle Sigefer&d;es are &amp; Morcares. &amp; &t;&ae;t folc eall him tobeah. 
 &amp; &t;a on &d;am ylcan timan com Cnut cyng to Sandwic. &amp; wende sona abutan Centland into West Seaxen o&d; he com to Fromu&d;an. &amp; hergode &t;a on Dors&ae;tum &amp; on Wiltunscire. &amp; on Sum&ae;rs&ae;ton. &t;a l&ae;g se cyng seoc &ae;t Cosham. 
 &D;a gaderode Eadric ealdorman fyrde &amp; se &ae;&d;eling Eadmund be nor&d;an. 
 &D;a hi tog&ae;dere comon. &t;a wolde se ealdorman beswicon &t;one &ae;&t;eling. &amp; hi tohwurfon &t;a buton gefeohte for&t;am. &amp; rimdon heora feondum. 
 &amp; Eadric ealdormann aspeon &t;a xl scipa fram &t;am cyning. &amp; beah &t;a to Cnute. 
 &amp; West Seaxe bugon &amp; gislodon. &amp; horsodon &t;one here. &amp; he w&ae;s &t;&ae;r &t;a o&d; midne winter. 
 Her on &t;issum geare com Cnut cyning mid his here clx scipa. &amp; Eadirc ealdormann mid him ofer Temese into Myrcan &ae;t Cr&ae;cilade.

 &D;a ongan se &ae;&d;eling Eadmund to gadrienne fyrde. 
 &T;a seo fyrd gesomnod w&ae;s. &t;a ne onhagode him buton se cyng &t;&ae;re w&ae;re. &amp; hi h&ae;fdon &t;&ae;re burhware fultum of Lundene. 
 Geswicon &t;a &t;&ae;re fyrding. &amp; f&ae;rde &ae;lc mann him ham. 
 &D;a &ae;fter &t;&ae;re tide &t;a bead mann eft fyrde be fullum wite. &t;&ae;t &ae;lc mann &t;e feor w&ae;re for&d; gewende.

 &D;a hi ealle tosomne comon. &t;a ne beheold hit naht &t;e ma &t;e hit oftor &ae;r dyde. 
 &T;a cydde mann &t;am cyninge &t;&ae;t hine mann beswicon wolde. &t;a &t;e him on fultume beon sceolden. Forlet &d;a &t;a fyrde. &amp; cyrde him eft to Lundene. 
 &D;a rad se &ae;&t;eling Eadmund to Nor&d;hymbran to Vhtrede eorl. &amp; w&ae;nde &ae;lc mann &t;&ae;t hi woldon fyrde somnian ongean Cnut cyng. 
 &T;a ferdon hi into St&ae;ffordscire. &amp; into Scrobbesbyrig. &amp; to Legeceastre. 
 &amp; hergodon hi on heora healfe &amp; Cnut on his. 
 &amp; wende him &t;a ut &t;urh Buccingahamscire into Beadafordscire. &amp; &t;anon to Huntandunscire. andlang fennes to Stanforda. &amp; &d;a into Lincolnescire. &t;anon to Snotingahamscire. &amp; swa to Nor&d;hymbran to Eoforwicweard. 
 &D;a Uhtred geaxode &t;is. &d;a forlet he his hergunga &amp; efeste nor&d;weard. &amp; beah &t;a for nede. &amp; ealle Nor&d;hymbran mid him. 
 &amp; he gislode. &amp; hine man &d;eah hw&ae;&d;ere ofsloh. &amp; &t;urcytel Nafanan sunu mid him. 
 &amp; &t;a &ae;fter &t;&ae;s se cyng Cnut ges&ae;tte Yric into Nor&d;hymbran to eorle. eall swa Uhtred w&ae;s. 
 &amp; sy&d;&d;an wendon him su&d;weard o&d;res weges eall be westan. &amp; com &t;a eall se here toforan &t;am Eastron to scipon. 
 &amp; se &ae;&t;eling &AE;dmund wende to Lundene to his f&ae;der. &amp; &t;a &ae;fter Eastron wende se cyng Cnut mid eallum his scipum to Lundeneweard. 
 &D;a gelamp hit &t;et se cyng &ae;&d;elred for&d;ferde &ae;r &d;a scipu comon. 
 He geendode his dagas on sanctes Georius m&ae;ssed&ae;ge &ae;fter mycclum geswince. &amp; earfo&d;nissum his lifes. 
 &amp; &t;a &ae;fter his ende. ealle &t;a witan &t;e on Lundene w&ae;ron &amp; se burhwaru gecuron Eadmund to cynge. &amp; his rice he heardlice werode &t;a hwile &t;e his tima w&ae;s. 
 &T;a comon &t;a scipo to Grenawic to &t;am gandagum. &amp; binnon lytlum f&ae;ce wendon to Lundene. 
 &amp; dulfon &t;a ane mycele dic on &d;a su&d;healfe &amp; drogon heora scipa on westhealfe &t;&ae;re brycge. &amp; bedicodon sy&d;&d;on &t;a burh uton &t;&ae;t nan mann ne mihte ne inn ne ut. 
 &amp; oft r&ae;dlice on &d;a burh fuhton. ac hi heom heardlice wi&d;stodon. 
 &T;a w&ae;s Eadmund cyng &ae;r &t;am gewend ut. &amp; gerad &t;a West Seaxan. &amp; him beah eall folc to. 
 &amp; ra&d;e &ae;fter &t;am he gefeaht wi&d; &t;one here &ae;t Peonnan wi&d; Gillinga. &amp; o&d;er gefeoht he gefeaht &ae;fter middan sumera &ae;t Sceortstane. 
 &amp; &t;&ae;r mycel w&ae;ll feoll on &ae;g&d;re healfe. &amp; &t;a heres him sylfe toeodon on &d;am gefeohte. 
 &amp; Eadric ealdorman &amp; &AE;lm&ae;r Deorlingc w&ae;ron &t;am here on fultume ongean Eadmund cyng. 
 &amp; &t;a gegaderode he iii si&d;e fyrde &amp; ferde to Lundene. &amp; &t;a burhware ahredde. &amp; &t;one here aflymde to scipon. 
 &amp; &t;a w&ae;s ymbe twa niht &t;&ae;t se cyning gewende ofer &ae;t Brentforda. &amp; &t;a wi&d; &t;one here gefeaht &amp; hine aflymde.

 &amp; on &t;isum geare for&d;ferde Eadsige arcebiscop iiii kalend&ae; Novembris. 
 Her on &t;isum geare Eadward cyng gesette Rodbyrd on Lundene to arcebiscop to Cantwarabyrig on Lengtene. &amp; &t;&ae;s sylfan Lentenes he for to Rome &ae;fter his pallium. 
 &amp; se cyng geaf &t;et biscoprice on Lundene Sparhafoc abbot of Abbandune. &amp; se cyng geaf &t;&ae;t abbotrice Ro&d;ulfe biscop his m&ae;ge. 
 &D;a com se arcebiscop fram Rome ane d&ae;ge &ae;r sanctus Petrus m&ae;sse&ae;fene. &amp; ges&ae;t his arcebiscopstol &ae;t Cristescyrcean on sanctus Petrus m&ae;ssed&ae;g. &amp; sona &t;&ae;s to &t;am cyng gew&ae;nde. 
 &D;a com Sparhafoc abbod be wege to him mid &t;&ae;s cynges gewrite &amp; insegle. to &t;an &t;et he hine hadian sceolde to biscop into Lundene. &t;a wi&d;cwe&d; se arcebiscop. &amp; cw&ae;&d; &t;et se papa hit him forboden h&ae;fde. 
 &T;a gewende se abbod ongean &t;one arcebiscop eft to &d;am  &amp; &t;&ae;r &t;es biscophades gernde. &amp; se arcebiscop him anr&ae;dlice forwernde. &amp; cw&ae;&d; &t;et se papa hit him forboden h&ae;fde. 
 &D;a gewende se abbod to Lundene. &amp; s&ae;t on &t;am biscoprice &t;e se cyng him &ae;r geunnan h&ae;fde be his fulre leafe ealne &t;one sumor &amp; &t;one h&ae;rfest. 
 &amp; com &t;a Eustatius fram geondan s&ae; sona &ae;fter &t;am biscop. &amp; gewende to &d;am cynge. &amp; sp&ae;c wi&d; hine &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t he &t;a wolde. &amp; gewende &t;a hamweard. 
 &T;a he com to Cantwarbyrig east &t;a sn&ae;dde he &t;&ae;r &amp; his menn. &amp; to Dofran gewende. 
 &D;a he w&ae;s sume mila o&d;&d;e mare beheonan Dofran. &t;a dyde he on his byrnan. &amp; his geferan ealle. &amp; foran to Dofran. 
 &T;a hi &t;ider comon. &t;a woldon hi innian hi &t;&ae;r heom sylfan gelicode. 
 &T;a com an his manna. &amp; wolde wician &ae;t anes bundan huse his un&d;ances. &amp; gewundode &t;one husbundon. &amp; se husbunda ofsloh &t;one o&d;erne. 
 &D;a wear&d; Eustatius uppon his horse. &amp; his gefeoran uppon heora &amp; ferdon to &t;am husbundon. &amp; ofslogon hine binnan his agenan heor&d;&ae;. 
 &amp; wendon him &t;a up to &t;&ae;re burgeweard. &amp; ofslogon &ae;g&d;er ge wi&d;innan ge wi&d;utan. ma &t;anne xx manna. &amp; &t;a burhmen ofslogon xix menn on o&d;re healfe. &amp; gewundoden &t;&ae;t hi nystan hu fela. 
 &amp; Eustatius &ae;tb&ae;rst mid feawum mannum. &amp; gewende ongean to &t;am cynge. &amp; cydde be d&ae;le hu hi gefaren h&ae;fdon. 
 &amp; wear&d; se cyng swi&t;e gram wi&d; &t;a burhware. &amp; ofs&ae;nde se cyng Godwine eorl. &amp; b&ae;d hine faran into Cent mid unfri&d;a to Dofran. for&t;an Eustatius h&ae;fde gecydd &t;am cynge &t;et hit sceolde beon mare gylt &t;&ae;re burhwaru &t;onne his. 
 Ac hit n&ae;s na swa. &amp; se eorl nolde na ge&d;w&ae;rian &t;&ae;re infare. for&t;an him w&ae;s la&d; to amyrrene his agenne folga&d;. 
 &D;a sende se cyng &ae;fter eallon his witan. &amp; bead heom cuman to Gleaweceastre neh &t;&ae;re &ae;ftre sancte Maria m&ae;ssan. 
 &T;a h&ae;fdon &t;a welisce menn gewroht &ae;nne castel on Herefordscire on Swegenes eorles folgo&d;e. &amp; wrohten &ae;lc &t;&ae;ra harme. &amp; bismere &t;&ae;s cynges mannan &t;&ae;r abutan &t;e hi mihton. 
 &D;a com Godwine eorl &amp; Swegen eorl &amp; Harold eorl tog&ae;dere &ae;t Byferesstane. &amp; manig mann mid heom. to &d;on &t;&ae;t hi woldon faran to heora cynehlaforde. &amp; to &t;am witan eallon &t;e mid him gegaderode w&ae;ron. &t;&ae;t hi &t;&ae;s cynges r&ae;d h&ae;fdon &amp; his fultum. &amp; ealra witena. hu hi mihton &t;&ae;s cynges bismer awrecan &amp; ealles &t;eodscipes. 
 &D;a w&ae;ron &t;a w&ae;lisce men &ae;tforan mid &t;am cynge. &amp; forwregdon &d;a eorlas. &t;et hi ne moston cuman on his eagon gesih&d;e. For&d;an hi s&ae;don &t;&ae;t hi woldon cuman &t;ider for &t;es cynges swicdome. 
 W&ae;s &t;&ae;r cuman Siward eorl &amp; Leofric eorl. &amp; mycel folc mid heom nor&t;an to &t;am cynge. &amp; w&ae;s &t;am eorle Godwine &amp; his sunan gecydd &t;&ae;t se cyng &amp; &t;a menn &t;e mid him w&ae;ron. woldon r&ae;don on hi. &amp; hi trymedon hi f&ae;stlice ongean. &t;&ae;h him la&d; w&ae;re &t;&ae;t hi ongean heora cynehlaford standan sceoldan. 
 &D;a ger&ae;dden &t;a witan on &ae;g&d;er halfe &t;&ae;t man &d;a &ae;lces yfeles geswac. &amp; geaf se cyng Godes gri&d; &amp; his fulne freondscipe on &ae;g&d;re healfe. 
 &D;a ger&ae;dde se cyning &amp; his witan &t;&ae;t man sceolde o&d;re sy&d;an habban ealra gewitena gemot on Lundene to h&ae;rfestes emnihte. 
 &amp; het se cyning bannan ut here. &ae;g&d;er ge besu&d;an Temese ge benor&d;an eall &t;&ae;t &ae;fre betst w&ae;s.

 &T;a hi &t;ider utcomon. &t;a stefnede heom man to gemote. &t;a gyrnde he gri&d;es &amp; gisla. &t;et he moste unswican into gemote cuman. &amp; ut of gemote. 
 &D;a gyrnde se cyng ealra &t;&ae;ra &t;egna &t;e &t;a eorlas &ae;r h&ae;fdon. &amp; hi letan hi ealle him to handa.

 &T;a geornde se eorl eft gri&d;es &amp; gisla. &t;&ae;t he moste hine betellan &ae;t &ae;lc &t;&ae;ra &t;inga &t;e him man on lede. 
 &T;a wyrnde him mann &d;era gisla. &amp; sceawede him mann v nihta gri&d; ut of lande tofarenne.

 Her on &d;isum geare for&d;ferde &AE;lfgiue Ymma Eadwardes cynges modor &amp; Hardacnutes cynges.

 &D;a gewende Godwine eorl ut fram Brycge mid his scypum to Yseran. and let ut ane d&ae;ge &ae;r midsumeres m&ae;sse&ae;fene &t;&ae;t he com to N&ae;sse. &t;e is besu&d;an Rumenea. 
 &T;a com hit to witenne &t;am eorlum ut to Sandwic. &amp; hi &t;a gewendon ut &ae;fter &t;am o&d;rum scipum. &amp; bead man landfyrde ut ongean &t;a scipu.

 &amp; gewende &t;a Godwine eorl ut agean &t;&ae;t he com eft to Brycge. &amp; &d;a o&d;ra scipu gewenden heom eft ongean to Sandwic.

 &amp; gewendon heom &t;a westweard o&d; &t;et hi comon to Portlande. &amp; eodon &t;&ae;r up &amp; dydon to hearme swa hwet swa hi don mihton.

 &amp; l&ae;ddon nor&d; mid heom. swa &t;et seo scyre &amp; &t;a o&d;ra scyre &t;e &t;&ae;r neh sindon. wurdon fela wintra &t;e wyrsan. 
 &amp; Tostig eorl. and his wif &amp; ealle &t;a &t;e woldon &t;&ae;t he wolde. foron su&d; ofer s&ae; mid him to Baldewine eorle. &amp; he hig ealle underfeng. &amp; hi w&ae;ron ealne &t;one winter &t;&ae;r. 
 On &t;issum geare man halgode &t;et mynster &ae;t Westmynster on Cildam&ae;ssed&ae;g. 
 &amp; se cyng Eadward for&d;ferde on twelfta m&ae;sse &ae;fen. &amp; hine mann bebyrgede on twelftan m&ae;ssed&ae;g. innan &t;&ae;re niwan halgodre circean on Westmynstre. 
 &amp; Harold eorl feng to Englalandes cynerice. swa swa se cyng hit him geu&d;e. &amp; eac men hine &t;&ae;r togecuron. &amp; w&ae;s gebletsod to cynge on twelftan m&ae;ssed&ae;g. 
 &amp; &t;y ilcan geare &t;e he cyng w&ae;s. he for ut mid sciphere togeanes Willelme. 
 &amp; &t;a hwile com Tostig. eorl into Humbran mid lx scipum. Eadwine eorl com mid landfyrde. &amp; draf hine ut. &amp; &t;a butse carlas hine forsocan. 
 &amp; he for to Scotlande mid xii snaccum. &amp; hine gemette Harold se Norrena cyng mid ccc scipum. &amp; Tostig him tobeah. 
 &amp; hi b&ae;gen foran into Humbran. o&d; &t;et hi coman to Eoferwic. &amp; heom wi&d;feaht Morkere eorl. &amp; Eadwine eorl. &amp; se Norrena cyng ahte siges geweald. 
 &amp; man cydde Harolde cyng hu hit w&ae;s &t;&ae;r gedon &amp; geworden. &amp; he com mid mycclum here Engliscra manna. &amp; gemette hine &ae;t St&ae;ngfordes brycge. &amp; hine ofsloh. &amp; &t;one eorl Tostig. &amp; eallne &t;one here ahtlice ofercom. 
 &amp; &t;a hwile com Willelm eorl upp &ae;t Hestingan on sancte Michaeles m&ae;ssed&ae;g. &amp; Harold com nor&d;an &amp; him wi&d;feaht ear &t;an &t;e his here come eall. &amp; &t;&ae;r he feoll. &amp; his tw&ae;gen gebro&d;ra Gyr&d; &amp; Leofwine. 
 &amp; Willelm &t;is land geeode. &amp; com to Westmynstre. &amp; Ealdred arcebiscop hine to cynge gehalgode. &amp; menn guldon him gyld. &amp; gislas sealdon. &amp; sy&d;&d;an heora land bohtan. 
 &amp; &d;a w&ae;s Leofric abbot of Burh &ae;t &t;&ae;t ilca feord. &amp; s&ae;clode &t;&ae;r &amp; com ham. &amp; w&ae;s d&ae;d sone &t;&ae;r &ae;fter on &ae;lre halgan m&ae;sseniht. 
 God are his saule. 
 On his d&ae;g w&ae;s ealle blisse &amp; ealle gode on Burh. &amp; he w&ae;s leaf eall folc. swa &t;&ae;t se cyng geaf sancte Peter &amp; him &t;&ae;t abbotrice on Byrtune. &amp; se of Couentre &t;&ae;t se eorl Leofric &t;e w&ae;s his eam &ae;r heafde macod. &amp; se of Crulande. &amp; se of &t;orneie. 
 &amp; he dyde swa mycel to gode into &t;&ae;t mynstre of Burh on golde &amp; on seolfre &amp; on scrud &amp; on lande. swa nefre nan o&d;re ne dyde toforen him ne nan &ae;fter him. 
 &T;a wear&d; gildene burh to wrecce burh. 
 &D;a cusen &t;a munecas to abbot Brand prouost. for&d;an &t;&ae;t he w&ae;s swi&d;e god man &amp; swi&d;e wis. &amp; senden him &t;a to &AE;dgar &ae;&d;eling. for&d;an &t;et &t;e landfolc wendon &t;&ae;t he sceolde cyng wur&d;en. &amp; se &ae;&d;eling hit him geatte &t;a bli&t;olice. 
 &T;a &t;e cyng Willelm geherde &t;&ae;t secgen. &t;a wear&d; he swi&d;e wra&d;. &amp; s&ae;de &t;&ae;t se abbot him heafde forsegon. 
 &T;a eodon gode men heom betwenen &amp; sahtloden heom for&d;an &t;&ae;t se abbot w&ae;s goddera manne. 
 Geaf &t;a &t;one cyng xl marc goldes to sahtnysse. &amp; &t;a lifede he litle hwile &t;&ae;r &ae;fter buton &t;ry gear. 
 Sy&d;&d;on comen ealle dr&ae;uednysse &amp; ealle ifele to &t;one mynstre. 
 God his gemyltse. 
 Her for se cyng ofer s&ae;. &amp; h&ae;fde mid him gislas &amp; sceattas. 
 &amp; com &t;&ae;s o&d;res geares on sancte Nicolaes m&ae;ssed&ae;g. &amp; &t;&ae;s d&ae;ges forbearn Cristes cyrce on Cantwarabyrig. 
 &amp; he geaf &ae;lces mannes land &t;a he ongean com.
