 Her on &t;issum geare Willelm cyng geaf Rodberde eorle &t;one eorldom on Nor&d;hymbraland. 
 &D;a comon &t;a landesmenn togeanes him. &amp; hine ofslogon. &amp; ix hund manna mid him. 
 And Eadgar &ae;&d;eling com &t;a mid eallum Nor&d;hymbram to Eoferwic. &amp; &t;a portmen wi&d; hine gri&d;edon. 
 &amp; se cyng Willelm com su&d;an mid eallan his fyrde. &amp; &t;a burh forhergode. &amp; fela hund manna ofsloh. &amp; se &ae;&d;eling for eft to Scotlande. 
 Her man wr&ae;gde &t;one biscop &AE;gelric on Burh. &amp; sende hine to Westmynstre. &amp; utlagode his bro&d;er &AE;gelwine biscop. 
 &T;a betwyx &t;am twam sancta Marian m&ae;ssan. comon easton of D&ae;nmarcun mid ccc scipum. &t;&ae;t w&ae;ron Sw&ae;gnes sunan cynges. &amp; his bro&d;er Osbearn eorl. 
 &amp; &t;a ferde se eorl Wal&d;eaf ut. &amp; com he &amp; Eadgar &ae;&d;eling. &amp; fela hund manna mid heom. &amp; gemetton &t;et li&d; innan Humbran. 
 &amp; ferdon to Eoferwic. &amp; upp eodan &amp; &t;a castelas gewunnan. &amp; ofslogon fela hund manna. &amp; to scipe l&ae;ddon sceattas fela. &amp; &t;a heafodmen h&ae;fdon on beandon. &amp; lagon betwyx Vsan &amp; Trentan ealne &t;one winter. 
 &amp; se cyng Willelm for into &t;&ae;re scire. &amp; hi eall fordyde. 
 &amp; on &t;isum ilcan geare for&d;ferde Brand abbod of Burh. on v kalend&ae; Decembris. 
 Her se eorl Wal&t;eof gri&d;ede wi&d; &t;one cyng. &amp; &t;&ae;s on lengten se cyng let hergian ealle &t;a mynstra &t;e on Englalande w&ae;ron. 
 &T;a on &t;am ilcan geare com Swegn cyng of Denmarcan into Humbran. &amp; &t;&ae;t landfolc comen him ongean &amp; gri&d;edon wi&d; hine w&ae;ndon &t;&ae;t he sceolde &t;et land ofergan. 
 &T;a comen into Elig Cristien &t;a Densce biscop &amp; Osbearn eorl &amp; &t;a Densca huscarles mid heom. 
 &amp; &t;et Englisce folc of eall &t;a feonlandes comen to heom. wendon &t;&ae;t hi sceoldon winnon eall &t;&ae;t land. 
 &T;a herdon &t;a munecas of Burh s&ae;gen &t;&ae;t heora agene menn wolden hergon &t;one mynstre  &t;&ae;t w&ae;s Hereward &amp; his genge. 
 &T;&ae;t w&ae;s for&d;an &t;et hi herdon s&ae;cgen &t;et se cyng heafde gifen &t;&ae;t abbotrice an Frencisce abbot Turolde w&ae;s gehaten. &amp; &t;&ae;t he w&ae;s swi&d;e styrne man. &amp; w&ae;s cumen &t;a into Stanforde mid ealle hise Frencisce menn. 
 &T;a w&ae;s &t;&ae;re an cyrceweard Yware w&ae;s gehaten. nam &t;a be nihte eall &t;et he mihte. &t;et w&ae;ron Cristes bec &amp; m&ae;ssehakeles &amp; cantelcapas &amp; reafes &amp; swilce litles hwat. swa hwat swa he mihte. 
 &amp; ferde sona &ae;r d&ae;g to &t;one abbot Turolde &amp; s&ae;gde him &t;&ae;t he sohte his gri&d;e. &amp; cydde him hu &t;a utlages sceolden cumen to Burh. &t;&ae;t he dyde eall be &t;&ae;re munece r&ae;de. 
 &T;a sona on morgen comen ealle &t;a utlaga mid fela scipe  &amp; woldon into &t;am mynstre. &amp; &t;a munecas wi&d;stoden &t;&ae;t hi na mihton incumen. 
 &T;a l&ae;gdon hi fyr on. &amp; forb&ae;rndon ealle &t;a munece huses &amp; eall &t;a tun buton ane huse. 
 &T;a comen hi &t;urh fyre in &ae;t Bolhi&d;e geate. &amp; &t;a munecas comen heom togeanes. beaden heom gri&d;  ac hi na rohten na &t;ing. 
 Geodon into &t;e mynstre. clumben upp to &t;e halge rode. namen &t;a &t;e kynehelm of ure Drihtnes heafod eall of smeate golde. namen &t;a &t;et fotspure &t;e w&ae;s undern&ae;&d;en his fote. &t;&ae;t w&ae;s eall of read golde. 
 Clumben upp to &t;e stepel. brohton dune &t;&ae;t h&ae;cce &t;e &t;&ae;r w&ae;s behid. hit w&ae;s eall of gold &amp; of seolfre. hi namen &t;&ae;re twa gildene scrines &amp; ix seolferne. 
 &amp; hi namen fiftene mycele roden. ge of golde ge of seolfre. 
 Hi namen &t;&ae;re swa mycele gold &amp; seolfre &amp; swa manega gersumas on sceat &amp; on scrud &amp; on bokes swa nan man ne m&ae;i o&d;er t&ae;llen. s&ae;gdon &t;&ae;t hi hit dyden for &d;es mynstres holdscipe. 
 Sy&d;&d;on geden heom to scipe. ferden heom to Elig  bet&ae;htan &t;&ae;r &t;a ealla &t;a g&ae;rsume; 
 &T;a Denesc&ae; menn w&ae;ndon &t;&ae;t hi sceoldon ofercumen &t;a Frencisca men. &t;a todrefodon ealle &t;a munekes. beleaf &t;&ae;r nan butan an munec he w&ae;s gehaten Leofwine lange. he l&ae;i seoc in &t;a secr&ae;man in. 
 &D;a com Turold abbot &amp; &ae;hte si&t;e twenti Frencisce men mid him &amp; ealle fullwepnode. 
 &T;a he &t;ider com &t;a fand he forb&ae;rnd wi&d;innan &amp; wi&d;utan. eall butan &t;a cyrece ane. 
 &T;a w&ae;ron &t;a utlagas ealle on flote. wistan &t;&ae;t he scolde &t;ider cumen. 
 &T;is w&ae;s don &t;&ae;s d&ae;ges iiii Non&ae; Iunii. 
 &T;a twegen kyngas Willelm &amp; Sw&ae;gn wur&d;on s&ae;htlod. &t;a ferdon &t;a D&ae;nesca menn ut of Elig mid ealle &t;a forenspr&ae;cena g&ae;rsume &amp; l&ae;ddon mid heom. 
 &T;a hi comen on middewarde &t;e s&ae;. &t;a com an mycel storm &amp; todr&ae;fede ealle &t;a scipe &t;&ae;r &t;a gersumes w&ae;ron inne. sume ferdon to Norw&ae;ge. sume to Yrlande. sume to D&ae;nmarce. 
 &amp; eall &t;&ae;t &t;ider com &t;&ae;t w&ae;s &t;one h&ae;cce &amp; sume scrine &amp; sume roden &amp; fela of &t;a o&d;re g&ae;rsume. &amp; brohten hit to an cynges tun hatte. &amp; dyden hit eall &t;a in &t;one cyrce. 
 &D;a sy&d;&d;on &t;urh heora gemelest &amp; &t;urh heora druncenhed on an niht forb&ae;rnde &t;a cyrce. &amp; eall &t;et &t;&ae;r inn&ae; w&ae;s. 
 &D;us w&ae;s se mynstre of Burch forb&ae;rnd &amp; forh&ae;rgod. 
 &AE;lmihtig God hit gemiltse &t;urh his mycele mildhertnesse. 
 And &t;us se abbot Turolde com to Burh. &amp; &t;a munecas comen &t;a ongean. &amp; dydan Cristes &t;eudom in &t;&ae;re cyrce. &t;&ae;t &ae;r h&ae;fde standen fulle seofeniht forutan &ae;lces cynnes riht. 
 &D;a herde &AE;gelric biscop &t;et gesecgon. &t;a amansumede he ealle &t;a men &t;a &t;&ae;t yfel d&ae;de h&ae;fden don. 
 &D;a w&ae;s mycel hunger &t;&ae;s geares. 
 &amp; &t;a &t;&ae;s sumeres com &t;et li&d; nor&d;an of Humbran into T&ae;mese. &amp; lagon &t;&ae;r twa niht. &amp; heoldan sy&d;&d;on to D&ae;nmercan. 
 And Baldewine eorl for&d;ferde. &amp; his sunu Arnulf feng to rice. 
 &amp; Willelm eorl sceolde ben his geheald. &amp; Franca cyng eac. &amp; com &t;a Rodbriht eorl &amp; ofsloh his m&ae;g Arnulf. &amp; &t;one eorl. &amp; &t;one cyng aflymda. and his menn ofsloh fela &t;usenda. 
 Her &AE;dwine eorl &amp; Morkere eorl uthlupon &amp; mislice ferdon on wudu &amp; on felda. 
 &D;a gewende Morkere eorl to Elig on scipe. And Eadwine eorl wear&d; ofslagen arhlice fram his agenum mannum. 
 &amp; com se biscop Egelwine. &amp; Siward Bearn. &amp; fela hund manna mid heom into Elig. 
 &amp; &t;a &t;e se cyng Willelm &t;&ae;t geaxode. &t;a bead he ut scipfyrde &amp; landfyrde. &amp; &t;et land abutan s&ae;t. &amp; brycge gewrohte. &amp; inn for. &amp; seo scipfyrde on &t;a s&ae;healfe. 
 &amp; &t;a utlagan &t;a ealle on hand eodan. &t;&ae;t w&ae;s Egelwine biscop. &amp; Morkere eorl. &amp; ealle &t;a &t;e mid heom w&ae;ron buton Herewarde ane. 
 &amp; ealle &t;a &t;e mid him woldon. &amp; he hi ahtlice utl&ae;dde. 
 &amp; se cyng genam scipa &amp; w&ae;pna &amp; sceattas manega. &amp; &t;a men he ateah swa swa he wolde. &amp; &t;one biscop Egelwine he sende to Abbandune. &amp; he &t;&ae;r for&d;ferde sona &t;&ae;s wintres. 
 Her Willelm cyng l&ae;dde scipfyrde &amp; landfyrde to Scotlande. &amp; &t;&ae;t land on &t;a s&ae;healfe mid scipum ymbel&ae;g. &amp; his landfyrde &ae;t &t;am Gew&ae;de innl&ae;dde. &amp; he &t;&ae;r naht ne funde &t;&ae;s &t;e him &t;e bet w&ae;re. 
 &amp; se cyng Melcolm com &amp; gri&d;ede wi&d; &t;one cyng Willelm &amp; gislas sealde. &amp; his man w&ae;s. 
 &amp; se cyng ham gewende mid ealre his fyrde. 
 &amp; se biscop Egelric for&d;ferde. he w&ae;s to biscop hadod to Eoferwic. ac hit w&ae;s mid unrihte him ofgenumon. 
 &amp; man geaf him &t;&ae;t biscoprice on Dunholme. &amp; he heafde hit &t;a hwile &t;e he wolde. &amp; forlet hit sy&d;&d;an. &amp; ferde to Burch to sancte Petres mynstre. &amp; &t;&ae;r drohtnode xii gear. 
 &D;a &ae;fter &t;am &t;e Willelm cyng gewan Englalande. &t;a nam he hine of Burch &amp; sende hine to Westmynstre. 
 &amp; he for&d;ferde on IDus Octobris. &amp; he is bebyrged &t;&ae;r innan &t;am mynstre. innon sanctus Nicolaus portice. 
 On &t;isum geare Willelm cyng l&ae;dde Engliscne here &amp; Frencisce ofer s&ae;. &amp; gewan &t;&ae;t land Mans. 
 &amp; hit Englisce men swy&d;e amyrdon. wingear&d;as hi fordydon. &amp; burga forb&ae;rndon. &amp; swi&d;e &t;et land amyrdon. &amp; hit eall abegdon Willelme to handa. 
 &amp; hi sy&d;&d;on ham gewendon to Englalande. 
 On &t;isum geare for Willelm cyng ofer s&ae; to Normandig. &amp; Eadgar cild com of Scotland to Normandige. 
 &amp; se cyng hine geinlagode. &amp; ealle his men. &amp; he w&ae;s on &t;es cynges hyrede. &amp; nam swilce gerihta swa se cyng him geu&d;e. 
 On &t;isum geare Willelm cyng geaf Raulfe eorle Willelmes dohtor Osbearnes sunu. &amp; se ylca Raulf w&ae;s Bryttisc on his moderhealfe. &amp; his f&ae;der w&ae;s Englisc Raulf hatte. &amp; w&ae;s geboren on Nor&d;folc. 
 &T;a geaf se cyng his sunu &t;one eorldom on Nor&d;folc. &amp; Su&d;folc. &t;a l&ae;dde he &t;&ae;t wif to Nor&d;wic. 
 &T;&ae;r wes &t;&ae;t brydeala mannum to beala. 
 &D;&ae;r w&ae;s Roger eorl. &amp; Wal&t;eof eorl. &amp; biscopas &amp; abbotes. &amp; r&ae;ddon &t;&ae;r swa &t;&ae;t hi woldon &t;one cyng gesettan ut of Englelandes cynedome. 
 &amp; hit wear&d; sona gecydd &t;am cynge to Normandige hu hit w&ae;s ger&ae;d. &t;&ae;t w&ae;s Roger eorl. &amp; Raulf eorl. &t;e w&ae;ron yldast to &d;am unreode. &amp; hi speonan &t;a Bryttas heom to. &amp; sendon east to Denmearcan &ae;fter sciphere heom to fultume. 
 &amp; Roger ferde west to his eorldome. &amp; gegaderode his folc to &t;&ae;s cynges un&t;earfe. ac he wear&d; gelet. 
 &amp; Raulf eac on his eorldome wolde for&d;gan mid his folce. ac &t;a castelmen &t;e w&ae;ron on Englalande &amp; eac &t;&ae;t landfolc him togeanes comen. &amp; gemacodon &t;&ae;t he naht ne dyde. ac for to scipe &ae;t Nor&d;wic. 
 &amp; his wif w&ae;s innan &t;am castele. &amp; hine heold swa lange &t;&ae;t man hire gri&d; sealde. &amp; heo ut ferde &t;a of Englalande. &amp; ealle hire men &t;e hire mid woldon. 
 &amp; se cyng si&d;&d;an com to Englalande. &amp; genam Roger eorl his m&ae;g. &amp; gefestnode hine. &amp; Wal&t;eof eorl he genam eac. 
 &amp; sona &ae;fter &t;am comon eastan of Denmearcan cc scipa. &amp; &t;&ae;r on w&ae;ron tw&ae;gen heafodmenn. Cnut Sw&ae;gnes sunu. &amp; Hacun eorl. &amp; hi ne dorstan nan gefeoht healdan wi&d; Willelm cynge. ac heoldon ofer s&ae; to Flandran. 
 &amp; Eadgi&d; seo hl&ae;fdig for&d;ferde on Winceastre vii nihton &ae;r Cristes m&ae;ssan. &amp; se cyng hi let bryngan to Westmynstre mid mycclan wur&d;scipe. &amp; l&ae;gde hi wi&d; Eadward kyng hire hlaforde. 
 &amp; se w&ae;s on Westmynstre &t;one midewinter. &amp; man fordyde &t;&ae;r ealle &t;a Bryttas &t;e w&ae;ron &ae;t &t;am brydealo&d; &ae;t Nor&d;wic. 
 Sume hy wurdon abl&ae;nde &amp; sume of land adrifene. swa wurdon Willelmes swican geni&d;rade.

 &amp; se cyng geaf Westmynster Vithele abbode se w&ae;s &ae;r abbod on B&ae;rnege. &amp; Wal&t;eof eorl wes beheafdod on Winceastre. &amp; his lic wear&d; gelead to Crulande. 
 &amp; se cyng for ofer s&ae;. &amp; l&ae;dde his fyrde to Brytlande. &amp; beset &t;one castel Dol. 
 &amp; &t;a Bryttas hine heoldon &t;&ae;t se cyng com of Francland. &amp; Willelm &t;anon for. &amp; &t;&ae;r forleas &ae;g&d;er ge men ge hors. &amp; feola his gersuma. 
 Her on &t;isum geare wurdon s&ae;hte Franca cyng &amp; Willelm Englalandes cyng. ac hit heold litle hwile. 
 &amp; &d;es geares forbarn Lundenburh anre nihte &ae;r Assumptio sancte Mari&ae; swa swy&d;e swa heo n&ae;fre &ae;r n&ae;s sy&d;&t;an heo gestabeled w&ae;s. 
 And on &t;isum geare for&d;fyrde &AE;gelwig abbod on Euesham on &t;am d&ae;ge xiv kalend&ae; Marcii. And Hereman biscop eac for&d;ferde on &t;am d&ae;ge x kalend&ae; Marcii. 
 On &t;isum geare com Melcolm cyng of Scotlande into Englelande betwyx &t;am twam Mariam m&ae;ssan mid mycclum fyrde. &amp; gehergode Nor&d;hymbraland o&d; hit com to Tine. &amp; ofsloh feala hund manna. &amp; ham l&ae;dde manige sceattas. &amp; gersuma. &amp; menn on heftninge. 
 And &t;i ilcan geare se cyng Willelm gefeaht togeanes his sunu Rotbearde wi&d;utan Normandige be anum castele Gerborne&d; hatte. &amp; se cyng Willelm wear&d; &t;&ae;r gewundod. &amp; his hors ofslagen &t;e he on s&ae;t. &amp; eac his sunu Willelm wear&d; &t;&ae;r gewundod. &amp; fela manna ofslagene. 
 On &t;isum geare w&ae;s se biscop Walchere ofslagen on Dunholme &ae;t anum gemote. &amp; an hund manna mid him Frencisce &amp; Flemisce. &amp; he sylf w&ae;s on Hlo&d;eringa geboren. &t;is dydon Nor&d;hymbran on Maies mon&d;e. 
 ON &t;isum geare se cyng l&ae;dde fyrde into Wealan. &amp; &t;&ae;r gefreode fela hund manna. 
 Her nam se cyng Odan biscop. &amp; her w&ae;s mycel hungor. 
 On &t;isum geare aras seo ungehw&ae;rnes on Gl&ae;stingabyrig betwyx &t;am abbode &T;urstane. &amp; his munecan. 
 &AE;rest hit com of &t;&ae;s abbotes unwisdome. &t;&ae;t he misbead his munecan on fela &t;ingan. 
 &amp; &d;a munecas hit m&ae;ndon lufelice to him. &amp; beadon hine &t;&ae;t he sceolde healdan hi rihtlice. &amp; lufian hi. &amp; hi woldon him beon holde. &amp; gehyrsume. 
 Ac se abbot nolde &t;&ae;s naht. ac dyde heom yfele. &amp; beheot heom wyrs. 
 Anes d&ae;ges &t;e abbot eode into capitulan. &amp; spr&ae;c uppon &t;a munecas. &amp; wolde hi mistukian. 
 &amp; sende &ae;fter l&ae;wede mannum. &amp; hi comon into capitulan on uppon &t;a munecas full gewepnede. &amp; &t;a w&ae;ron &t;a munecas swi&d;e aferede of heom. nyston hwet heom to donne w&ae;re. 
 Ac to scuton. sume urnon into cyrcean. &amp; belucan &t;a duran into heom. &amp; hi ferdon &ae;fter heom into &t;am mynstre. &amp; woldon hit utdragan. &t;a&d;a hig ne dorsten na utgan. 
 Ac reowlic &t;ing &t;&ae;r gelamp on d&ae;g. &t;&ae;t &t;a Frencisce men br&ae;cen &t;one chor &amp; torfedon tow&ae;rd &t;am weofode &t;&ae;r &d;a munecas w&ae;ron. &amp; sume of &d;am cnihtan ferdon uppon &t;one uppflore. &amp; scotedon adunweard mid arewan toweard &t;am haligdome. swa &t;&ae;t on &t;&ae;re rode &t;e stod bufon &t;am weofode sticodon on m&ae;nige arewan. 
 &amp; &t;a wreccan munecas lagon onbuton &t;am weofode. &amp; sume crupon under. &amp; gyrne cleopedon to Gode his miltse biddende. &t;a &t;a hi ne mihton nane miltse &ae;t mannum begytan. 
 Hw&ae;t magon we secgean. buton &t;&ae;t hi scotedon swi&d;e. &amp; &t;a o&d;re &d;a dura br&ae;con &t;&ae;r adune &amp; eodon inn. 
 &amp; ofslogon sume &t;a munecas to dea&d;e. &amp; m&ae;nige gewundedon &t;&ae;rinne. swa &t;&ae;t &d;et blod com of &d;am weofode uppon &t;am gradan. &amp; of &d;am gradan on &t;a flore. 
 &T;reo &t;&ae;r w&ae;ron ofslagene to dea&d;e. &amp; eahteteone gewundade. 
 &amp; on &t;&ae;s ilcan geares for&d;ferde Mahtild Willelmes cynges cwen. on &t;one d&ae;g &ae;fter ealra halgena m&ae;ssed&ae;g. 
 And on &t;es ylcan geares &ae;fter midewintre se cyng let beodan mycel gyld &amp; hefelic ofer eall Englaland. &t;&ae;t w&ae;s &ae;t &ae;lcere hyde twa &amp; hund seofenti peanega. 
 Her on &d;isum geare for&d;ferde Wulfuuold abbod on Ceortesege. on &t;am d&ae;ge xiii kalend&ae; Mai. 
 On &t;isum geare menn cwydodon &amp; to so&d;an s&ae;dan. &t;&ae;t Cnut cyng of Denmearcan Sw&ae;gnes sune cynges fundade hiderward. &amp; wolde gewinnan &t;is land mid Rodbeardes eorles fultume of Flandran. for&d;an &t;e Cnut heafde Rodbeardes dohter. 
 &D;a Willelm Englalandes cyng &t;e &t;a w&ae;s sittende on Normandige. for&d;ig he ahte &ae;g&d;er ge Englaland ge Normandige. &t;is geaxode. he ferde into Englalande mid swa mycclan here ridendra manna. &amp; gangendra of Francrice and of Brytlande. swa n&ae;fre &ae;r &t;is land ne gesohte. swa &t;&ae;t menn wundredon hu &t;is land mihte eall &t;one here afedan. 
 Ac se cyng let toscyfton &t;one here geond eall &t;is land to his mannon. &amp; hi f&ae;ddon &t;one here &ae;lc be his landefne. 
 &amp; men heafdon mycel geswinc &t;&ae;s geares. &amp; se cyng lett awestan &t;&ae;t land abutan &t;a s&ae;. &t;et gif his feond comen upp. &t;&ae;t hi n&ae;fdon na on hwam hi fengon swa r&ae;dlice. 
 Ac &t;a se cyng geaxode to so&d;an &t;&ae;t his feond gel&ae;tte w&ae;ron. &amp; ne mihten na gefor&d;ian heora fare. &t;a lett he sum &t;one here faren to heora agene lande. &amp; sum he heold on &t;isum lande ofer winter. 
 &D;a to &t;am midewintre w&ae;s se cyng on Gleaweceastre mid his witan. &amp; heold &t;&ae;r his hired v dagas. &amp; sy&d;&d;an &t;e arcebiscop &amp; gehadode men h&ae;fden sino&d; &t;reo dagas. 
 &D;&ae;r w&ae;s Mauricius gecoren to biscop on Lundene. &amp; Willelm to Nor&d;folce &amp; Rodbeard to Ceasterscire. hi w&ae;ron ealle &t;&ae;s cynges clerecas. 
 &AE;fter &t;isum h&ae;fde se cyng mycel ge&t;eaht. &amp; swi&d;e deope sp&ae;ce wi&d; his witan ymbe &t;is land hu hit w&ae;re gesett. o&d;&d;e mid hwylcon mannon. 
 Sende &t;a ofer eall Englaland into &ae;lcere scire his men. &amp; lett agan ut hu fela hundred hyda w&ae;ron innon &t;&ae;re scire. o&d;&d;e hwet se cyng him sylf h&ae;fde landes. &amp; orfes innan &t;am lande. o&d;&d;e hwilce geriht&ae; he ahte to habbanne to xii mon&t;um of &d;&ae;re scire. 
 Eac he lett gewritan hu mycel landes his arcebiscops h&ae;fdon. &amp; his leodbiscops. &amp; his abbods. &amp; his eorlas. &amp; &t;eah ic hit lengre telle. hw&ae;t o&d;&d;e hu mycel &ae;lc mann h&ae;fde &t;e landsittende w&ae;s innan Englalande. on lande. o&d;&d;e on orfe. &amp; hu mycel feos hit w&ae;re wur&d;. 
 Swa swy&d;e nearwelice he hit lett ut aspyrian. &t;&ae;t n&ae;s an &ae;lpig hide. ne an gyrde landes. ne fur&d;on  hit is sceame to tellanne. ac hit ne &t;uhte him nan sceame to donne. an oxe. ne an cu. ne an swin. n&ae;s belyfon. &t;&ae;t n&ae;s ges&ae;t on his gewrite. 
 &amp; ealle &t;a gewrita w&ae;ron gebroht to him sy&d;&d;an. 
 Her se cyng b&ae;r his corona &amp; heold his hired on Winceastre to &t;am Eastran. &amp; swa he ferde &t;&ae;t he w&ae;s to &t;am Pentecosten &ae;t W&ae;stminstre. &amp; dubbade his sunu Henric to ridere &t;&ae;r. 
 Sy&d;&d;an he ferde abutan swa &t;&ae;t he com to Lamm&ae;ssan to Searebyrig. &amp; &t;&ae;r him comon to his witan. and ealle &t;a landsittende men. &t;e ahtes w&ae;ron ofer eall Engleland. w&ae;ron &t;&ae;s mannes men &t;e hi w&ae;ron. 
 &amp; ealle hi bugon to him. &amp; weron his menn. &amp; him holda&d;as sworon &t;&ae;t hi woldon ongean ealle o&d;re men him holde beon. 
 &D;anon he ferde into Wiht. for&t;ig he wolde faran into Normandige &amp; swa dyde sy&d;&d;an. 
 And &t;eah he dyde &ae;rest &ae;fter his gewunan. begeat swi&d;e mycelne sceatt of his mannan &t;&ae;r he mihte &ae;nige teale tohabban o&d;&d;e mid rihte o&d;&d;e elles. 
 Ferde &t;a sy&d;&d;an into Normandige. &amp; Eadgar &AE;&t;eling &AE;dwardes m&ae;g cynges beah &t;a fram him for&t;ig he n&ae;fde na mycelne wur&d;scipe of him. ac se &ae;lmihtiga God him gife wur&d;scipe on &t;am toweardan. 
 &amp; Cristina &t;&ae;s &ae;&d;elinges swuster beah into mynstre to Rumesege. &amp; underfeng halig rest. 
 &amp; &t;&ae;s ilcan geares w&ae;s swi&d;e hefelic gear. &amp; swi&d;e swincfull &amp; sorhfull gear innan Englelande on orfcwealme. &amp; corn. &amp; w&ae;stmas w&ae;ron &ae;tstandene. 
 &amp; swa mycel ungelimp on w&ae;derunge. swa man naht &ae;&d;elice ge&t;encean ne m&ae;g. swa stor &t;unring. &amp; l&ae;gt wes. swa &t;&ae;t hit acwealde manige men. &amp; aa hit wyrsode mid mannan swi&d;or &amp; swi&d;or. 
 GEbete hit God elmihtiga. &t;onne his willa sy. 
 &AE;fter ure Drihtnes H&ae;lendes Cristes gebyrtide. an &t;usend wintra &amp; seofan &amp; hundeahtatig wintra. on &t;am an &amp; twentigan geare &t;&ae;s &t;e Willelm weolde &amp; stihte Engleland swa him God u&d;e. gewear&d; swi&d;e hefelic and swi&d;e woldberendlic gear on &t;issum lande. 
 Swylc co&d;e com on mannum. &t;&ae;t fullneah &ae;fre &t;e o&d;er man wear&d; on &t;am wyrrestan yfele. &t;et is on &d;am drife. &amp; &t;et swa stranglice. &t;&ae;t m&ae;nige menn swulton on &d;am yfele. 
 Sy&d;&d;an com &t;urh &t;a mycclan ungewiderunge &t;e comon swa we beforan tealdon. swy&d;e mycel hungor ofer eall Engleland. &t;&ae;t manig hundred manna earmlice dea&d;e swulton &t;urh &t;one hungor. 
 Eala hu earmlice &amp; hu reowlic tid w&ae;s &d;a. 
 &D;a &d;a wrecc&ae; men l&ae;gen fordrifene fullneah to dea&d;e. &amp; sy&d;&d;an com se scearpa hungor &amp; adyde hi mid ealle. 
 Hwam ne m&ae;g earmian swylcere tide? 
 O&d;&d;e hwa is swa heardheort &t;&ae;t ne m&ae;g wepan swylces ungelimpes? 
 Ac swylce &t;ing gewur&d;a&t; for folces synna &t;&ae;t hi nella&d; lufian God &amp; rihtwisnesse. 
 Swa swa hit w&ae;s &t;a on &d;am dagum. &t;&ae;t litel rihtwisnesse w&ae;s on &t;isum lande mid &ae;nige menn. buton mid munecan ane &t;&ae;r &t;&ae;r hi w&ae;ll ferdon. 
 Se cyng &amp; &t;a heafod men lufedon swi&d;e &amp; oferswi&d;e gitsunge. on golde. &amp; on seolfre. &amp; ne rohtan hu synlice hit w&ae;re begytan buton hit come to heom. 
 Se cyng sealde his land swa deore to male. swa heo deorost mihte. 
 &D;onne com sum o&d;er &amp; bead mare &t;onne &t;e o&d;er &ae;r sealde. &amp; se cyng hit lett &t;am menn &t;e him mare bead. 
 &D;onne com se &t;ridde. &amp; bead geat mare. &amp; se cyng hit let &t;am men to handa &t;e him eallra meast bead. &amp; ne rohte na hu swi&d;e synlice &t;a gerefan hit begeatan of earme mannon. ne hu manige unlaga hi dydon. 
 Ac swa man swy&d;or sp&ae;c embe rihte lage. swa mann dyde mare unlaga. 
 Hy arerdon unrihte tollas. &amp; manige o&d;re unriht hi dydan. &t;e sindon earfe&t;e to areccenne. 
 Eac on &d;am ilcan geare &ae;tforan h&ae;rfeste forbarn &t;&ae;t halige mynster sancte Paule &t;e biscopstol on Lundene. &amp; m&ae;nige o&d;re mynstres. &amp; &t;&ae;t m&ae;ste d&ae;l &amp; &t;&ae;t rotteste ealle &t;&ae;re burh. 
 Swylce eac on &d;am ilcan timan forbarn fullneah &ae;lc heafodport on eallon Englalande. 
 Eala reowlic &amp; wependlic tid w&ae;s &t;&ae;s geares. &t;e swa manig ungelimp w&ae;s for&d;bringende. 
 Eac on &t;am ilcan geare toforan Assumptio sancte Marie for Willelm cyng of Normandige into France mid fyrde. &amp; hergode uppan his agenne hlaford Philippe &t;am cynge. 
 &amp; sloh of his mannon mycelne d&ae;l. &amp; forbearnde &t;a burh Ma&d;ante. &amp; ealle &t;a halige mynstres &t;e w&ae;ron innon &t;&ae;re burh. &amp; twegen halige menn &t;e hyrsumedon Gode on ancersettle wuniende. &t;&ae;r w&ae;ron forbearnde. 
 &D;issum &t;us gedone. se cyng Willelm cearde ongean to Normandige. 
 Reowlic &t;ing he dyde. &amp; reowlicor him gelamp. 
 Hu reowlicor? 
 Him geyfelade. &amp; &t;&ae;t him stranglice eglade. 
 Hw&ae;t m&ae;g ic teollan? 
 Se scearpa dea&d; &t;e ne forlet ne rice menn. ne heane. seo hine genam. 
 He swealt on Normandige on &t;one nextan d&ae;g &ae;fter natiuitas sancte Marie. &amp; man bebyrgede hine on Ca&t;um &ae;t sancte Stephanes mynstre. &ae;rer he hit ar&ae;rde. &amp; sy&d;&d;an m&ae;nifealdlice gegodade. 
 Eala hu leas &amp; hu unwrest is &t;ysses middaneardes wela. 
 Se &t;e w&ae;s &ae;rur rice cyng. &amp; maniges landes hlaford. he n&ae;fde &t;a ealles landes buton seofon fot m&ae;l. &amp; se &t;e w&ae;s hwilon gescrid mid golde. &amp; mid gimmum. he l&ae;g &t;a oferwrogen mid moldan. 
 He l&ae;fde &ae;fter him &t;reo sunan. Rodbeard het se yldesta. se w&ae;s eorl on Normandige &ae;fter him. se o&d;er het Willelm. &t;e b&ae;r &ae;fter him on Engleland &t;one kinehelm. Se &t;ridda het Heanric. &t;am se f&ae;der becw&ae;&d; gersuman unateallendlice. 
 Gif hwa gewilnige&d; to gewitane hu gedon mann he w&ae;s. o&d;&d;e hwilcne wur&d;scipe he h&ae;fde. o&d;&d;e hu fela lande he w&ae;re hlaford. &d;onne wille we be him awritan swa swa we hine ageaton. &d;e him on locodan. &amp; o&d;re hwile on his hirede wunedon. 
 Se cyng Willelm &t;e we embe speca&d; w&ae;s swi&d;e wisman. &amp; swi&d;e rice. &amp; wur&d;fulre and strengere &t;onne &ae;nig his foregenga w&ae;re. 
 He w&ae;s milde &t;am godum mannum &t;e God lufedon. &amp; ofer eall gemett stearc &t;am mannum &t;e wi&d;cw&ae;don his willan. 
 On &d;am ilcan steode &t;e God him geu&d;e &t;&ae;t he moste Engleland gegan. he arerde m&ae;re mynster. &amp; munecas &t;&ae;r ges&ae;tte. &amp; hit w&ae;ll gegodade. 
 On his dagan w&ae;s &t;&ae;t m&ae;re mynster on Cantwarbyrig getymbrad. &amp; eac swi&d;e manig o&d;er ofer eall Englaland. 
 Eac &t;is land w&ae;s swi&d;e afylled mid munecan. &amp; &t;a leofodan heora lif &ae;fter sanctus Benedictus regule. 
 &amp; se Cristendom w&ae;s swilc on his d&ae;ge &t;&ae;t &ae;lc man hw&ae;t his hade to belumpe. folgade se &t;e wolde. 
 Eac he w&ae;s swy&d;e wur&d;ful. &t;riwa he b&ae;r his cynehelm &ae;lce geare. swa oft swa he w&ae;s on Englelande. 
 On Eastron he hine b&ae;r on Winceastre. on Pentecosten on Westmynstre. on midewintre on Gleaweceastre. 
 &amp; &t;&ae;nne w&ae;ron mid him ealle &t;a rice men ofer eall Englaland. arcebiscopas. &amp; leodbiscopas. abbodas &amp; eorlas. &t;egnas &amp; cnihtas. 
 Swilce he w&ae;s eac swy&d;e stearc man &amp; r&ae;&d;e. swa &t;&ae;t man ne dorste nan &t;ing ongean his willan don. 
 He h&ae;fde eorlas on his bendum. &t;e dydan ongean his willan. 
 Biscopas he s&ae;tte of heora biscoprice. &amp; abbodas of heora abbodrice. &amp; &t;&ae;gnas on cweartern. &amp; &ae;t nextan he ne sparode his agenne bro&d;or. Odo het. 
 He w&ae;s swi&d;e rice biscop on Normandige. on Baius w&ae;s his biscopstol. &amp; w&ae;s manna fyrmest toeacan &t;am cynge. 
 &amp; he h&ae;fde eorldom on Englelande. &amp; &t;onne se cyng w&ae;s on Normandige. &t;onne w&ae;s he m&ae;gest on &t;isum lande. 
 &amp; hine he s&ae;tte on cweartern. 
 Betwyx o&d;rum &t;ingum nis na to forgytane &t;&ae;t gode fri&d; &t;e he macode on &t;isan lande. swa &t;&ae;t an man &t;e him sylf aht w&ae;re. mihte faran ofer his rice mid his bosum full goldes ungederad. &amp; nan man ne dorste slean o&d;erne man. n&ae;fde he n&ae;fre swa mycel yfel gedon wi&d; &t;one o&d;erne. 
 &amp; Gif hwilc carl man h&ae;mde wi&d; Wimman hire un&d;ances. sona he forleas &t;a limu &t;e he mid pleagode. 
 He rixade ofer Engl&ae;land. &amp; hit mid his geapscipe swa &t;urhsmeade. &t;&ae;t n&ae;s an hid landes innan Engl&ae;lande. &t;&ae;t he nyste hwa heo h&ae;fde. o&d;&d;e hw&ae;s heo wur&d; w&ae;s. &amp; sy&d;&d;an on his gewrit ges&ae;tt. 
 Brytland him w&ae;s on gewealde. &amp; he &t;&ae;r inne casteles gewrohte. &amp; &t;et Manncynn mid ealle gewealde. 
 Swilce eac Scotland he him under&t;&ae;dde. for his mycele streng&t;e. 
 Normandige &t;&ae;t land w&ae;s his gecynde. 
 &amp; ofer &t;one eorldom &t;e Mans is gehaten he rixade. 
 &amp; Gif he moste &t;a gyt twa gear libban. he h&ae;fde Yrlande mid his werscipe gewunnon. &amp; wi&d;utan &ae;lcon w&ae;pnon. 
 Witodlice on his timan h&ae;fdon men mycel geswinc. &amp; swi&d;e manige teonan. 
 Castelas he let wyrcean &amp; earme men swi&d;e swencean. 
 Se cyng w&ae;s swa swi&d;e stearc &amp; benam of his under&t;eoddan man manig marc goldes &amp; ma hundred punda seolfres. 
 &D;et he nam be wihte &amp; mid mycelan unrihte of his landleode for littelre neode. 
 He w&ae;s on gitsunge befeallan &amp; gr&ae;din&ae;sse he lufode mid ealle. 
 He s&ae;tte mycel deorfri&d; &amp; he l&ae;gde laga &t;&ae;rwi&d;  &t;&ae;t swa hwa swa sloge heort o&d;&d;e hinde  &t;&ae;t hine man sceolde blendian. 
 He forbead &t;a heortas swylce eac &t;a baras  swa swi&d;e he lufode &t;a headeor swilce he w&ae;re heora f&ae;der. 
 Eac he s&ae;tte be &t;am haran &t;&ae;t hi mosten freo faran. 
 His rice men hit m&ae;ndon &amp; &t;a earme men hit beceorodan. 
 Ac he w&ae;s swa sti&d; &t;&ae;t he ne rohte heora eallra ni&d;  ac hi moston mid ealle &t;es cynges wille folgian  gif hi woldon libban o&d;&d;e land habban  land o&d;&d;e eahta o&d;&d;e wel his sehta. 
 Wala wa  &t;&ae;t &ae;nig man sceolde modigan swa hine sylf upp ahebban &amp; ofer ealle men tellan. 
 Se &ae;lmihtiga God cy&t;&ae; his saule mildheortnisse &amp; do him his synna forgifenesse. 
 &D;as &t;ing we habba&d; be him gewritene. &ae;g&d;er ge gode ge yfele. &t;&ae;t &t;a godan men niman &ae;fter &t;eora godnesse. &amp; forleon mid ealle yfelnesse. &amp; gan on &d;one weg. &t;e us lett to heofonan rice. 
 Fela &t;inga we magon writan &t;e on &d;am ilcan geare gewordene w&ae;ron. 
 Swa hit w&ae;s on Denmearcan. &t;&ae;t &t;a D&ae;nescan &t;e w&ae;s &ae;rur geteald eallra folca getreowast. wurdon awende to &t;&ae;re meste untriw&d;e. &amp; to &t;am m&ae;sten swicdome &t;e &ae;fre mihte gewur&d;an. 
 Hi gecuron &amp; abugan to Cnute cynge. &amp; him a&d;as sworon. &amp; sy&d;&d;an hine earhlice ofslogon innan anre cyrcean. 
 Eac wear&d; on Ispanie &t;&ae;t &t;a h&ae;&d;enan men foran &amp; hergodan uppon &t;am Cristenan mannan. &amp; mycel abegdan to heora anwealde. 
 Ac se Cristena cyng  Anphos w&ae;s gehaten  he sende ofer eall into &ae;lcan lande. &amp; gyrnde fultumes. &amp; him com to fultum of &ae;lcen lande &t;e Cristen w&ae;s  &amp; ferdon &amp; ofslogon &amp; aweg adrifan eall &t;et h&ae;&d;ena folc. &amp; gewunnon heora land ongean. &t;urh Godes fultum. 
 Eac on &t;isan ilcan lande on &t;am ilcan geare. for&d;ferdon manega rice men. Stigand biscop of Ciceastre. &amp; se abbod of sancte Augustine. &amp; se abbod of Ba&d;on. &amp; &t;e of Perscoran. &amp; &d;a heora eallra hlaford Willelm Engl&ae;landes cyng. &t;e we &ae;r beforan embe sp&ae;con. 
 &AE;fter his dea&d;e his sune. Willelm h&ae;t eallswa &t;e f&ae;der. feng to &t;am rice &amp; wear&d; gebletsod to cynge fram Landfrance arcebiscop on Westmynstre. &t;reom dagum &ae;r Michaeles m&ae;ssed&ae;g. &amp; ealle &t;a men on Englalande him to abugon. &amp; him a&d;as sworon. 
 &D;isum &t;us gedone. se cyng ferde to Winceastre. &amp; sceawode &t;&ae;t madmehus. &amp; &t;a gersuman &t;e his f&ae;der &ae;r gegaderode. 
 &T;a w&ae;ron unasecgendlice &ae;nie men hu mycel &t;&ae;r w&ae;s gegaderod. on golde &amp; on seolfre. &amp; on faton. &amp; on p&ae;llan. &amp; on gimman. &amp; on manige o&d;re deorwur&d;e &t;ingon. &t;e earfo&d;e sindon to ateallene. 
 Se cyng dyde &t;a swa his f&ae;der him bebead &ae;r he dead w&ae;re. d&ae;lde &t;a gersuman for his f&ae;der saule. to &ae;lcen mynstre &t;e wes innan Englelande to suman mynstre x marc goldes. to suman vi &amp; to &ae;lcen cyrcean uppe land lx p&ae;nega. &amp; into &ae;lcere scire man seonde hundred punda feos. to d&ae;lanne earme mannan for his saule. 
 &amp; &ae;r he for&d;ferde he bead &t;&ae;t man sceolde unlesan ealle &t;a menn &t;e on h&ae;ftnunge w&ae;ron under his anwealde. 
 &amp; se cyng w&ae;s on &d;am midewintre on Lundene. 
 On &t;isum geare w&ae;s &t;is land swi&d;e astirad. &amp; mid mycele swicdome afylled. swa &t;&ae;t &t;a riceste Frencisce men &t;e weron innan &t;isan lande. wolden swican heora hlaforde &t;am cynge. &amp; woldon habban his bro&d;er to cynge Rodbeard &t;e w&ae;s eorl on Normandige. 
 On &t;isum r&ae;de w&ae;s &ae;rest Oda biscop. &amp; Gosfri&d; biscop. &amp; Willelm biscop on Dunholme. 
 Swa w&ae;ll dyde se cyng be &t;am biscop. &t;&ae;t eall Englaland f&ae;rde &ae;fter his r&ae;de. &amp; swa swa he wolde. &amp; he &t;ohte to donne be him eall swa Iudas Scarioth dyde be ure Drihtene. 
 &amp; Rogere eorl w&ae;s eac &ae;t &t;am unr&ae;de. &amp; swi&d;e mycel folc mid heom ealle Frencisce men. &amp; &t;&ae;s unr&ae;d w&ae;r&d; ger&ae;d innan &t;am lengtene. 
 Sona swa hit com to &t;am Eastron. &t;a ferdon hi &amp; hergodon &amp; b&ae;rndon &amp; aweston &t;&ae;s cynges feormehames. &amp; eallra &t;&ae;ra manna land hi fordydon &t;e w&ae;ron innan &t;&ae;s cynges holdscipe. 
 &amp; heora &ae;lc ferde to his castele. &amp; &t;one mannoden &amp; metsoden swa hig betst mihton. 
 Gosfri&d; biscop &amp; Rodbeard a Mundbr&ae;g ferdon to Bricgstowe &amp; hergodon &amp; brohton to &t;am castele &t;a hergunge. &amp; sy&d;&d;on foron ut of &d;am castele &amp; hergodon Ba&d;on. &amp; eall &t;&ae;t land &t;&ae;r abutan. &amp; eall Beorclea hyrnesse hi aw&ae;ston. 
 &amp; &d;a men &t;e yldest w&ae;ron of Hereforde. &amp; eall &t;eo scir for&d; mid. &amp; &t;a men of Scrobscyre mid mycele folce of Brytlande comon &amp; hergodon &amp; b&ae;rndon on Wi&d;receastrescire for&d; &t;&ae;t hi comon to &t;am porte sylfan. &amp; woldon &t;a &d;&ae;ne port b&ae;rnen. &amp; &t;&ae;t mynster reafian. &amp; &t;&ae;s cynges castel gewinnan heom to handa. 
 &D;as &t;ing geseonde se arwur&d;a biscop Wlstan. wear&d; swi&d;e gedrefed on his mode. for&d;ig him w&ae;s bet&ae;ht &t;e castel to healdene. 
 &T;eah hwe&d;er his hired men ferdon ut mid feawe mannan of &t;am castele. &amp; &t;urh Godes mildheortnisse &amp; &t;urh &t;&ae;s biscopas geearnunga ofslogon &amp; gel&ae;hton fif hundred manna. &amp; &t;a o&d;re ealle aflymdon. 
 Se biscop of Dunholme dyde to hearme &t;&ae;t he mihte ofer eall be nor&d;an. 
 Roger het an of heom. se hleop into &t;am castele &ae;t Nor&d;wic. &amp; dyde git eallra w&ae;rst ofer eall &t;&ae;t land. 
 Hugo eac an &t;e hit ne gebette nan &t;ing. ne innan L&ae;greceastrescire. ne innan Nor&d;hamtune. 
 &D;e biscop Odo &t;e &t;as &t;yng of awocan ferde into Cent to his eorldome. &amp; fordyde hit swy&d;e. &amp; &t;&ae;s cynges land. &amp; &t;&ae;s arcebiscopas mid ealle aweston. &amp; brohte eall &t;&ae;t god into his castele on Hrofeceastre. 
 &D;a &t;e cyng undergeat ealle &t;as &t;ing. &amp; hwilcne swicdom hi dydon toweard his. &t;a wear&d; he on his mode swi&d;e gedrefed. 
 Sende &t;a &ae;fter Englisce mannan. &amp; heom fores&ae;de his neode. &amp; gyrnde heora fultumes. 
 &amp; behet heom &t;a betsta laga &t;a &ae;fre &ae;r w&ae;s on &t;isan lande. &amp; &ae;lc unriht geold he forbead. &amp; geatte mannan heora wudas. and sl&ae;tinge. ac hit ne stod nane hwile. 
 Ac Englisce men swa &t;eah fengon to &t;am cynge heora hlaforde on fultume. 
 Ferdon &t;a toweard Hrofeceastre. &amp; woldon &t;one biscop Odan begytan. &t;ohtan gif hi h&ae;fdon hine &t;e w&ae;s &ae;rur heafod to &d;am unr&ae;de. &t;&ae;t hi mihton &t;e bet begytan ealla &t;a o&d;re. 
 Hi comon &t;a to &t;am castele to Tonebricge. &t;a w&ae;ron innan &t;am castele Oda biscopes cnihtas. &amp; o&d;re manige &t;e hine healdon woldan ongean &t;one cyng. 
 Ac &t;a Englisce men ferdon. &amp; tobr&ae;con &t;one castel. &amp; &t;a men &t;e &t;&ae;rinne w&ae;ron. gri&d;odon wi&d; &t;one cyng. 
 Se cyng mid his here ferde toweard Hrofeceastre. &amp; wendon &t;&ae;t se biscop w&ae;re &t;&ae;rinne. ac hit wear&d; &t;am cynge cu&d; &t;et se biscop w&ae;s afaren to &d;am castele a Pefenesea. 
 &amp; se cyng mid his here ferde &ae;fter. &amp; bes&ae;tt &t;one castel abutan. mid swi&d;e mycele here fulle six wucan. 
 Betwyx &t;issum se eorl of Normandige Rodbeard &t;es cynges bro&d;er gaderode swi&d;e mycel folc. &amp; &t;ohte to gewinnane Engleland mid &t;&ae;ra manna fultume &t;e w&ae;ron innan &t;isan lande ongean &t;one cyng. &amp; he sende of his mannan to &t;isum lande. &amp; wolde cuman himsylf &ae;fter. 
 Ac &t;a Englisce men &t;e w&ae;rdedon &t;&ae;re s&ae;. gel&ae;hton of &t;am mannon. &amp; slogon. &amp; adrengton ma &t;onne &ae;nig man wiste to tellanne. 
 Sy&d;&d;an heom ateorede mete wi&d;innan &t;am castele. &d;a gyrndon hi gri&d;as. &amp; agefan hine &t;am cynge. 
 &amp; se biscop swor &t;&ae;t he wolde ut of Englelande faran. &amp; na mare cuman on &d;isan lande butan se cyng him &ae;fter sende. &amp; &t;&ae;t he wolde agifan &t;one castel on Hrofeceastre. 
 Ealswa se biscop ferde &amp; sceolde agifan &t;one castel. &amp; se cyng sende his men mid him. 
 &D;a arisan &t;a men &t;e w&ae;ron innan &t;am castele. &amp; namon &t;one biscop &amp; &t;es cynges men. &amp; dydon hi on h&ae;ftnunge. 
 Innan &t;am castele w&ae;ron swi&d;e gode cnihtas. Eustatius &t;e iunga. &amp; Rogeres eorles &t;reo sunan. &amp; ealle &t;a betstboren men. &t;e w&ae;ron innan &t;isan lande. o&d;&d;e on Normandige. 
 &D;a se cyng undergeat &t;as &t;ing. &t;a ferde he &ae;fter mid &t;am here &t;e he &d;&ae;r h&ae;fde. &amp; sende ofer eall Englalande. &amp; bead &t;&ae;t &ae;lc man &t;e w&ae;re unni&d;ing sceolde cuman to him  Frencisce &amp; Englisce. of porte &amp; of uppelande. 
 Him com &t;a mycel folc to. &amp; he for to Hrofeceastre. &amp; bes&ae;tt &t;one castel. o&d;&d;et hi gri&d;edon &t;&ae; &t;&ae;r inne w&ae;ron. &amp; &t;one castel ageafon. 
 Se biscop Odo mid &t;am mannum &t;e innan &t;am castele w&ae;ron ofer s&ae; ferdon. &amp; se biscop swa forlet &t;one wur&d;scipe &t;e he on &t;is land h&ae;fde. 
 Se cyng sy&d;&d;an sende here to Dunholme. &amp; let besittan &t;one castel. &amp; se biscop gri&d;ode and ageaf &t;one castel. &amp; forlet his biscoprice. &amp; ferde to Normandige. 
 Eac manige Frencisce men forleton heora land. &amp; ferdon ofer s&ae;. &amp; se cyng geaf heora land &t;am mannum &t;e him holde w&ae;ron. 
 On &t;isum geare se arwur&d;a muneca feder &amp; frouer Landfranc arcebiscop gewat of &t;issum life. ac we hopia&d; &t;&ae;t he ferde to &t;&ae;t heofanlice rice. 
 Swilce eac gewar&d; ofer eall Engleland mycel eor&d;styrunge. on &t;one d&ae;g iii IDus Augustus. 
 &amp; w&ae;s swi&d;e l&ae;tsum gear on corne. &amp; on &ae;lces cynnes w&ae;stmum. swa &t;&ae;t manig men r&ae;pon heora corn onbutan Martines m&ae;ssan. &amp; gyt lator. 
 INDICTIONE XIII. 
 &D;issum &t;us gedon. eall swa w&ae; &ae;r abufan s&ae;dan be &t;am cynge. &amp; be his bro&d;er. &amp; be his mannon. Se cyng w&ae;s sm&ae;gende hu he mihte wrecon his bro&d;er Rodbeard swi&d;ost swencean. &amp; Normandige of him gewinnan. 
 &D;eah &t;urh his geapscipe. o&d;&d;e &t;urh g&ae;rsuma he begeat &t;one castel &ae;t sancte Waleri. &amp; &t;a h&ae;fenan. 
 &amp; swa he begeat &t;one &ae;t Albemare. &amp; &t;arinne he sette his cnihtas. &amp; hi dydon hearmes uppon &t;am lande on hergunge &amp; on b&ae;rnete. 
 &AE;fter &t;isum he begeat ma castelas innan &t;am lande. &amp; &t;&ae;r inne his rideras gelogode. 
 Se eorl of Normandige Rodbeard sy&d;&d;an he undergeat &t;&ae;t his gesworene men him trucedon. &amp; agefon hera castelas him to hearme. &t;a sende he to his hlaforde Philippe Francena cynge. &amp; he com to Normandige mid mycelan here. 
 &amp; se cyng &amp; se eorl mid orm&ae;tre fyrde bes&ae;ton &t;one castel abuton. &t;&ae;r &t;&ae;s cynges men of Engleland inne w&ae;ron. 
 Se cyng Willelm of Englalande sende to Philippe Francena cynge. &amp; he for his lufan o&d;&d;e for his mycele gersuma forlet swa his man &t;one eorl Rodbeard &amp; his land. &amp; ferde ongean to France &amp; let heom swa weor&d;an. 
 &amp; betwyx &t;isum &t;ingum &t;is land w&ae;s swi&d;e fordon. on unlagagelde. &amp; on o&d;re manige ungelimpe. 
 On &t;isum geare se cyng Willelm heold his hired to Cristes messan on W&ae;stmynstre. &amp; &t;&ae;r &ae;fter to Candelm&ae;ssan he ferde for his bro&d;&ae;r un&t;earfe ut of Englalande into Normandige. 
 Onmang &t;am &t;e he &t;&ae;r w&ae;s. heora sehte tog&ae;dere eode. on &t;&ae;t gerad &t;&ae;t se eorl him to handan let Uescam. &amp; &t;one eorldom &ae;t Ou. &amp; Ki&ae;resburh. And &t;&ae;rtoeacan &t;es cynges men sacleas beon moston. on &t;am castelan. &t;e hi &ae;r &t;es eorles un&t;ances begiten h&ae;fdon. 
 &amp; Se cyng him ongean &t;a Manige behet  &t;e &ae;r heora f&ae;der gewann. &amp; &t;a fram &t;am eorle gebogen w&ae;s  gebygle to donne. &amp; eall &t;&ae;t his f&ae;der &t;&ae;r begeondan h&ae;fde. butan &t;am &t;e he &t;am cynge &t;a geunnen h&ae;fde. 
 &amp; &t;&ae;t ealle &t;a &t;e on Englelande for &t;am eorle &ae;ror heora land forluron. hit on &t;isum sehte habban sceoldan. &amp; se eorl on Englelande eall swa mycel swa on heora forewarde w&ae;s. 
 And gif se eorl for&d;ferde butan sunu be rihtre &ae;we. w&ae;re se cyng yrfenuma of eallon Normandig. Be &t;isre sylfan forewarde gif se cyng swulte. w&ae;re se eorl yrfenuma ealles Englalandes. 
 &D;as forewarde gesworan xii &t;a betste of &t;es cynges healfe. and xii of &t;es eorles. &t;eah hit sy&d;&d;an litle hwile stode. 
 On mang &t;isum s&ae;hte wear&d; Eadgar &ae;&t;eling belandod. of &t;am &t;e se eorl him &ae;ror &t;&ae;r to handa gel&ae;ten h&ae;fde. &amp; ut of Normandig for to &t;am cynge his a&d;ume to Scotlande. &amp; to his swustor. 
 On mang &t;am &t;e se cyng Willelm ut of Englelande w&ae;s. ferde se cyng Melcolm of Scotlande hider into Englum. &amp; his mycelne d&ae;l oferhergode. o&d; &t;&ae;t &t;a gode m&ae;n &t;e &t;is land bewiston. him fyrde ongean s&ae;ndon. &amp; hine gecyrdon. 
 &D;a &t;a se cyng Willelm into Normandige &t;is gehyrde. &t;a gearcode he his fare. &amp; to Englelande com. &amp; his bro&d;er se eorl Rodbeard mid him. 
 &amp; sona fyrde het ut abeodan. &ae;g&d;er scipfyrde &amp; landfyrde. ac seo scipfyrde &ae;r he to Scotlande cuman mihte. &ae;lm&ae;st earmlice forfor. feowan dagon toforan sancte Mich&ae;les m&ae;ssan. 
 And se cyng &amp; his bro&d;er mid &t;&ae;re landfyrde ferdon. ac &t;a &d;a se cyng Melcolm gehyrde &t;&ae;t hine man mid fyrde secean wolde. he for mid his fyrde ut of Scotlande into Lo&d;ene on Englaland &amp; &t;&ae;r abad. 
 &D;a &t;a se cyng Willelm mid his fyrde genealehte. &t;a ferdon betwux Rodbeard eorl &amp; Eadgar &ae;&d;eling &amp; &t;&ae;ra cinga sehte swa gemacedon. &t;&ae;t se cyng Melcolm to uran cynge com. &amp; his man wear&d; to eallswilcre gehyrsumnisse swa he &ae;r his f&ae;der dyde. &amp; &t;&ae;t mid a&d;e gefestnode. 
 &amp; se cyng Willelm him behet on lande &amp; on ealle &t;inge &t;&ae;s &t;e he under his f&ae;der &ae;r h&ae;fde. 
 On &t;isum sehte wear&d; eac Eadgar e&t;eling wi&d; &t;one cyng ges&ae;htlad. &amp; &t;a cyngas &t;a mid mycclum sehte tohwurfon. ac &t;&ae;t litle hwile stod. 
 And se eorl Rodbeard her o&d; Cristes m&ae;sse forneah mid &t;am cynge wunode. &amp; litel so&d;es &t;&ae;r on mang. of heora forewarde onfand. &amp; twam dagon &ae;r &t;&ae;re tide on Wiht scipode. &amp; into Normandig for. &amp; Eadgar &ae;&d;eling mid him. 
 On &t;isum geare se cyng Willelm mid mycelre fyrde ferde nor&d; to Cardeol. &amp; &t;a burh ge&ae;&d;sta&t;elede. &amp; &t;one castel arerde. &amp; Dolfin utadraf &t;e &ae;ror &t;&ae;r &t;es landes weold. &amp; &t;one castel mid his mannan gesette. 
 &amp; sy&d;&d;an hider su&d; gew&ae;nde. &amp; mycele m&ae;nige Eyrlisces folces mid wifa &amp; mid orfe &t;yder s&ae;nde. &t;&ae;r to wunigenne &t;&ae;t land to tilianne. 
 On &t;isum geare to &t;am l&ae;ngtene war&d; se cyng Willelm on Gleaweceastre to &t;am swi&d;e geseclod. &t;&ae;t he w&ae;s ofer eall dead gekyd. 
 &amp; on his broke he Gode fela beh&ae;sa behet. his agen lif on riht to l&ae;dene. &amp; Godes cyrcean gri&d;ian &amp; fri&d;ian. &amp; n&ae;fre ma eft wi&d; feo gesyllan. &amp; ealle rihte lage on his &t;eode to habbene. 
 And &t;&ae;t arcebiscoprice on Cantwarbyrig &t;e &ae;r on his agenre hand stod. Anselme bet&ae;hte. se w&ae;s &ae;r abbod on B&ae;c. &amp; Rodbeard his cancelere &t;&ae;t biscoprice on Lincolne. 
 &amp; to manegan mynstren land geu&d;e. ac &t;&ae;t he sy&d;&d;an &ae;tbr&ae;d. &t;a him gebotad w&ae;s. &amp; ealle &t;a gode laga forl&ae;t. &t;e he us &ae;r behet. 
 &D;a &ae;fter &t;isson sende se cyng of Scotlande. &amp; &t;&ae;re forewarde gyrnde &t;e him behaten w&ae;s. 
 And se cing Willelm him steofnode to Gloweceastre. &amp; him to Scotlande gislas sende. &amp; Eadgar &ae;&t;eling &ae;fter. &amp; &t;a men sy&d;&d;an ongean. &t;e hine mid mycclon wur&d;scipe to &t;am cynge brohtan. 
 Ac &t;a &d;a he to &t;am cynge com ne mihte he beon weor&d;e na&d;er ne ure cynges sp&ae;ce. ne &t;&ae;ra forewarde &t;e him &ae;r behatene w&ae;ron. &amp; for&t;i hi &t;a mid mycelon unsehte tohwurfon. &amp; se cyng Melcolm ham to Scotlande gew&ae;nde. 
 Ac hra&d;e &t;&ae;s &t;e he ham com. he his fyrde gegaderode. &amp; into Englelande hergende mid maran unr&ae;de ferde &t;one him abehofode. &amp; hine &t;a Rodbeard se eorl of Nor&d;hymbran mid his mannan unw&ae;res besyrede &amp; ofsloh. 
 Hine sloh Mor&ae;l of B&ae;bbaburh. se w&ae;s &t;&ae;s eorles stiward. &amp; Melcolmes cynges godsib. 
 Mid him w&ae;s eac Eadward his sune ofslagen. se &ae;fter him cyng beon sceolde. gif he hit gelifode. 
 &D;a &t;a seo gode cwen Margarita &t;is gehyrde. hyre &t;a leofstan hlaford &amp; sunu &t;us beswikene. heo wear&d; o&d; dea&d; on mode geancsumed. &amp; mid hire prestan to cyrcean eode. &amp; hire gerihtan underfeng. &amp; &ae;t Gode ab&ae;d. &t;&ae;t heo hire gast ageaf. 
 &amp; &d;a Scottas &t;a Dufenal to cynge gecuron Melcolmes bro&d;er. &amp; ealle &t;a Englisce ut adr&ae;fdon. &t;e &ae;r mid &t;am cynge Melcolme w&ae;ron. 
 &D;a &t;a Dunecan Melcolmes cynges sunu &t;is eall gehyrde &t;us gefaren. se on &t;&ae;s cynges hyrede Willelmes w&ae;s. swa swa his f&ae;der hine ures cynges f&ae;der &ae;r to gisle geseald h&ae;fde. &amp; her swa sy&d;&d;an belaf. he to &t;am cynge com. 
 &amp; swilce getryw&d;a dyde. swa se cyng &ae;t him habban wolde. &amp; swa mid his unne to Scotlande for. mid &t;am fultume &t;e he begytan mihte Engliscra &amp; Frenciscra. and his m&ae;ge Dufenal &t;es rices benam. &amp; to cynge wear&d; underfangen. 
 Ac &t;a Scottas hi eft sume gegaderoden. &amp; forneah ealle his m&ae;nu ofslogan. &amp; he sylf mid feawum &ae;tb&ae;rst. 
 Sy&d;&d;an hi wurdon sehte. on &t;a gerad &t;&ae;t he n&ae;fre eft Englisce ne Frencisce into &t;am lande ne gelogige. 
 Her h&ae;fde se cyng Willelm to Cristes m&ae;ssan his hired &ae;t Gleaweceastre. &amp; him &t;ider fram his bro&d;er Rodbearde of Normandig bodan coman. 
 &T;a cyddon &t;&ae;t his bro&d;er gri&d; &amp; forewarde eall &ae;fter cw&ae;&d;. butan se cyng gel&ae;stan wolde eall &t;et hi on forewarde h&ae;fdon &ae;r gewroht. &amp; uppon &t;&ae;t hine forsworenne &amp; trywleasne clypode. buton he &t;a forewarda geheolde. o&d;&d;e &t;ider ferde &amp; hine &t;&ae;r betealde &t;&ae;r seo forewarde &ae;r w&ae;s gewroht &amp; eac gesworen. 
 &D;a ferde se cyng to H&ae;stingan to &t;am Candelm&ae;ssan. &amp; on mang &t;am &t;e he &t;&ae;r wederes abad. he let halgian &t;&ae;t mynster &ae;t &t;&ae;re Bataille. &amp; Herbearde Losange &t;am biscop of &t;eotfordan his st&ae;f benam. 
 &amp; &t;&ae;r &ae;fter to midlengtene ofer s&ae; for into Normandige. 
 Sy&d;&d;an he &t;ider com. he &amp; his bro&d;er Rodbeard se eorl gecw&ae;&d;an. &t;&ae;t hi mid gri&d;e tog&ae;dere cuman sceoldan. &amp; swa dydon. &amp; gesemede beon ne mihtan. 
 Sy&d;&d;an eft hi tog&ae;dere coman mid &t;am ilcan mannan &t;e &ae;r &t;&ae;t loc makedon. &amp; eac &t;a a&d;as sworen. &amp; ealne &t;one bryce uppon &t;one cyng tealdon. ac he nolde &t;&ae;s ge&t;afa beon. ne eac &t;a forewarde healdan. &amp; for&t;am hi &t;a mid mycelon unsehte tocyrdon. 
 And se cyng sy&d;&d;an &t;one castel &ae;t Bures gewann. &amp; &t;es eorles men &t;&ae;r inne genam. &t;a sume hyder to lande sende. 
 &D;&ae;r togeanes se eorl mid &t;es cynges fultume of France gewann &t;one castel &ae;t Argentses. &amp; &t;earinne Rogger Peiteuin genam. &amp; seofen hundred &t;es cynges cnihta mid him. &amp; sy&d;&d;an &t;one &ae;t Hulme. 
 &amp; Oft r&ae;dlice heora &ae;g&d;er uppon o&d;erne tunas b&ae;rnde. &amp; eac menne l&ae;hte. 
 &D;a sende se cyng hider to lande. &amp; het abeodan ut xx &t;usenda Engliscra manna him to fultume to Normandig. ac &t;a hi to s&ae; coman. &t;a het hi man cyrran. &amp; &t;&ae;t feoh syllan to &t;&ae;s cynges behofe &t;e hi genumen h&ae;fdon. &t;et w&ae;s &ae;lc man healf punda. &amp; hi swa dydon. 
 &amp; se eorl innon Normandig &ae;fter &t;ison mid &t;am cynge of France. &amp; mid eallon &t;an &t;e hi gegaderian mihton ferdon towardes Ou &t;&ae;r se cyng Willelm inne w&ae;s. &amp; &t;ohtan hine inne to besittanne. &amp; swa foran o&d; hi coman to Lungeuile. 
 &D;&ae;r wear&d; se cyng of France &t;urh gesmeah gecyrred. &amp; swa sy&d;&d;an eall seo fyrding tohwearf. 
 Her onmang &t;ison se cyng Willelm sende &ae;fter his bro&d;er Heanrige. se w&ae;s on &t;am castele &ae;t Damfront. ac for&t;i &t;e he mid fri&d;e &t;urh Normandig faran ne mihte. he him sende scipon &ae;fter. &amp; Hugo eorl of Ceastre. 
 Ac &t;a &d;a hi towardes Ou faran sceoldan &t;&ae;r se cyng w&ae;s. hi foran to Englelande. &amp; up coman &ae;t Hamtune on ealra halgena m&ae;sse&ae;fne. &amp; her sy&d;&d;on wunedon. &amp; to Cristes m&ae;ssan w&ae;ron on Lunden. 
 Eac on &t;isum ylcan geare &t;a Wylisce menn hi gegaderodon. &amp; wi&d; &t;a Frencisce &t;e on Walon. o&d;&d;e on &t;&ae;re neawiste w&ae;ron &amp; hi &ae;r belandedon. gewinn upahofon. &amp; manige festena &amp; castelas abr&ae;con. &amp; men ofslogon. 
 An sy&d;&d;an heora gefylce weox. hi hi on ma tod&ae;ldon. 
 Wi&d; sum &t;&ae;ra d&ae;le gefeaht Hugo eorl of Scrobscire &amp; hi aflymde. 
 Ac &t;eah hwe&d;er &t;a o&d;re. ealles &t;&ae;s geares nanes yfeles ne geswicon &t;e hi don mihton. 
 &D;ises geares eac &t;a Scottas heora cyng Dunecan besyredon &amp; ofslogan. &amp; heom sy&d;&d;an eft o&d;re sy&d;e his f&ae;deran Dufenal to cynge genamon. &t;urh &t;es lare &amp; to tihtinge he wear&d; to dea&d;e beswicen. 
 On &t;isum geare w&ae;s se cyng Willelm to Cristes m&ae;ssan &t;a feower forewarde dagas on Hwitsand. &amp; &ae;fter &t;am feor&d;an d&ae;ge hider to lande for. &amp; upp com &ae;t Doferan. 
 And Heanrig &t;es cynges bro&d;er her on lande o&d; lengten wunode. &amp; &t;a ofer s&ae; for to Normandig mid mycclon gersuman. on &t;&ae;s cynges heldan uppon heora bro&d;er Rodbeard eorl. 
 &amp; gelomlice uppon &t;one eorl wann. &amp; him mycelne hearm &ae;g&d;er on lande &amp; on mannan dyde. 
 And &t;a to Eastran heold se cyng his hired on Winceastre. &amp; se eorl Rodbeard of Nor&d;hymbran nolde to hirede cuman. 
 &amp; se cyng for&d;an wear&d; wi&d; hine swi&d;e astyrod. &amp; him to s&ae;nde &amp; heardlice bead gif he gri&d;es weor&d;e beon wolde. &t;&ae;t he to Pentecosten to hired come. 
 On &t;isum geare w&ae;ron Eastron on viii kalend&ae; Aprilis. 
 &amp; &t;a uppon Eastron on sancte Ambrosius m&ae;sse niht. &t;&ae;t is ii Non&ae; Aprilis w&ae;s gesewen forneah ofer eall &t;is land swilce forneah ealle &t;a niht swi&d;e m&ae;nifealdlice steorran of heofenan feollan. naht be anan o&d;&d;e twam. ac swa &t;iclice &t;&ae;t hit nan mann ateallan ne mihte. 
 Her &ae;fter to Pentecosten w&ae;s se cyng on Windlesoran. &amp; ealle his witan mid him. butan &t;am eorle of Nor&d;hymbran. for&t;am se cyng him na&t;er nolde ne gislas syllan. ne uppon tryw&d;an geunnon &t;&ae;t he mid gri&d;e cumon moste &amp; faran. 
 &amp; se cyng for&t;i his fyrde bead. &amp; uppon &t;one eorl to Nor&d;hymbran for. 
 &amp; sona &t;es &t;e he &t;ider com. he manege &amp; forneah ealle &t;a betste of &t;es eorles hirede innan anan f&ae;stene gewann. &amp; on h&ae;ftene gedyde. 
 &amp; &t;one castel &ae;t Tinemu&d;an bes&ae;t o&d;&d;et he hine gewann. &amp; &t;&ae;s eorles bro&d;er &t;&ae;rinne &amp; ealle &t;a &t;e him mid w&ae;ron. and sy&d;&d;an ferde to Bebbaburh. &amp; &t;one eorl &t;&ae;rinne bes&ae;t. 
 Ac &t;a &d;a se cyng geseah &t;&ae;t he hine gewinnan ne mihte. &t;a het he makian &ae;nne castel toforan Bebbaburh. &amp; hine on his sp&ae;ce Malueisin het. &t;&ae;t is on Englisc Yfel nehhebur. 
 &amp; hine swi&d;e mid his mannan ges&ae;tte. &amp; sy&d;&d;an su&d;weard for. 
 &D;a sona &ae;fter &t;am &t;e se cyng w&ae;s su&d; afaren. feorde se eorl anre nihte ut of Bebbaburh towardes Tinemu&d;an. 
 Ac &t;a &t;e innan &t;am niwan castele w&ae;ron. his gew&ae;r wurdon. &amp; him &ae;fter foran &amp; onfuhton. &amp; hine gewundedon. &amp; sy&d;&d;an gel&ae;hton. &amp; &t;a &t;e mid him w&ae;ron sume ofslogan. sume lifes gefengon. 
 Onmang &t;ison wear&d; &t;am cynge cu&d;. &t;&ae;t &t;a Wylisce men on Wealon sumne castel heafdon tobroken Muntgumni hatte. &amp; Hugon eorles menn ofslagene &t;e hine healdon sceoldan. 
 &amp; he for&t;i o&d;re fyrde het fearlice abannan. &amp; &ae;fter sancte Michaelesm&ae;sse into Wealan ferde. 
 &amp; his fyrde toscyfte. &amp; &t;&ae;t land eall &t;urhfor. swa &t;&ae;t seo fyrde eall tog&ae;dere com to ealra halgena to Snawdune. 
 Ac &t;a Wylisce a toforan into muntan and moran ferdan &t;&ae;t heom man to cuman ne mihte. &amp; se cyng &t;a hamweard gewende for&t;am he geseah &t;&ae;t he &t;&ae;r &t;es wintres mare don ne mihte. 
 &D;a &t;a se cyng ongean com. &t;a het he niman &t;one eorl Rotbeard of Nor&d;hymbran &amp; to B&ae;bbaburh l&ae;dan. &amp; &ae;g&d;er eage utadon. buton &t;a &t;e &t;&ae;r inne w&ae;ron &t;one castel agyfan woldan. 
 Hine heoldan his wif. &amp; Moreal se w&ae;s stiward &amp; eac his m&ae;g. 
 &D;urh &t;is wear&d; se castel &t;a agyfen. &amp; Moreal wear&d; &t;a on &t;es cynges hirede. &amp; &t;urh hine wurdon manege &ae;g&d;er ge gehadode &amp; eac l&ae;wede geypte. &t;e mid heora r&ae;de on &t;es cynges unheldan w&ae;ron. 
 &T;a se cyng sume &ae;r &t;&ae;re tide het on h&ae;ftne&d;e gebringan. &amp; sy&d;&d;an swi&d;e gemahlice ofer eall &t;is land beodan. &t;&ae;t ealle &t;a &t;e of &t;am cynge land heoldan. eall swa hi fri&d;es weor&d;e beon woldan. &t;&ae;t hi on hirede to tide w&ae;ron. 
 And &t;one eorl Rotbert het se cyng to Windlesoran l&ae;dan. &amp; &t;&ae;r innan &t;am castele healdan. 
 Eac on &t;is ylcan geare togeanes Eastron com &t;&ae;s Papan sande hider to lande. &t;&ae;t w&ae;s Waltear bisceop swi&d;e god lifes man of Albin &t;&ae;re ceastre. &amp; &t;am arcebiscope Ansealme uppon Pentecosten of &t;&ae;s Papan healfe Urbanus his pallium geaf. 
 &amp; he hine underfeng &ae;t his arcestole on Cantwarabyrig. and se biscop Waltear her on lande &t;&ae;s geares sy&d;&d;an lange wunode. &amp; man sy&d;&d;an &t;&ae;t Rom gesceot be him sende. swa man manegan gearan &ae;ror ne dyde. 
 &D;ises ylcan eac geares w&ae;ron swi&d;e untid gewidera. &amp; for&t;i geond eall &t;is land wurdon eor&d;w&ae;stmas eall to medemlice gewende. 
 On &t;ison geare heold se cyng Willelm his hired to Cristes m&ae;ssan on Windlesoran. 
 &amp; Willelm biscop of Dunholme &t;&ae;r for&d;ferde to geares d&ae;ge. 
 And on Octabris Epiphanis w&ae;s se cyng &amp; ealle his witan on Searbyrig. 
 &T;&ae;r beteah Gosfrei Bainard Willelm of Ou &t;es cynges m&ae;g &t;&ae;t he heafde gebeon on &t;es cynges swicdome. &amp; hit him on gefeaht. &amp; hine on orreste ofercom. 
 &amp; sy&d;&d;an he ofercumen w&ae;s. him het se cyng &t;a eagan utadon. &amp; sy&t;&d;an belisnian. 
 &amp; his stiward Willelm hatte. se w&ae;s his modrian sunu. het se cyng on rode ahon. 
 &D;&ae;r wear&d; eac Eoda eorl of Campaine &t;&ae;s cynges a&d;um &amp; manege o&d;re belende. &amp; sumne man to Lundene l&ae;dde. &amp; &t;&ae;r spilde. 
 &D;ises geares eac to &t;am Eastran wear&d; swi&d;e mycel styrung geond ealle &t;as &t;eode. &amp; fela o&d;ra &t;eodan &t;urh Urbanus se w&ae;s Papa gehaten &t;eah &t;e he &t;&ae;s setles na&t;ing n&ae;fde on Rome. 
 &amp; ferde unarimedlice folc mid wifan &amp; cildan to &t;i &t;&ae;t hi uppon h&ae;&d;ene &t;eodan winnan woldan. 
 &D;urh &t;as fare wear&d; se cyng &amp; his bro&d;or Rodbeard eorl sehte. swa &t;&ae;t se cyng ofer s&ae; for. &amp; eall Normandig &ae;t him mid feo alisde. swa swa hi &t;a sehte w&ae;ron. 
 And se eorl sy&d;&d;an ferde. &amp; mid him se eorl of Flandran. &amp; se of Bunan. &amp; eac manige o&d;re heafodmen. &amp; se eorl Rotbeard &amp; &t;a &t;e mid him ferdon &t;one winter on Puille wunedon. 
 Ac &t;es folces &t;e be Hungrie for. fela &t;usenda &t;&ae;r &amp; be w&ae;ge earmlice forforan. &amp; fela hreowlice &amp; hungerbitene ongean winterham tugon. 
 &D;is w&ae;s swi&d;e hefigtime gear geond eall Angelcyn. &ae;g&d;er ge &t;urh m&ae;nigfealde gylda. &amp; eac &t;urh swi&d;e hefigtymne hunger. &t;e &t;isne eard &t;&ae;s geares swi&d;e gedrehte. 
 Eac on &t;ison geare &t;a heafodmen &t;e &t;is land heoldan oft r&ae;dlice fyrde into Wealon sendon. &amp; m&ae;nig man mid &t;am swi&d;e gedrehtan. ac man &t;&ae;r ne gesp&ae;dde. butan manmyrringe. &amp; feohspillinge. 
 Her on &t;ison geare weas se cyng Willelm to Cristes m&ae;ssan on Normandig. &amp; &t;a togeanes Eastron hider to lande for. for&t;am he &t;ohte his hired on Winceastre to healdenne. 
 Ac he wear&d; &t;urh weder gelet. o&d;&d;et Eastre &ae;fen &t;&ae;t he up com &ae;rost &ae;t Arundel. &amp; for&t;i his hired &ae;t Windlesoran heold. 
 &amp; &t;&ae;r &ae;fter mid mycclum here into Wealon ferde. &amp; &t;&ae;t land swi&d;e mid his fyrde &t;urhfor. &t;urh sume &t;a Wyliscean &t;e him to w&ae;ron cumen &amp; his l&ae;dteowas w&ae;ron. 
 &amp; &t;&ae;rinne wunode fram middesumeran forneah o&d; August. &amp; mycel &t;&ae;rinne forleas on mannan &amp; on horsan. &amp; eac on manegan o&d;ran &t;ingan. 
 &D;a Wylisce men sy&d;&d;on hi fram &t;am cynge gebugon. heom manege ealdras of heom sylfan gecuron. sum &t;&ae;ra w&ae;s Caduugaun gehaten &t;e heora weor&d;ast w&ae;s. se w&ae;s Griffines bro&d;er sunu cynges. 
 Ac &t;a &d;a se cyng geseah &t;&ae;t he nan &t;ingc his willes &t;&ae;r gefor&d;ian ne mihte. he ongean into &t;ison lande for. &amp; hra&d;e &ae;fter &t;am. he be &t;am gem&ae;ron castelas let gemakian. 
 &D;a uppon sancte Michaeles m&ae;ssan iiii Non&ae; Octobris &ae;tywde an selcu&d; steorra on &ae;fen scynende &amp; sona to setle gangende. 
 He w&ae;s gesewen su&d;weast. &amp; se leoma &t;e him ofstod. w&ae;s swi&d;e lang ge&t;uht su&d;east scinende. &amp; forneah ealle &t;a wucan on &t;as wisan &ae;tywde. 
 Manige men leton &t;&ae;t hit cometa w&ae;re. 
 Sona &ae;fter &t;yson. se arcebiscop Ansealm of Cantwarbyrig. leafe &ae;t &t;am cynge nam. &t;eah hit &t;am cynge unge will w&ae;re &t;&ae;s &t;e men leton. &amp; ofer s&ae; for. for&t;am him &t;uhte &t;&ae;t man on &t;isne &t;eodan lytel &ae;fter rihte &amp; &ae;fter his dyhte dyde. 
 And se cyng &t;&ae;r &ae;fter uppon sancte Martines m&ae;ssan ofer s&ae; into Normandig for. ac &t;a hwile &t;e he wederes abad. his hired innon &t;am sciran &t;&ae;r hi lagon. &t;one m&ae;ston hearm dydon &t;e &ae;fre hired o&d;&d;e here innon fri&d;lande don sceolde. 
 &D;is w&ae;s on eallon &t;ingan swi&d;e hefigtyme gear. &amp; ofer geswincfull. on ungewederan &t;a man o&d;&d;e tilian sceolde. o&d;&d;e eft til&d;a gegaderian. &amp; on ungyldan &t;a n&ae;fre ne ablunnon. 
 Eac manege sciran &t;e mid weorce to Lundenne belumpon. wurdon &t;&ae;rle gedrehte. &t;urh &t;one weall &t;e hi worhton onbutan &t;one tur. &amp; &t;urh &t;a brycge &t;e forneah eall toflotan w&ae;s. &amp; &t;urh &t;&ae;s cynges healle geweorc &t;e man on Westmynstre worhte. &amp; m&ae;nige man &t;&ae;r mid gedrehte. 
 Eac on &t;ysum ylcan geare sona uppon sancte Michaeles m&ae;ssan ferde Eadgar &ae;&t;eling mid fyrde &t;urh &t;&ae;s cynges fultum into Scotlande. &amp; &t;et land mid stranglicum feohte gewann. 
 &amp; &t;one cyng Dufenal ut adr&ae;fde. &amp; his m&ae;g Eadgar se w&ae;s Melcolmes sunu cynges &amp; Margarite &t;&ae;re cwenan he &t;&ae;r on &t;&ae;s cynges Willelmes heldan to cynge gesette. &amp; sy&d;&d;an ongean into Engleland for. 
 On &t;ysum geare to Cristes m&ae;ssan w&ae;s se cyng Willelm on Normandig. 
 &amp; Walcelin biscop on Winceastre. &amp; Baldewine abbod on sancte &AE;dmund innan &t;&ae;re tide b&ae;gen for&d;ferdan. 
 &amp; On &t;isum geare eac Turold abbod of Burh for&d;ferde. 
 &D;ises geares eac to &t;an sumeran innan Barrucscire &ae;t Finchamst&ae;de an mere blod weoll. swa swa manige trywe men s&ae;dan &t;e hit geseon sceoldan. 
 &amp; Hugo eorl wear&d; ofslagen innan Anglesege fram utwikingan. &amp; his bro&d;er Rodbert wear&d; his yrfenuma. swa swa he hit &ae;t &t;am cynge ofeode. 
 Toforan sancte Michaeles m&ae;ssan &ae;tywde seo heofon swilce heo forneah ealle &t;a niht byrnende w&ae;re. 
 &D;is w&ae;s swi&d;e geswincfull gear &t;urh manigfealde ungyld. &amp; &t;urh mycele renas &t;e ealles geares ne ablunnon. forneah &ae;lc til&d; on mersclande forferde. 
 Her w&ae;s se cyng Willelm to midewintra on Normandig. &amp; to Eastron hider to lande com. &amp; to Pentecosten forman si&d;e his hired innan his niwan gebyttlan &ae;t Westmynstre heold. 
 &amp; &t;&ae;r Rannulfe his capellane &t;&ae;t biscoprice on Dunholme geaf. &t;e &ae;ror ealle his gemot ofer eall Engleland draf. &amp; bewiste. 
 &amp; sona &t;&ae;r &ae;fter ofer s&ae; for. &amp; &t;one eorl Elias of &t;&ae;re Manige adraf. &amp; hy sy&d;&d;an on his geweald ges&ae;tte. &amp; swa to sancte Michaeles m&ae;ssan eft hider to lande com. 
 &D;ises geares eac on sancte Martines m&ae;ssed&ae;g. asprang up to &t;an swi&d;e s&ae;flod. &amp; swa mycel to hearme gedyde. swa nan man ne gemunet &t;&ae;t hi &ae;fre &ae;ror dyde. 
 &amp; w&ae;s &d;&ae;s ylcan d&ae;ges luna prima. 
 And Osmund biscop of Searbyrig innon Aduent for&d;ferde. 
 On &t;ison geare se cyng Willelm heold his hired to Cristes m&ae;ssa on Gleaweceastre. &amp; to Eastron on Winceastre. &amp; to Pentecosten on Westmynstre. 
 &amp; to &t;am Pentecosten w&ae;s gesewen innan Barrucscire &ae;t anan tune blod weallan of eor&t;an. swa swa m&ae;nige s&ae;dan &t;e hit geseon sceoldan. 
 And &t;&ae;r &ae;fter on morgen &ae;fter hlamm&ae;ssed&ae;ge wear&d; se cyng Willelm on huntno&d;e fram his anan men mid anre fla ofsceoten. &amp; sy&d;&d;an to Winceastre gebroht. &amp; on &t;am biscoprice bebyrged. &t;&ae;t w&ae;s &t;&ae;s &t;reotte&d;an geares &t;e he rice onfeng. 
 He w&ae;s swi&d;e strang &amp; re&d;e ofer his land &amp; his m&ae;nn. &amp; wi&d; ealle his neahheburas. &amp; swi&d;e ondr&ae;dendlic. 
 &amp; &t;urh yfelra manna r&ae;das &t;e him &ae;fre gecweme w&ae;ran. &amp; &t;urh his agene gitsunga. he &ae;fre &t;as leode mid here &amp; mid ungylde tyrwigende w&ae;s. 
 For&t;an &t;e on his dagan &ae;lc riht afeoll. &amp; &ae;lc unriht for Gode &amp; for worulde up aras. 
 Godes cyrcean he ny&d;erade. &amp; &t;a biscoprices &amp; abbotrices &t;e &t;a ealdras on his dagan feollan. 
 Ealle he hi o&d;&d;e wi&d; feo gesealde. o&d;&d;e on his agenre hand heold. &amp; to gafle gesette. for&t;an &t;e he &ae;lces mannes gehadodes &amp; l&ae;wedes yrfenuma beon wolde. 
 &amp; swa &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;s d&ae;ges &t;e he gefeoll. he heafde on his agenre hand &t;&ae;t arcebiscoprice on Cantwarbyrig. &amp; &t;&ae;t bisceoprice on Winceastre. &amp; &t;&ae;t on Searbyrig. &amp; xi abbodrices. ealle to gafle gesette. 
 And &t;eah &t;e ic hit l&ae;ng ylde. eall &t;et &t;e Gode w&ae;s la&d; &amp; rihtfullan mannan. eall &t;&ae;t w&ae;s gewunelic on &t;isan lande on his tyman. &amp; for&t;i he w&ae;s forneah ealre his leode la&d;. &amp; Gode ands&ae;te. 
 Swa swa his &ae;nde &ae;tywde. for&t;an &t;e he on middewardan his unrihte buten behreowsunge &amp; &ae;lcere d&ae;dbote gewat. 
 On &t;&ae;ne &t;unresd&ae;g he w&ae;s ofslagen. &amp; &t;&ae;s on morgen bebyrged. 
 &amp; sy&d;&t;an he bebyrged w&ae;s. &t;a witan &t;e &t;a neh handa w&ae;ron. his bro&d;er Heanrig to cynge gecuran. 
 &amp; he &t;&ae;rrihte &t;&ae;t biscoprice on Winceastre Willelme Giffarde geaf. &amp; si&t;&t;an to Lundene for. 
 &amp; on &t;an Sunnand&ae;ge &t;&ae;r &ae;fter toforan &t;am weofode on Westmynstre Gode &amp; eallan folce behet ealle &t;a unriht to aleggenne &t;e on his bro&d;er timan w&ae;ran. &amp; &t;a betstan lage to healdene &t;e on &ae;niges cynges d&ae;ge toforan him stodan. 
 And hine sy&d;&d;an &ae;fter &t;am se biscop of Lundene Mauricius to cynge gehalgode. &amp; him ealle on &t;eosan lande to abugan. &amp; a&d;as sworan. &amp; his men wurdon. 
 And se cyng sona &ae;fter &t;am be &t;&ae;re r&ae;de &t;e him abutan w&ae;ran. &t;one biscop Rannulf of Dunholme let niman. &amp; into &t;am ture on Lundene let gebringon. &amp; &t;&ae;r healdan. 
 &D;a toforan Sancte Michaeles m&ae;ssan com se arcebiscop Ansealm of Cantwarbyrig hider to lande. swa swa se cyng Heanrig be his witena r&ae;de him &ae;fter sende. for&t;an &t;e he w&ae;s ut of &t;is lande gefaren. for &t;an mycelan unrihte &t;e se cyng Willelm him dyde. 
 And si&d;&t;an sona her&ae;fter se cyng genam Mahalde him to wife Malcolmes cynges dohter of Scotlande. &amp; Margareta &t;&ae;re goda cw&ae;ne Eadwardes cynges magan. &amp; of &t;an rihtan &AE;ngla landes kynekynne. 
 &amp; on sancte Martines m&ae;ssed&ae;g heo wear&d; him mid mycelan weor&d;scipe forgifen on Westmynstre. &amp; se arcebiscop Ansealm hi him bew&ae;ddade. &amp; si&d;&d;an to cwene gehalgode. 
 And se arcebiscop Thomas of Eoferwic her &ae;fter sona for&d;ferde. 
 &D;eoses ylces geares eac innan h&ae;rfest com se eorl Rotbert ham into Normandi. &amp; se eorl Rotbert of Flandran. &amp; Eustatius eorl of Bunan fram Ierusalem. 
 &amp; sona swa se eorl Rotbert into Normandig com. he wear&d; fram eallan &t;am folce bli&t;elice underfangen. butan &t;am castelan &d;e w&ae;ron ges&ae;tte mid &t;&ae;s cynges Heanriges manna. togeanes &t;an he manega gewealc &amp; gewinn h&ae;fde. 
 Her on &t;isum geare to Cristes m&ae;ssan heold se cyng Heanrig his hired on Westmynstre. &amp; to Eastran on Winceastre. 
 &amp; &t;a sona &t;&ae;r&ae;fter wurdon &t;a heafodmen her on lande wi&d;err&ae;den togeanes &t;am cynge. &ae;g&d;er ge for heoran agenan mycelan ungetryw&d;an. &amp; eac &t;urh &t;one eorl Rodbert of Normandig. &t;e mid unfri&d;e hider to lande fundode. 
 And se cyng sy&d;&d;an scipa ut on s&ae; sende his bro&d;er to d&ae;re &amp; to l&ae;ttinge. ac hi sume &ae;ft &ae;t &t;&ae;re neode abru&d;on. &amp; fram &t;am cynge gecyrdon. &amp; to &t;am eorle Rotberte gebugan. 
 &D;a to midde sumeran ferde se cyng ut to Pefenes&ae; mid eall his fyrde togeanes his bro&d;er &amp; his &t;&ae;r abad. ac onmanig &t;ison com se eorl Rotbert up &ae;t Portesmu&d;an xii nihtan toforan Hlafm&ae;ssan. 
 &amp; se cyng mid ealre his fyrde him togeanes com. ac &t;a heafod men heom betwenan foran. 
 &amp; &t;a bro&d;ra gesehtodan on &t;a gerad. &t;et se cyng forlet eall &t;&ae;t he mid streang&d;e innan Normandig togeanes &t;am eorle heold. &amp; &t;&ae;t ealle &t;a on Englelande heora land ongean heafdon. &t;e hit &ae;r &t;urh &t;one eorl forluron. &amp; Eustaties eorl eac eall his f&ae;der land her on lande. 
 &amp; &t;et se eorl Rotbert &ae;lce geare sceolde of Englalande &t;reo &t;usend marc seolfres habban. &amp; loc hwe&d;er &t;&ae;ra gebro&d;ra o&d;erne oferbide. w&ae;re yrfeweard ealles Englalandes &amp; eac Normandiges. buton se for&d;farena yrfenuman heafde be rihtre &ae;we. 
 &amp; &t;is &t;a mid a&d;e gefestnodan xii &t;a hihste of &ae;g&d;re healfe. 
 And se eorl sy&d;&d;an o&d; &d;et ofer sancte Michaeles m&ae;sse her on lande wunode. &amp; his men mycel to hearme &ae;fre gedydon swa hi geferdon. &t;a hwile &t;e se eorl her on lande wunode. 
 &D;ises geares eac se biscop Rannulf to &t;am Candelm&ae;ssan ut of &t;am ture on Lunden nihtes o&d;b&ae;rst &t;&ae;r he on h&ae;ftne&d;e w&ae;s. &amp; to Normandige for. &t;urh &t;es macunge m&ae;st &amp; to spryttinge se eorl Rotbert &t;ises geares &t;is land mid unfri&d;e gesohte. 
 On &t;isum geare to Natiuite&d; w&ae;s se cyng Heanrig on Westmynstre. &amp; to Eastron on Winceastre. 
 &amp; sona &t;&ae;r &ae;fter wurdon unsehte se cyng &amp; se eorl Rotbert of B&ae;l&ae;sme se h&ae;fde &t;one eorldom her on lande on Scrobbesbyrig &t;e his f&ae;der Roger eorl &ae;r ahte. &amp; micel rice &t;&ae;rto. &ae;g&d;er ge beheonon s&ae; ge begeondon. 
 &amp; se cyng ferde &amp; bes&ae;t &t;one castel &ae;t Arundel. ac &t;a he hine swa hra&d;e gewinnan ne mihte. he let &t;&ae;r toforan castelas gemakian. &amp; hi mid his mannan gesette. 
 &amp; sy&d;&d;an mid ealre his fyrde ferde to Brigge. &amp; &t;&ae;r wunode o&d;&d;et he &t;one castel h&ae;fde. &amp; &t;one eorl Rotbert bel&ae;nde. &amp; ealles ben&ae;mde. &t;es he on Englalande h&ae;fde. 
 &amp; se eorl swa ofer s&ae; gewat. &amp; se fyrde sy&d;&d;an ham cyrde. 
 &D;a &t;&ae;r &ae;fter to sancte Michaeles m&ae;ssan w&ae;s se cyng &ae;t W&ae;stmynstre. &amp; ealle &t;a h&ae;fodmen on &t;is lande gehadode &amp; l&ae;wede. 
 &amp; se arcebiscop Ansealm heold gehadodra manna sino&d;. &amp; hi &t;&ae;r manega beboda setton &t;e to Cristendome belimpa&d;. 
 &amp; &ae;g&d;er manige Frencisce &amp; Englisce &t;&ae;r heora stafas &amp; rice forluron. &t;e hi mid unrihte begeaton. o&d;&d;e mid woge &t;&ae;r on lifedon. 
 &amp; On &d;isum ylcan geare on Pentecosten m&ae;ssan wuce. &t;a coman &t;eofas sum of Aluearnie. sum of France. &amp; sum of Flandres. &amp; breokan &t;a mynstre of Burh &amp; &t;&ae;rinne naman mycel to gode on golde &amp; on seolfre. &t;et w&ae;ron roden &amp; calicen &amp; candelsticcan. 
 Her on &t;isum geare to midewintra w&ae;s se cyng Heanrig &ae;t Westmynstre. 
 &amp; &t;&ae;r &ae;fter sona ferde se biscop Willelm Giffard ut of &t;is land. for&t;an &t;e he ongean riht nolde his hades onfon &ae;t &t;am arcebiscop Girarde of Eoferwic. 
 &amp; &t;a to &t;an Eastran heold se cyng his hired on Winceastre. 
 &amp; &t;&ae;r &ae;fter ferde se arcebiscop Ansealm of Cantwarbyrig to Rome. swa swa him &amp; &t;am cynge gewear&d;. 
 &D;ises geares eac com se eorl Rotbert of Normandig to sprecene wi&d; &t;one cyng her on lande. 
 &amp; &ae;r he heonne ferde he forgeaf &t;a &t;reo &t;usend marc &t;e him seo cyng Heanrig be foreweard &ae;lce geare gifan sceolde. 
 On &t;isum geare eac &ae;t Heamstede innan Barrucscire. w&ae;s gesewen blod of eor&d;an. 
 &D;is w&ae;s swi&d;e gedeorfsum gear her on lande. &t;urh m&ae;nifealde gyld.&amp; &t;urh orfcwealm. &amp; w&ae;stma forweor&t;enesse &ae;g&d;er ge on corne. &amp; eac on eallon treoww&ae;stman. 
 Eac on morgen uppon sancte Laurenties m&ae;ssed&ae;g gedyde se wind swa mycel to hearme her on lande on eallon w&ae;stman. swa nan man ne gemunde &t;&ae;t &ae;fre &ae;nig &ae;r gedyde. 
 On &d;isum ylcan geare Mathias abbod of Burh for&d;ferde. se ne lyfode na leng &t;an an geare. sy&d;&d;an he abbod w&ae;s. 
 &AE;fter sancte Michaeles m&ae;ssan on xii kalend&ae; Novembris he w&ae;s mid procession underfangan to abbod. &amp; on &d;am ylcan d&ae;ge &t;es o&d;res geares he wear&d; dead on Gleawceastre. &amp; &t;&ae;r bebyrged. 
 Her on &t;isum geare to Cristes m&ae;ssan heold se cyng Heanrig his hired &ae;t W&ae;stminstre. &amp; to Eastron on Winceastre. &amp; to Pentecosten eft on Westmynstre. 
 &D;ises geares w&ae;s se forma Pentecostes d&ae;g on Non&ae; Iunii. 
 &amp; on &t;am Tiw&ae;sd&ae;ge &t;&ae;r&ae;fter &ae;tywdan feower circulas to &t;am mid d&ae;ge onbutan &t;&ae;re sunnan hwites hiwes. &ae;lc under o&d;ran gebroiden. swylce hi gemette w&ae;ron. 
 Ealle &t;e hit gesawon wundredon. for&t;an hi n&ae;fre &ae;r swilce ne gemundon. 
 Her&ae;fter wurdon sehte se eorl Rotbert of Normandig. &amp; Rotbert de B&ae;lesme &t;e se cyng Heanri &ae;ror bel&ae;nd h&ae;fde &amp; of Englalande adrifen. 
 &amp; &t;urh heora sehte wurdon wi&d;err&ae;de se cyng of Englalande &amp; se eorl of Normandig. 
 &amp; se cyng his folc ofer s&ae; into Normandig sende. &amp; &t;a heafodmen &t;&ae;r on lande hi underfengon. 
 &amp; on heora hlafordes &t;&ae;s eorles swicdome into heora castelan gelogodan. &t;anon hi manige gedrecednissa on hergunga &amp; on b&ae;rninge &t;am eorle gedydon. 
 Eac &t;ises geares Willelm eorl of Moretoin heonon of lande into Normandig for. 
 Ac sy&d;&d;an he afaren wes. he wi&d; &t;one cyng geworhte. for hwan hine se cyng ealles ben&ae;mde. &amp; bel&ae;nde &t;&ae;s &t;e he her on lande h&ae;fde. 
 Nis ea&d;e to asecgenne &t;ises landes earm&d;a &t;e hit to &t;ysan timan dreogende w&ae;s. &t;urh mistlice &amp; m&ae;nigfealdlice unriht &amp; gyld. &t;&ae; n&ae;fre ne geswican ne ne ateorodon. 
 &amp; &ae;fre ealswa se cyng for. full hergung &t;urh his hired uppon his wreccea folc w&ae;s. &amp; &t;&ae;r onmang foroft b&ae;rneta. &amp; manslihtas. 
 Eall &t;is w&ae;s God mid to gremienne. &amp; &t;as arme leode mid to tregienne. 
 On &t;isum geare to Natiuite&d; heold se cyng Heanrig his hired &ae;t Windlesoran. 
 &amp; &t;&ae;r&ae;fter to &t;am lengtene he for ofer s&ae; into Normandig uppon his bro&d;er Rotbert eorl. 
 &amp; onmang &t;am &t;e he &t;&ae;r wunode he gewann of his bro&d;er Ca&t;um &amp; Baius. &amp; m&ae;st ealle &t;a castelas &amp; &t;a heafodmen &t;&ae;r on lande him wurdon under&t;eodde. &amp; se sy&d;&d;an to herfest eft ongean hider to lande com. 
 &amp; &t;&ae;t he on Normandig gewunnen h&ae;fde. sy&d;&d;an on sibbe &amp; him gebygle wunode. butan &t;a &t;e &t;am eorle Willelme of Mortoin ahw&ae;r neah wunedon. &t;a he gelomlice gesw&ae;ncte swa he swi&d;ost mihte. for his landlyre her on lande. 
 And &t;a toforan Cristes m&ae;ssan com Rotbert de B&ae;lesme hider to lande to &t;am cynge. 
 &D;is w&ae;s swi&d;e gedyrfsum gear her on lande &t;urh w&ae;stma forwordenessa. &amp; &t;urh &t;a m&ae;nigfealde gyld &t;e n&ae;fre ne geswican &ae;r se cyng oferfore. &amp; &t;a hwile &t;e he &t;&ae;r w&ae;s. &amp; eft sy&d;&d;an he ongean com. 
 Her on &t;ison geare w&ae;s se cyng Henrig to Natiuite&d; on Westmynstre. &amp; &t;&ae;r his hired heold. 
 &amp; uppon &t;&ae;re tide Rotbert de B&ae;lesme mid unsehte fram &t;am cynge ut of &t;ison lande into Normandige for. 
 &D;a her &ae;fter onforan l&ae;ngtene w&ae;s se cyng &ae;t Nor&d;hamtune. &amp; se eorl Rotbert his bro&d;er of Normandig &t;yder to him com. 
 &amp; for&t;am se cyng him nolde agifan &t;&ae;t &t;e he on Normandige uppon him genumen h&ae;fde. hi mid unsehte tohwurfon. &amp; se eorl ferde ofer s&e; sona eft ongean. 
 On &t;&ae;re forman l&ae;ngtenwucan on &t;one Friged&ae;g i xiiii kalend&ae; Marcii on &ae;fen &ae;tywde an ungewunelic steorra. &amp; lange stunde &t;&ae;r&ae;fter w&ae;s &ae;lce &ae;fen gesewen hwile scinende. 
 Se steorra &ae;tywde innon &t;&ae;t su&d;west. he w&ae;s litel ge&t;uht. and deorc. ac se leoma &t;e him fram stod w&ae;s swi&d;e beorht. &amp; swilce orm&ae;te beam ge&t;uht nor&d;east scinende. 
 &amp; sumne &ae;fen w&ae;s ges&ae;wen swilce se beam ongeanweardes wi&d; &t;es steorran ward fyrcliende w&ae;re. 
 Gehwylce s&ae;don &t;&ae;t hig ma on &t;ison timon uncu&d;ra steorra gesawon. ac we hit openlicor ne awriton. for&t;am &t;e we hit sylfe ne sawon. 
 On &t;a niht &t;e on morgen w&ae;s Cena Domini. &t;&ae;t is se &t;unresd&ae;g toforan Eastran. w&ae;ron gesewen twegen monan on &t;&ae;re heofonan toforan &t;am d&ae;ge o&d;er beeastan. &amp; se o&d;er be westan begen fulle. &amp; &t;&ae;s ylcan d&ae;ges w&ae;s se mona xiiii. 
 To Eastran w&ae;s se cyng &ae;t Ba&d;an. &amp; to Pentecosten &ae;t Searbyrig. for&t;am &t;e he nolde on his fundunge ofer s&ae; hired healdan. 
 &D;&ae;r&ae;fter toforan August ferde se cyng ofer s&ae; into Normandig. &amp; ealle m&ae;st &t;e &t;&ae;r on lande w&ae;ron him on his willan to gebugon. wi&d;uton Rotbert de B&ae;lesme. &amp; &t;am eorle of Moretoin. &amp; feawa o&d;re of &t;am heafodmannan &t;e mid &t;am eorle of Normandige &t;e gyt heoldan. 
 &amp; for&t;an se cyng sy&d;&d;an mid fyrde for. &amp; bes&ae;t &t;&ae;s eorles &ae;nne castel of Moretoin Tenercebrai hatte. 
 Onmang &t;am &t;e se cyng &t;one castel bes&ae;t. com se eorl Rotbert of Normandig on sancte Michaeles m&ae;sse&ae;fen uppon &t;one cyng mid his fyrde. &amp; mid him Rotbert de B&ae;lesme. &amp; Willelm eorl of Moretoin. &amp; ealle &t;a &t;e mid heom woldan. 
 Ac seo streong&d;e &amp; se sige wear&d; &t;&ae;s cynges. 
 &D;&ae;r wear&d; se eorl of Normandig gefangen. &amp; se eorl of Moretoin. &amp; Rotbert de Stutteuile. &amp; to Englalande sy&d;&d;an gesende. &amp; on h&ae;ftne&d;e gebrohte. 
 Rotbert de B&ae;lesme &t;&ae;r wear&d; aflymed. &amp; Willelm Crispin gel&ae;ht. &amp; manige for&d; mid. 
 Eadgar &ae;&t;eling &t;e litle &ae;r fram &t;am cynge to &t;am eorle w&ae;s gefaren &t;&ae;r w&ae;s eac gefangen. &t;one let se cyng sy&d;&d;an sacleas faran. 
 Sy&d;&d;an geeode se cyng eall &t;&ae;t on Normandige w&ae;s. &amp; hit on his willan &amp; geweald gesette. 
 &D;ises geares eac w&ae;ron swi&d;e hefige &amp; sinlice gewinn betwux &t;am Casere of Sexlande &amp; his sunu. &amp; onmang &t;am gewinnan se f&ae;der for&d;ferde. &amp; se sunu feng to &t;am rice. 
 On &t;isum geare to Cristes m&ae;ssan w&ae;s se cyng Henri on Normandig. &amp; &t;&ae;t land on his geweald dihte. &amp; sette. 
 &amp; &t;&ae;r&ae;fter to l&ae;ngtene hider to lande com. &amp; to Eastran his hired on Windlesoran heold. &amp; to Pentecosten on Westminstre. 
 &amp; sy&d;&d;an eft to Augustes anginne on Westmynstre w&ae;s. &amp; &t;&ae;r &t;a biscopricen &amp; abbodricen geaf. &amp; sette. &t;e on Englelande o&d;&d;e on Normandige buton ealdre &amp; hyrde w&ae;ron. 
 &D;era w&ae;ron swa fela swa nan man n&ae;s &t;e gemvnde &t;&ae;t &ae;fre &ae;r swa fela tog&ae;dere gyfene w&ae;ron. 
 &amp; &ae;t &t;es ylcan sy&d;e. onmang &t;a o&d;&d;re &t;e abbodrices underfengon. Ernulf &t;e &ae;r w&ae;s prior on Cantwarbyrig feng to &t;am abbodrice on Burh. 
 &D;is w&ae;s rihtlice ymbe vii gear &t;&ae;s &t;e se cyng Henri cynedomes onfeng. &amp; w&ae;s &t;&ae;t an and fowertige&d;e gear &t;&ae;s &t;e Francan &t;yses landes weoldan. 
 Manege s&ae;don &t;et hi on &t;am monan &t;yses geares mistlice tacna gesawon. &amp; ongean cynde his leoman wexende &amp; waniende. 
 &D;ises geares for&d;ferdon. Mauricius biscop on Lunden. &amp; Rotbert abbod on sancte Eadmundes byrig. &amp; Ricard abbod on Elig. 
 &D;ises geares eac for&d;ferde se cyng Eadgar on Scotlande IDus Ianuarii. &amp; feng Alexander his bro&d;er to &t;am rice swa se cyng Henri him geu&d;e. 
 Her on &t;isum geare wes se cyng Henri to Natiuite&d; on Westmynstre. &amp; to Eastron on Winceastre. &amp; to Pentecosten eft on Westmynstre. &amp; &t;&ae;r&ae;fter toforan Augusti he ferde into Normandig. 
 &amp; se cyng of France Philippus for&d;ferde Non&ae; Augusti. &amp; feng his sunu Lo&d;ewis to &t;am rice. 
 &amp; wurdon sy&d;&d;on manege gewinn betwux &t;am cynge of France &amp; &t;am of Englelande. &t;a hwile &t;e he on Normandig wunode. 
 On &t;isum geare eac for&d;ferde se arcebiscop Girard of Eoferwic toforan Pentecosten. &amp; wear&d; sy&d;&d;an Thomas &t;&ae;rto gesett. 
 Her on &t;ison geare w&ae;s se cyng Henri to Cristes m&ae;ssan &amp; to Eastron on Normandig. &amp; toforan Pentecosten hider to lande com. &amp; his hired on Westmynstre heold. 
 &D;&ae;r wurdon &t;a forewearda fullworhte. &amp; &t;a a&d;as gesworene his dohter &t;am Casere to gifene. 
 &D;ises geares gewurdon swi&d;e fela &t;unra. &amp; &t;a swi&d;e &ae;geslice. 
 And se arcebiscop Ansealm of Cantwarabyrig for&d;ferde on &t;am d&ae;ge xi kalend&ae; Aprilis. &amp; w&ae;s se forma Easterd&ae;g on Letania maior. 
 On &t;isum geare heold se cyng Henri his hired to Cristesm&ae;ssan &ae;t Westmynstre. &amp; to Eastron he w&ae;s &ae;t M&ae;rlebeorge. &amp; to Pentecosten forman si&t;e his hired on &t;am niwan Windlesoran heold. 
 &D;ises geares sende se cyng toforan l&ae;ngtene his dohter mid m&ae;nigfealdan madman ofer s&ae;. &amp; hi &t;am Casere forgeaf. 
 On &t;&ae;re fiftan nihte on Maies mon&d;e. &ae;tywde se mona on &ae;fen beorhte scinende. &amp; sy&d;&d;an litlan &amp; litlan his leoht wanode. swa &t;&ae;t he sona nihtes to &t;am swi&d;e mid ealle acwanc. &t;&ae;t na&t;er ne leoht ne tr&ae;ndel ne nan &t;ing mid ealle of him w&ae;s ges&ae;wen. 
 &amp; swa &t;urhwunode fullneah o&d; d&ae;g. &amp; sy&d;&t;an full &amp; beorhte scinende &ae;tywde. he w&ae;s &t;&ae;s ylcan d&ae;ges feowertyne nihta eald. 
 Ealle &t;a niht w&ae;s seo lyft swi&d;e clene. &amp; &t;a steorran ofer eall &t;a heofon swi&d;e beorhte scinende. &amp; treoww&ae;stmas wurdon &t;&ae;re nihte &t;urh forste swi&d;e fornumene. 
 &D;&ae;r &ae;fter on Iunies mon&d;e &ae;tywde an steorra nor&d;aneastan. &amp; his leoma stod toforan him on &t;et su&d;west. &amp; &t;us manega niht w&ae;s ges&ae;wen. 
 &amp; fur&d;or nihtes sy&d;&d;an he ufor astah. he w&ae;s gesewen onb&ae;c on &t;&ae;t nor&d;west gangende. 
 &D;ises geares wurdon bel&ae;nde Philippus de Brause. &amp; Willelm Mallet. &amp; Willelm Bainart. 
 Eac &t;ises geares for&d;ferde Elias eorl. &t;e &t;a Mannie of &t;am cynge Heanri geheold. &amp; on cweow. 
 &amp; &ae;fter his forsi&d;e feng to se eorl of Angeow. &amp; hi togeanes &t;am cynge heold.
