 &D;is w&ae;s swi&d;e gedeorfsum gear her on lande &t;urh gyld &t;e se cyng nam for his dohter gyfte. &amp; &t;urh ungew&ae;dera. for hwan eor&d;westmas wurdon swi&d;e amyrde. &amp; treowwestmas ofer eall &t;is land forneah eall forwurdon. 
 &D;ises geares me began &ae;rost to weorcenne on &t;am niwan mynstre on Ceortes&ae;ge. 
 On &t;ison geare ne b&ae;r se kyng Henri his coronan to Cristes m&ae;ssan. ne to Eastron. ne to Pentecosten. 
 &amp; innan August he ferde ofer s&ae; into Normandig. for unsehte &t;e wi&d; him h&ae;fdon sume be &t;am gem&ae;ran of France. &amp; swi&d;ost for &t;am eorle of Angeow &t;e &t;a Mannie togeanes him heold. 
 And sy&d;&d;an he &t;yder ofer com. manega unrada &amp; b&ae;rnetta &amp; hergunga hi heom betweonan gedydan. 
 On &t;ison geare for&d;ferde se eorl Rotbert of Flandran. &amp; feng his sunu Baldewine &t;&ae;rto. 
 &D;ises geares w&ae;s swi&d;e lang winter. &amp; hefig tyme. &amp; strang. &amp; &t;urh &t;&ae;t eor&d;w&ae;stmas wurdon swi&d;e amyrde. &amp; gewear&d; se m&ae;sta orfcwealm &t;e &ae;nig mann mihte gemunan. 
 Eall &t;is gear wunode se cyng Henri on Normandig for &t;&ae;re unsehte &t;e he h&ae;fde wi&d; France. &amp; wi&d; &t;one eorl of Angeow &t;e &t;a Mannie togeanes him heold. 
 &amp; onmang &t;am &t;e he &t;&ae;r w&ae;s. he bel&ae;nde &t;one eorl of Eureus. &amp; Willelm Crispin. &amp; ut of Normandi adraf. 
 &amp; Philippe de Braus his land ageaf. &t;e &ae;r w&ae;s bel&ae;nd. &amp; Rotbert de B&ae;lesme he let niman &amp; on prisune don. 
 &D;is w&ae;s swi&d;e god gear &amp; swi&d;e wistfull on wudan &amp; on feldan. ac hit w&ae;s swi&d;e hefig tyme &amp; sorhfull &t;urh orm&ae;tne mancwealm. 
 Her on &t;ison gear w&ae;s se cyng Henri to Natiuite&d; &amp; to Eastron. &amp; to Pentecosten on Normandig. 
 &amp; &t;&ae;r&ae;fter to sumeran he s&ae;nde hider to lande Rotbert de B&ae;lesme into &t;am castele to W&ae;rham. &amp; himsylf sona &t;&ae;r&ae;fter hider to lande com. 
 On &t;ison geare heold se cyng Henri his hyred to Natiuite&d; on Windlesoran. &amp; &t;&ae;r geares sy&d;&d;an he ne heold hired nan oftar. 
 And tomiddan sumeran he ferde mid fyrde into Wealon. &amp; &t;a Wyliscean coman &amp; wi&d; &t;one cyng gri&d;edon. 
 &amp; he let &t;&ae;r inne castelas weorcean. &amp; &t;&ae;r&ae;fter innan Septembris he for ofer s&ae; into Normandig. 
 &D;ises geares on &ae;fteward Mai w&ae;s gesewen an selcu&d; steorra mid langan leoman manege niht scinende. 
 Eac on &t;is ylcan geare w&ae;s swa mycel ebba &ae;ghw&ae;r anes d&ae;ges swa nan man &ae;ror ne gemunde. &amp; swa &t;&ae;t man ferde ridende &amp; gangende ofer T&ae;mese be eastan &t;&ae;re brigge on Lunden. 
 &T;ises geares w&ae;ron swi&d;e mycele windas on Octobris mon&d;e. ac he w&ae;s orm&ae;te mycel on &t;a niht Octabris sancti Martini. &amp; &t;&ae;t gehw&ae;r on wudan &amp; on tunan gecydde. 
 Eac on &t;isum geare se cyng geaf &t;et arcebiscoprice on Cantwarabyrig Raulfe. se w&ae;s &ae;ror biscop on Hrofeceastre. 
 And se arcebiscop on Eoferwic Thomas for&d;ferde. &amp; feng Turstein &t;&ae;rto. se w&ae;s &ae;ror &t;&ae;s cynges capelein. 
 On &t;&ae;s ylcan tyme feorde se cyng toweard &t;one s&ae; &amp; ofer wolde. ac w&ae;der him l&ae;tte. 
 &T;a hwile &t;a sende he his writ &ae;fter &t;one abbod Ernulf of Burh. &amp; bebead him &t;&ae;t he efeostlice scolde to him cuman. for&t;i &t;&ae;t he wolde sprecon mid him d&ae;rne sprece. 
 &D;a he to him com. &t;a neodde he him to &t;am biscoprice of Hrofeceastre. &amp; &t;a arcebiscopes &amp; biscopes &amp; &t;&ae;t duge&d; &t;&ae;t w&ae;s on Englalande for&d; mid se cyng. 
 &amp; he lange wi&d;stod. ac hit ne forheol naht. 
 &amp; se cyng &t;a bebead &t;one arcebiscop &t;&ae;t he sceolde him l&ae;den to Cantwarabyrig &amp; bl&ae;tson him to biscop wolde he nolde he. 
 &T;is w&ae;s don on &t;&ae;re tuna &t;a man cleopa&d; Burne. &t;&ae;t w&ae;s &t;es d&ae;ges xvii kalend&ae; Octobris. 
 &D;a &t;e munecas of Burch hit herdon s&ae;gen. &t;a w&ae;ron hi swa sari swa hi n&ae;fre &ae;r ne w&ae;ron. for&t;i &t;&ae;t he w&ae;s swi&d;e god &amp; softe man. &amp; dyde mycel to gode wi&d;innan &amp; wi&d;utan. &t;a hwile &t;e he &t;&ae;r wunode. 
 God &ae;lmihtig wunie &ae;fre mid him. 
 &D;a sona &t;&ae;r&ae;fter &t;a geaf se cyng &t;one abbodrice an munec of S&ae;is Iohan w&ae;s gehaten. &t;urh &t;&ae;s arcebiscopes gearnunge of Cantwarbyrig. 
 &amp; sona &t;&ae;r&ae;fter sende se cyng him &amp; se arcebiscop of Cantwarbyrig to Rome &ae;fter &t;es &ae;rcebiscopes pallium. &amp; an munec mid him Warner is gehaten. &amp; &t;one &ae;rcedi&ae;cne Iohane &t;es arcebiscop neafe. &amp; hi &t;&ae;r wellsp&ae;ddon. 
 &D;is w&ae;s don &t;es d&ae;ges xi kalend&ae; Octobris  on &t;one tuna &t;e man cleopa&d; Rugenore. 
 &amp; &t;es ylces d&ae;ges eode se cyng on scipa on Portesmu&d;e. 
 Her w&ae;s se cyng Henri to Natiuite&d; on Normandig. &amp; onmang &t;am &t;e he &t;&ae;r w&ae;s. he dyde &t;&ae;t ealle &t;a heafodm&ae;n on Normandig dydon manr&ae;den &amp; holda&d;as his sunu Willelme &t;e he be his cwene h&ae;fde. 
 &amp; &ae;fter &t;an sy&d;&d;an innon Iulies mon&d;e hider into lande com. 
 &D;ises geares w&ae;s swa strang winter mid snawe &amp; mid forste. swa nan man &t;e &t;a lifode &ae;r &t;an nan strengre ne gemunde. &amp; wear&d; &t;urh &t;&ae;t ungem&ae;te orfcwealm. 
 On &t;ison geare s&ae;nde se papa Paschalis Raulfe &ae;rcebiscop on Cantwarabyrig pallium hider to lande. &amp; he his onfeng mid mycelan wur&d;scipe &ae;t his arcestole on Cantwarabyrig. 
 Hine brohte Ansealm abbod of Rome se w&ae;s nefa Ansealmes &ae;rcebiscop. &amp; se abbod Iohan of Burh. 
 On &t;ison geare w&ae;s se cyng Henri to Natiuite&d; &ae;t sancte Albane. &amp; &t;&ae;r let &t;&ae;t mynster halgian. &amp; to Eastron on Wudiham. 
 &amp; Wes eac &t;yses geares swi&d;e hefigtyme winter &amp; strang &amp; lang. wi&d; orf &amp; wi&d; ealle &t;ing. 
 And se cyng &ae;fter Eastron sona ferde ofer s&ae; into Normandig. &amp; wurdon manega unrada &amp; r&ae;funga. &amp; castelas genumene betwux France &amp; Normandig. 
 M&ae;st &t;is unsehte w&ae;s for&t;an &t;e se cyng Henri fylste his nefan &t;am eorle T&ae;dbalde de Blais. &t;e &t;a wyrre h&ae;fde togeanes his hlaforde &t;am cynge of France Lo&d;ewis. 
 &D;is w&ae;s swi&d;e geswincfull gear &amp; byrstfull on eor&d;w&ae;stman. &t;urh &t;a orm&ae;te reinas &t;e coman sona onforan August. &amp; swi&d;e gedrehton &amp; geswencton &t;e gyt &t;e com Candelm&ae;ssan. 
 Eac &t;is gear w&ae;s swa g&ae;sne on m&ae;stene. swa &t;&ae;t on eallon &t;ison lande. ne eac on Wealon ne gehyrde me of nanan segcean. 
 &D;is land &amp; &t;as leodon wurdon eac &t;yses geares oftr&ae;dlice sare geswencte. &t;urh &t;a gyld &t;e se cyng nam. &ae;g&d;er ge binnan burgan &amp; butan. 
 On &t;isum ylcan geare b&ae;rnde eall &t;&ae;t mynstre of Burh. &amp; eall&ae; &t;a husas butan se Captelhus &amp; se Sl&ae;pperne. &amp; &t;&ae;r to eac b&ae;rnde eall &t;a m&ae;ste d&ae;l of &t;a tuna. 
 Eall &t;is belamp on an Frigd&ae;g. &t;&ae;t w&ae;s ii Non&ae; Augusti. 
 Eall &t;is gear wunode se cyng Henri on Normandig. for &t;es cynges unsehte of France &amp; his o&d;ra nehhebura. 
 &amp; &t;a to &d;an sumeran com se cyng of France &amp; se eorl of Flandra mid him mid fyrde into Normandig. &amp; ane niht &t;&ae;rinne wunedon. &amp; on morgen butan gefeohte ongean ferden. 
 &amp; Normandig wear&d; swi&d;e gedreht. &ae;g&d;er ge &t;urh gyld. ge &t;urh fyrde &t;e se cing Henri &t;&ae;r ongean gaderode. 
 Eac &t;eos &t;eode &t;urh &t;is ylce &t;urh manigfealde gyld. wear&d; strange geswenct. 
 &D;ises geares eac on &t;&ae;re nihte kalend&ae; Decembris wurdon orm&ae;tlica w&ae;dera mid &t;unre. &amp; lihtinge. &amp; reine. &amp; hagole. 
 And on &t;&ae;re nihte iii idus Decembris wear&d; se mona lange nihtes swylce he eall blodig w&ae;re. &amp; sy&d;&d;an a&d;istrode. 
 Eac on &t;&ae;re nihte xvii kalend&ae; Ianuarii w&ae;s seo heofon swy&d;e read gesewen. swylce hit bryne w&ae;re. 
 And on Octabus sancti Johannis Evangel&ae; w&ae;s seo mycele eor&d;byfung on Lumbardige. for hwan manega mynstras &amp; turas. &amp; huses gefeollon. &amp; mycelne hearm on mannan gedydon. 
 &D;is w&ae;s swy&d;e byrstful gear on corne. &t;urh &t;a renas &t;e forneh ealles geares ne geswicon. 
 And se abbod Gilebert of Westmynstre for&d;ferde viii idus Decembris. And Farits abbod of Abbandune vii kalend&ae; Martii. 
 And on &t;isum ylcan geare. 
 Her eall &t;is gear wunode se cyng Henri on Normandig. for &t;es cynges wyrre of France. &amp; &t;&ae;s eorles of Angeow. &amp; &t;&ae;s eorles of Flandran. 
 &amp; se eorl of Flandra war&d; innan Normandig gewundod. &amp; swa gewundod into Flandran for. 
 &D;urh &t;isra unsehte wear&d; se cyng swy&d;e gedreht. &amp; mycel forleas. &ae;g&d;er ge on feoh &amp; eac on lande. 
 &amp; m&ae;st hine dryfdon his agene m&ae;n &t;e him gelome fram bugon. &amp; swicon. &amp; to his feondan cyrdon. &amp; heom to &t;&ae;s cynges hearme &amp; swicdome heora castelas ageafon. 
 Eall &t;is strange gebohte Englaland. &t;urh &t;a m&ae;nigfealdlice gyld &t;e ealles &t;ises geares ne geswicon. 
 On &t;ison geare on &t;&ae;re wucon Theophanie w&ae;s anes &ae;fenes swy&d;e mycel lihtinge. &amp; ungemetlice sl&ae;ge &t;&ae;r&ae;fter. 
 And seo cwen Mahald for&d;ferde on Westmynstre &t;&ae;s d&ae;ges kalend&ae; Mai. &amp; &t;&ae;r w&ae;s bebyrged. 
 And se eorl Rotbert of Mellent &t;ises geares eac for&d;ferde. 
 Eac on &t;ison geare to sancte Thomas m&ae;sse. w&ae;s swa swi&d;e ungemetlice mycel wind. &t;&ae;t nan man &t;e &t;a lifode n&ae;nne maran ne gemunde. &amp; &t;&ae;t w&ae;s &ae;ghwer geseone. &ae;g&d;er ge on husan. &amp; eac on treowan. 
 &D;ises geares eac for&d;ferde se papa Paschalis. &amp; feng Iohan of Gaitan to &t;am papdome. &t;am w&ae;s o&d;er nama Gelasius. 
 &D;is gear eall wunode se cyng Henri on Normandig. &amp; w&ae;s &t;urh &t;&ae;s cynges wyrre of France. &amp; eac his agenra manna &t;e him mid swicdome fram w&ae;ron mid abugon. oft r&ae;dlice swy&t;e gedreht. o&d;&d;et &t;a twegen cyngas innan Normandige. mid heoran folcan coman tog&ae;dere. 
 &T;&ae;r wear&d; seo cyng of France aflymed. &amp; ealle his betste m&ae;n genumene. 
 &amp; sy&d;&d;an &t;&ae;s cynges m&ae;n Heanriges manega him to gebugen. &amp; wi&d; hine acordedan &t;e &ae;ror mid heora castelan him togeanes w&ae;ron. &amp; sume &t;a castelas he mid streng&d;e genam. 
 &D;ises geares ferde Willelm &t;&ae;s cynges sunu Heanriges &amp; &t;&ae;re cwene Mahalde into Normandige to his f&ae;der. &amp; &t;&ae;r wear&d; him forgifen &amp; to wife beweddod &t;&ae;s eorles dohter of Angeow. 
 On sancte Michaeles m&ae;sse&ae;fen w&ae;s mycel eor&d;bifung on suman steodan her on lande. &t;eah swy&d;ost on Gloweceastrescire. &amp; on Wigreceastrescire. 
 On &t;is ylcan geare for&d;ferde se papa Gelasius on &t;as halfe &t;&ae;re muntan. &amp; w&ae;s on Clunig bebyrged. 
 &amp; &ae;fter him se arcebiscop of uiana wear&d; to papan gecoren. &t;am wear&d; nama Calixtus. 
 Se sy&d;&d;an to sancte Lucas m&ae;ssan euangelista com into France to R&ae;ins. &amp; &t;&ae;r heold concilium. &amp; se arcebiscop Turstein of Eoferwic &t;yder ferde. 
 &amp; for&t;i &t;e he togeanes rihte &amp; togeanes &t;am arcestole on Cantwarabyrig. &amp; togeanes &t;&ae;s cynges willan his had &ae;t &t;am papan underfeng. him wi&d;cw&ae;&d; se cyng &ae;lces geanfares to Englalande. 
 &amp; he &t;us his arcebiscoprices &t;&ae;rnode. &amp; mid &t;am papan towardes Rome for. 
 Eac on &t;ison geare for&d;ferde se eorl Baldewine of Flandran of &t;am wundan &t;e he innan Normandige gefeng. 
 &amp; &ae;fter him feng Carl his fa&d;asunu to &t;am rice. se w&ae;s Cnutes sunu &t;&ae;s haligan cynges of Denmarcan. 
 &D;ises geares wurdon sehte seo cyng of Englelande &amp; se of France. 
 &amp; &ae;fter heora sehte acordedan ealles &t;&ae;s cynges Heanriges agene m&ae;n wi&d; hine innan Normandige. &amp; se eorl of Flandran. &amp; se of Puntiw. 
 Sy&d;&d;an her&ae;fter s&ae;tte se cyng Henrig his castelas &amp; his land on Normandi &ae;fter his willan. &amp; swa toforan Aduent hider to lande for. 
 &amp; on &t;am fare wurdon adruncene &t;&ae;s cynges twegen sunan Willelm &amp; Ricard. &amp; Ricard eorl of Ceastre. &amp; Ottuel his bro&d;or. &amp; swy&d;e manega of &t;&ae;s cynges hired  stiwardas  &amp; bur&t;enas  &amp; byrlas  &amp; of mystlicean wican. &amp; ungerim swy&d;e &ae;nlices folces for&d; mid. 
 &D;ysra dea&d; w&ae;s heora freondan twyfealdlic sar. an &t;et hi swa fearlice &t;ises lifes losedan. o&d;er &t;&ae;t feawa heora lichaman ahw&ae;r sy&d;&d;an fundena w&ae;ron. 
 &D;ises geares com &t;et leoht to Sepulchrum Domini innan Ierusalem twiges. &ae;nes to Eastron. and o&d;re si&d;e to Assumptio sancte Marie. swa swa geleaffulle s&ae;don &t;e &t;anon coman. 
 An se arcebiscop Turstein of Eoferwic wear&d; &t;urh &t;one papan wi&d; &t;one cyng acordad. &amp; hider to lande com. &amp; his biscoprices onfeng. &t;eah hit &t;am arcebiscop of Cantwarabyrig swy&d;e ungewille w&ae;re. 
 Her w&ae;s se cyng Henri to Cristes m&ae;ssan on Bramtune. &amp; &t;&ae;r&ae;fter toforan Candelm&ae;ssan on Windlesoran him to wife forgyfen A&d;elis &amp; sy&d;&d;an to cwene gehalgod. seo w&ae;s &t;&ae;s heretogan dohtor of Luuaine. 
 And se mona a&t;ystrode on &t;&ae;re nihte Non&ae; Aprilis. &amp; w&ae;s x iiii luna. 
 And se cyng w&ae;s to Eastran on Beorclea. and &t;&ae;r&ae;fter to Pentecosten he heold mycelne hired on Westmynstre. 
 And sy&d;&d;an &t;&ae;s sumeres mid ferde into Wealan for. &amp; &t;a Wyliscean him ongean coman. &amp; &ae;fter &t;es cynges willan hi wi&d; hine acordedan. 
 &D;ises geares com se eorl of Angeow fram Ierusalem into his lande. &amp; sy&d;&d;an hider to lande sende. &amp; his dohter let feccean seo w&ae;s Willelme &t;es cynges sune &ae;ror to wife forgyfan. 
 And on &t;&ae;re nihte uigilia Natalis Domini w&ae;s swy&d;e mycel wind ofer eall &t;is land. &amp; &t;et wear&d; on manegan &t;ingan swy&d;e gesene. 
 On &t;is geare w&ae;s se king Heanri on Cristes m&ae;ssan on Norhtwic. &amp; on Pasches he weas on Norhthamtune. 
 &amp; on &t;one lententyde &t;&ae;r toforen forbearn se burch on Gleaweceastre. 
 &T;a hwile &t;e &t;a munecas sungen &t;&ae;re messe. &amp; se d&ae;cne hafde ongunnan &t;one godspel Preteriens Ihesu. &t;a com se fir on ufenweard &t;one stepel. &amp; forbearnde ealle &t;e minstre. &amp; ealle &t;a gersumes &t;e &t;&ae;r binnen w&ae;ron for uton feawe bec. &amp; iii messehakeles. &t;et wes &t;es d&ae;ies viii idus Martii. 
 &amp; &t;&ae;r&ae;fter &t;e Tywesd&ae;i &ae;fter Palmes Sunend&ae;i w&ae;s swi&d;e micel wind on &t;&ae;t d&ae;i xi kalend&ae; Aprilis. 
 &T;&ae;r&ae;fter comen feale tacne widehwear on Englaland &amp; feole dwild wearen geseogen &amp; geheord. 
 &amp; &t;es niht viii kalend&ae; Augusti w&ae;s swi&d;e micel eor&d;dyne ofer eal Sumersetescire &amp; on Gleawecestrescire. 
 Si&d;&d;on on &t;&ae;s d&ae;i vi idus Septembris &t;et w&ae;s on sancte Mari&e; messed&ae;i. &t;a wear&d; swi&d;e mycel wind fram &t;a undern d&ae;ies to &t;a swarte nihte. 
 &T;eos ilce geares for&d;ferde Raulf seo &ae;rcebiscop of Cantwarbyrig. &t;&ae;t w&ae;s on &t;&ae;s d&ae;ies xiii kalend&ae; Nouembris. 
 &T;&ae;r&ae;fter w&ae;ron feole scipmen on s&ae;. &amp; on w&ae;ter. &amp; saedon &t;&ae;t hi s&ae;gon on nor&d;east fir micel &amp; brad wi&d; &t;one eor&d;e. &amp; weax on leng&t;e up on an to &t;am wolcne. 
 &amp; se wolcne undide on fower healfe and faht &t;&ae;r togeanes. swilc hit scolde acwencen. &amp; se fir weax na &t;a ma up to &t;e heouene. 
 &T;&ae;t fir hi seagon in &d;e d&ae;irime and l&ae;ste swa lange &t;&ae;t hit w&ae;s liht ofer eall. &t;et w&ae;s &t;&ae;s d&ae;ies vii IDVS Decembris. 
 On &t;yssum geare w&ae;s se king Henri on Cristes tyde &ae;t Dunestaple. &amp; &t;&ae;r comen &t;es eorles sandermen of Angeow to him. 
 &amp; &t;eonen he ferde to Wudestoke. &amp; his biscopes &amp; his hird eal mid him. 
 &T;a tidde hit on an Wodnesdei. &t;et w&ae;s on iiii idus Ianuarii. &t;et se king rad in his derfald and se biscop Roger of Seresbyrig on an half him. and se biscop Rotbert Bloet of Lincolne on o&d;er half him. &amp; riden &t;&ae;r sprecende. 
 &T;a aseh dune se biscop of Lincolne &amp; seide to &t;am kyng. laferd kyng ic swelte. 
 &amp; se kyng alihte dune of his hors &amp; alehte hine betwux his earmes. &amp; let hine beran ham to his inne. &amp; wear&d; &t;a sone dead. 
 &amp; man ferode hine to Lincolne mid micel wur&d;scipe. &amp; bebyrigde hine toforen sanct&e; Mari&e; wefod. 
 &amp; hine bebyrigde se biscop of Ceastre Rotbert Pecce&d; w&ae;s gehaten. 
 &D;a sone &t;&ae;r&ae;fter sende se kyng hise write ofer eall Englalande. &amp; bed hise biscopes &amp; hise abbates &amp; hise &t;eignes ealle &t;et hi scolden cumen to his gewitenemot on Candelmesse deig to Gleawceastre him togeanes. &amp; hi swa diden. 
 &D;a hi w&ae;ran &t;&ae;r gegaderod. &t;a bed se cyng heom &t;&ae;t hi scoldon cesen hem &ae;rcebiscop to Cantwarabyrig swa hwam swa swa hi woldon. &amp; he hem hit wolde ty&t;ian. 
 &D;a spr&ae;con &d;a biscopas hem betwenan. and s&ae;den &t;&ae;t hi n&ae;fre mare ne wolden hafen munechades man to ercebiscop ofer hem. 
 Ac iedon ealle samodlice to &t;one kyng and ieornden &t;&ae;t hi mosten cesen of clerchades man swa hwam swa swa hi wolden to ercebiscop. &amp; se kyng hit hem tidde. 
 &D;is w&ae;s eall ear gedon &d;urh se biscop of Seresbyrig. &amp; &t;urh se biscop of Lincolne &ae;r he w&ae;re dead. for&d;i &t;et n&ae;fre ne luueden hi munece regol. ac w&ae;ron &ae;fre tog&ae;nes muneces &amp; here regol. 
 And se prior &amp; se munecas of Cantwarabyrig. &amp; ealle &t;a o&d;re &t;e &d;&ae;r w&ae;ron munechades men hit wi&d;cw&ae;&d;en fulle twa dagas. 
 Ac hit naht ne beheld. for se biscop of S&ae;resbyrig w&ae;s strang &amp; wealde eall Engleland. &amp; w&ae;s &t;&ae;r togeanes eall &t;&ae;t he mihte &amp; cu&d;e. 
 &D;a cusen hi an clerc Willelm of Curboil w&ae;s gehaten. he was canonie of an mynstre Cicc hatte. &amp; brohten him toforen se kyng. 
 &amp; se kyng him geaf &d;one &ae;rcebiscoprice. &amp; ealle &t;a biscopas him underfengen. 
 Him wi&d;cw&ae;&d;en muneces &amp; eorles &amp; &t;eignes ealle mest &t;e &t;&ae;r w&ae;ron. 
 On &t;a ilca tyma ferden &t;es eorles sandermen mid uns&ae;hte fram kyng. na of his gyfe naht ne rohton. 
 On &t;a ilca tyma com an Legat of Rome Henri w&ae;s gehaten. he w&ae;s abbot of Sancti Johannis mynstre of Anieli. 
 &amp; he com &ae;fter &t;e Rome scot. &amp; he s&ae;de &t;one cyng &t;&ae;t hit w&ae;s togeanes riht &t;&ae;t man scolde setten clerc ofer muneces. &amp; swa swa hi h&ae;fden cosen &ae;rcebiscop &ae;ror in here capitele &ae;fter rihte. 
 Ac se cyng hit nolde undon. for &t;es biscop luuen of S&ae;resbyrig. 
 &D;a ferde se &ae;rcebiscop sone &t;&ae;r&ae;fter to Cantwarabyrig &amp; w&ae;s &t;&ae;r underfangan &t;&ae;h hit w&ae;re here un&t;ancas. &amp; was &t;&ae;re sone gebletsod to biscop fram se biscop of Lundene. &amp; se biscop Ernulf of Roueceastre. &amp; se biscop Willelm Gifard of Winceastre. &amp; se biscop Bernard of Wales. &amp; se biscop Roger of Searesbyrig. 
 &D;a sone in &t;e lenten ferde se &ae;rcebiscop to Rome &ae;fter his pallium. 
 &amp; mid him ferde se biscop Bernard of Wales. &amp; Sefred abbot of Gleastingbyrig. &amp; Anselm abbot os Sancti &AE;dmund. &amp; Iohan &ae;rced&ae;cne of Cantwarabyrig. &amp; Gifard w&ae;s &t;es kinges hirdclerc. 
 On &t;a ilca tima ferde se &ae;rcebiscop &d;urstan of Eoferwic to Rome &t;urh &t;es papes hese. 
 &amp; com &t;ider &d;re dagas &ae;r se &ae;rcebiscop of Cantwarabyrig come. &amp; w&ae;s &t;&ae;re underfangan mid micel wur&d;scipe. 
 &D;a com se &ae;rcebiscop of Cantwarabyrig &amp; w&ae;s &d;&ae;re fulle seoueniht &ae;r hi mihte cumen to &t;es papes spr&ae;ce. 
 &T;&ae;t w&ae;s for&t;an &t;&ae;t hit w&ae;s don &d;one pape to understanden &t;&ae;t he h&ae;fde underfangen &d;one &ae;rcebiscoprice togeanes &t;a muneces of &t;e mynstre &amp; togeanes rihte. 
 Ac &t;&ae;t ofercom Rome &t;et ofercume&d; eall weoruld &t;&ae;t is gold &amp; seolure. &amp; se pape swe&d;olode &amp; gaf him his pallium. 
 &amp; se &ae;rcebiscop swor him under&t;eodnysse of ealle &d;a &t;ing &t;&ae;t se papa him on leide on Sancti Petres heuod and Sancti Paules. &amp; sende him ham &d;a mid his bletsunge. 
 &D;a hwile &t;&ae;t se &ae;rcebiscop w&ae;s ut of lande. geaf se kyng &d;one biscoprice of Ba&d;e &t;es cwenes canceler Godefrei&d; w&ae;s gehaten. he w&ae;s boren of Luuein. &t;&ae;t w&ae;s &t;es d&ae;iges Annuntiatio Sancte Marie at Wudestoke. 
 &D;a sone &t;&ae;r&ae;fter ferde se king to Winceastre &amp; w&ae;s ealle Eastrentyde &t;&ae;re. 
 &amp; &t;a hwile &t;&ae;t he &t;&ae;r w&ae;s &t;a geaf he &t;one biscoprice of Lincolne an clerc Alexander w&ae;s gehaten. he w&ae;s &t;es biscopes nefe of Searesbyrig. 
 &T;is he dyde eall for &t;es biscopes luuen. 
 &D;a ferde se kyng &t;enen to Portesmu&d;e. &amp; l&ae;i &t;&ae;re eall ofer Pentecostewuce. 
 &T;a sone swa he h&ae;fde wind swa ferde he ofer into Normandie. &amp; bet&ae;hte &t;a eall Engleland to geamene &amp; to wealden &t;one biscop Roger of Searesbyrig. 
 &D;a w&ae;s se kyng eall &t;es geares in Normandie. &amp; weax &t;a micel unfri&d; betwux him &amp; hise &t;eignas. swa &t;&ae;t se eorl Walaram of Mellant. &amp; Hamalri. &amp; Hugo of Mundford. &amp; Willelm of Romare. and fela o&d;re wendan fram him &amp; helden here castles him togeanes. 
 &amp; se kyng held stranglice hem togeanes. &amp; &t;es ylces geares he wan of Walaram his castel Punt Aldemer. &amp; of Hugo Mundford. &amp; si&d;&d;en he spedde &ae;fre leong &t;e bet. 
 &D;es ylce geares &ae;r se biscop of Lincolne com to his biscoprice forbearn eallmeast se burh of Lincolne. &amp; micel ungerime folces w&ae;pmen &amp; wimmen forburnen. 
 &amp; swa mycel hearm &t;&ae;r w&ae;s gedon swa nan man hit cu&d;e o&t;er secgen. &t;et w&ae;s &t;es d&ae;ges xiiii kalend&ae; Iunii. 
 Eall &t;is gear wes se king Heanri on Normandi. &t;&ae;t wes for se miccle unfri&d; &t;&ae;t he heafde wi&d; se king Lo&d;ewis of France. &amp; wi&d; se eorl of Angeow. &amp; wi&d; his agene men alre mest. 
 &T;a gelamp hit on &t;es d&ae;ges Annuntiatio sanct&e; Marie &t;&ae;t se eorl Waleram of Mellant ferde fram his an castel Belmunt het to his an o&d;er castel Watteuile. 
 Mid him ferde &t;es kinges stiward of France Amalri. &amp; Hugo Gerueises sunu. &amp; Hugo of Munford. &amp; fela o&d;re godre cnihte. 
 &T;a comen hem togeanes &t;es kinges cnihtes of ealla &t;a casteles &d;a &t;&ae;r abuton w&ae;ron &amp; fuhton wi&d; hem &amp; aflemden hem &amp; namen &t;one eorl Waleram &amp; Hugo Gerueises sunu. &amp; Hugo of Mundford. &amp; fif &amp; twenti o&d;re cnihtes &amp; brohton hem to &t;one kinge. 
 &amp; se king let don &t;one eorl Waleram &amp; Hugo Gerueises sunu on heftnunge on &d;one castel on Ro&d;em. 
 &amp; Hugo of Mundford he sende to Engleland. &amp; let hine don on ifele bendas on &t;one castel on Gleucestre. 
 &amp; of &t;a o&d;re swa fela swa him &t;uhte he sende nor&d; &amp; su&d; to hise casteles on heftnunge. 
 &D;a si&d;&d;on ferde se king &amp; wan ealle &t;es eorles castelas Waleram &t;a w&ae;ron on Normandi. &amp; ealla &t;a o&d;re &t;a his wi&d;rewines healden him togeanes. 
 Eall was &t;es unfri&d; for &t;es eorles sunu Rotbert of Normandi Willelm het. 
 Se ilce Willelm hefde numen Fulkes eorles gingre dohter to wife of Angeow. 
 &amp; for&d;i se king of France &amp; ealle &t;as eorles heolden mid him &amp; ealle &t;a rice men. &amp; s&ae;idon &t;et se king heold his bro&d;er Rotbert mid wrange on heftnunge. &amp; his sunu Willelm mid unrihte aflemde ut of Normandi. 
 &D;es ilces geares w&ae;ron f&ae;la untime on Englelande. on corne &amp; on ealle westme. swa &t;&ae;t betweonen Cristesmesse &amp; Candelmesse man s&ae;lde &t;&ae;t acers&ae;d hw&ae;te &t;&ae;t is twegen sedl&ae;pas to six scillingas. &amp; &t;&ae;t b&ae;rlic &t;&ae;t is &t;re sedl&ae;pas to six scillingas. &amp; &t;&ae;t acers&ae;d aten &t;&ae;t is feower sedl&ae;pas to feower scillingas. 
 &T;et w&ae;s for&t;i &t;&ae;t corn w&ae;s litel. &amp; se penig w&ae;s swa ifel &t;&ae;t se man &t;a h&ae;fde at an market an pund he ne mihte cysten &t;&ae;rof for nan &t;ing twelfe penegas. 
 On &t;es ilces geares for&d;ferde se eadig biscop Ernulf of Roueceastre se &ae;ror w&ae;s abbot on Burch. &t;et w&ae;s &t;es d&ae;ies Idus Martii. 
 &amp; &t;&ae;r&ae;fter for&d;ferde se king Alexander of Scotlande on &t;es d&ae;ies ix kalend&ae; Mai. 
 &amp; Dauid his bro&d;er &t;a w&ae;s eorl on Nor&d;hamtunescire feng to rice and h&ae;fde &d;a ba&d;e togedere &t;one kinerice on Scotlande. &amp; &t;one eorldom on Englelande. 
 &amp; On &t;&ae;s d&ae;ies xix kalend&ae; Ianuarii for&d;ferde se pape on Rome Calistus w&ae;s gehaten. &amp; Honorius feng to papedom. 
 &D;es ilces geares &ae;fter sancti Andreas messe toforen Cristes messe held Raulf Basset &amp; &t;es kinges &d;&ae;ines gewitenemot on Le&t;ec&ae;strescire at Hundehoge. &amp; ahengen &t;&ae;r swa fela &t;efas swa n&ae;fre &ae;r ne w&ae;ron. &t;et w&ae;ron on &t;a litle hwile ealles feower &amp; feowerti manne  &amp; six men spilde of here &ae;gon &amp; of here stanes. 
 Fela so&d;feste men s&ae;idon &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;r w&ae;ron manege mid micel unrihte gespilde. 
 Oc ure Laford God &ae;lmihtig &t;a eall digelnesse se&d; &amp; wat  he seo&d; &t;&ae;t man l&ae;t &t;&ae;t &ae;rme folc mid ealle unrihte. &ae;rost man hem ber&ae;fo&d; her eahte and si&t;&d;on man hem ofsl&ae;&d;. 
 Ful heui g&ae;r w&ae;s hit se man &t;e &ae;ni god heafde. him me hit ber&ae;fode mid strange geoldes &amp; mid strange motes. &t;e nan ne heafde st&ae;rf of hungor. 
 On &t;is g&ae;r sende se king Henri toforen Cristes messe of Normandi to Englalande &amp; bebead &t;et man scolde beniman ealle &t;a minitere &t;e w&ae;ron on Englelande heora liman. &t;&ae;t w&ae;s here elces riht hand &amp; heora stanen bene&d;an. 
 &T;&ae;t w&ae;s for se man &d;e hafde an pund he ne mihte cysten &ae;nne peni at anne market. 
 &amp; se biscop Roger of S&ae;resbyrig sende ofer eall Englalande &amp; bebead hi ealle &t;&ae;t hi scolden cumen to Winceastre to Cristes messe. 
 &T;a hi &d;ider coman &d;a nam man an &amp; an &amp; benam &ae;lc &d;one riht hand &amp; &t;a stanes bene&d;an. 
 Eall &t;is w&ae;s gedon wi&d; innon &t;a twelfniht. &amp; &t;&ae;t w&ae;s eall mid micel rihte for&d;i &t;&ae;t hi hafden fordon eall &t;&ae;t land mid here micele fals. &t;&ae;t hi ealle abohton. 
 On &t;es ilces g&ae;res sende se papa of Rome to &d;ise lande an cardinal Iohan of Creme w&ae;s gehaten. 
 He com first to &t;one king on Normandi. &amp; se king hine underfeng mid micel wur&d;scipe. 
 Beteahte hine si&d;&d;on &t;one &ae;rcebiscop Willelme of Cantwarabyrig. &amp; he hine ledde to Cantwarabyrig. &amp; he w&ae;s &t;&ae;r underfangen mid micel wur&d;scipe &amp; mid micel processionem. 
 &amp; he sang &d;one hehmesse on Eastren d&ae;i &ae;t Cristes wefod. 
 &amp; si&d;&d;on he ferde ofer eall Englalande to ealle &t;a biscoprices &amp; abbotrices &t;a w&ae;ron on &t;is lande. 
 &amp; ofer eall he w&ae;s underfangen mid wur&d;scipe &amp; ealle hine i&ae;fen micele gife &amp; m&ae;re. 
 &amp; si&d;&d;on he heold his concilie on Lundene fulle &t;reo dagas on natiuitas sanct&e; Mari&e; on Septembris mid &ae;rcebiscopes &amp; mid leodbiscopas &amp; abbotes &amp; l&ae;red &amp; lawed. bead &t;&ae;r &t;a ilce lagas &t;a ANSELM &ae;rcebiscop h&ae;fde &ae;ror beboden &amp; feala ma &t;eah hit litel forstode. 
 &amp; &t;eonon he for ofer s&ae; sone &ae;fter sancte Michaeles messe &amp; swa to Rome. &amp; se &ae;rcebiscop Willelm of Cantwarabyrig. &amp; se &ae;rcebiscop Turstein of Eferwic. &amp; se biscop Alexander of Lincolne. &amp; se biscop of Lo&t;ene Iohan. &amp; se abbot of sancte Alban Gosfrei&d; &amp; w&ae;ran &t;&ae;r underfangen of &t;one pape Honorius mid micel wur&d;scipe. &amp; w&ae;ron &t;&ae;re eall &t;one wintre. 
 On &d;es ilces geares wear&d; swa micel flod on sancte Laurenties messed&ae;ig &t;&ae;t feola tunes &amp; men weor&d;an adrencte. &amp; brigges tobrokene. &amp; corn &amp; m&ae;dwe spilt mid ealle. &amp; hunger &amp; cwealm on men &amp; on erue. &amp; on ealle westme swa micel untime wear&d; swa hit ne w&ae;s feola gear &ae;r. 
 &amp; &t;es ilces geares for&d;ferde se abbot Iohan of Burch on ii IDus Octobris. 
 Eall &t;is geare w&ae;s se kyng Heanri on Normandi eall to &ae;fter heruest. 
 &T;a com he to &t;is lande betwyx natiuitas sancte Marie &amp; Michaeles messe. 
 Mid him com se cwen &amp; his dohter &t;&ae;t he &ae;ror hafde giuen &t;one kasere Heanri of Loherenge to wife. 
 &amp; he brohte mid him &t;one eorl Waleram &amp; Hugo Gerueises sunu. 
 &amp; &t;one eorl he sende to Brigge on heftnunge. &amp; &t;eonon he sende him to Walingeforde si&d;&d;on. &amp; Hugo to Windlesofra. &amp; let hine don on harde bande. 
 &amp; &t;a &ae;fter Michaeles messe com se Scotte kyng Dauid of Scotlande hider to lande. 
 &amp; se kyng Heanri underfeng hine mid micel wur&d;scipe. 
 &amp; he wunode &t;a eall &t;et gear on &t;is lande. 
 On &t;es ilces geares let se kyning nimen his bro&d;er Rotbert fram &t;one biscop Roger of S&ae;resbyri. &amp; betahte hine his sune Rotbert eorl of Gleuc&ae;stre. &amp; let hine l&ae;den to Bricstowe &amp; &t;&ae;r diden on &t;one castel. 
 &T;&ae;t w&ae;s eall don &d;urh his dohtres r&ae;d. &amp; &t;urh se Scotte kyng DAUID hire eam. 
 &D;is gear heald se kyng Heanri his hird &ae;t Cristes m&ae;sse on Windlesoure. 
 &T;&ae;r w&ae;s se Scotte kyng Dauid. &amp; eall &d;a heaued l&ae;red &amp; l&ae;uued &t;&ae;t w&ae;s on Engleland. 
 &amp; &t;&ae;r he let sweren ercebiscopes &amp; biscopes &amp; abbotes &amp; eorles &amp; ealle &t;a &d;eines &d;a &t;&ae;r w&ae;ron his dohter &AE;&d;elic Englaland &amp; Normandi to hande &ae;fter his d&ae;i. &t;e &ae;r w&ae;s &t;es Caseres wif of Sexlande. 
 &amp; sende hire si&d;&d;en to Normandi. &amp; mid hire ferde hire bro&d;er Rotbert eorl of Gleucestre. &amp; BRIAN &t;es eorles sunu Alein Fergan. &amp; leot hire beweddan &t;es eorles sunu of Angeow Gosfrei&d; Mart&ae;l w&ae;s gehaten. 
 Hit of&t;uhte na&t;ema ealle Frencisc &amp; Englisc. oc se kyng hit dide for to hauene sibbe of se eorl of Angeow. &amp; for helpe to hauene tog&ae;nes his neue Willelm. 
 &D;es ilces g&ae;res on &t;one lententide w&ae;s se eorl Karle of Flandres ofslagen on ane circe &t;&ae;r he l&ae;i &amp; b&ae;d hine to Gode to for &t;one weofede amang &t;ane messe fram his agene manne. 
 &amp; se kyng of France brohte &t;one eorles sunu Willelm of Normandi &amp; i&ae;f hine &t;one eorldom. &amp; &t;et landfolc him wi&d;toc. 
 &T;es ilce Willelm h&ae;fde &ae;ror numen &d;es eorles dohter of Angeow to wife oc hi w&ae;ron si&d;&d;en totweamde for sibreden. &t;et wes eall &d;urh &t;one kyng Heanri of Engleland. 
 Si&d;&d;en &t;a nam he &t;es kynges wifes swuster of France to wife. &amp; for&t;i i&ae;f se kyng him &t;one eorldom of Flandres. 
 &D;es ilce g&ae;res he g&ae;f &t;one abbotrice of Burch an abbot Heanri w&ae;s gehaten of Peitowe. se h&ae;fde his abbotrice Sancti Johannis of Angeli on hande. 
 &amp; ealle &t;a &ae;rcebiscopes &amp; biscopes seidon &t;&ae;t hit w&ae;s togeanes riht. &amp; &t;&ae;t he ne mihte hafen twa abbotrices on hande. 
 Oc se ilce Heanri dide &t;one king to understandene &t;&ae;t he h&ae;fde l&ae;ten his abbotrice for &t;&ae;t micele unsibbe &t;&ae;t w&ae;s on &t;&ae;t land. &amp; &t;&ae;t he dide &d;urh &t;es papes r&ae;d &amp; leue of Rome. &amp; &d;urh &t;es abbotes of Clunni. &amp; &t;urh &t;&ae;t he w&ae;s legat of &d;one Rome scott. 
 Oc hit ne w&ae;s na&d;ema eallswa. oc he wolde hauen ba&d;e on hand. &amp; swa hafde swa lange swa Godes wille w&ae;s. 
 He w&ae;s on his cl&ae;rchade biscop on Scesscuns. si&d;&d;an war&d; he munec on Clunni. &amp; si&d;&d;on prior on &t;one seolue minstre. &amp; si&d;&d;on he w&ae;r&d; prior on Sauenni. 
 &T;ar&ae;ftor &t;urh &t;&ae;t he w&ae;s &d;es kynges m&ae;i of Engleland &amp; &t;es eorles of Peitowe &t;a geaf se eorl him &t;one abbotrice of Sancti Johannis minstre of Angeli. 
 Si&d;&d;on &t;urh his micele wrences &d;a bei&ae;t he &t;one &ae;rcebiscoprice of Besencun &amp; h&ae;fde hit &t;a on hande &t;re dagas. &t;a forl&ae;s he &t;&ae;t mid rihte for&t;i &t;&ae;t he hit h&ae;fde &ae;ror beieten mid unrihte. 
 Si&d;&d;on &t;a beiet he &t;one biscoprice of Seintes &t;&ae;t w&ae;s fif mile fram his abbotrice &t;&ae;t he h&ae;fde fulneah seoueniht on hande. &t;enon brohte se abbot him of Clunni swa swa he &ae;ror dide of Besencun. 
 &T;a be&t;ohte he him &t;&ae;t gif he mihte ben rotfest on Engleland &t;&ae;t he mihte habben eal his wille. 
 Besohte &t;a &d;one kyng &amp; s&ae;ide him &t;&ae;t he w&ae;s eald man &amp; forbroken man  &amp; &t;&ae;t he ne mihte &d;olen &t;a micele unrihte &amp; &t;a micele unsibbe &d;a w&ae;ron on here land. 
 &amp; i&ae;rnde &t;a &t;urh him &amp; &d;urh ealle his freond namcu&d;lice &t;one abbotrice of Burhc  &amp; se kyng hit him i&ae;tte for&d;i &t;&ae;t he w&ae;s his m&ae;i. &amp; for&t;i &t;&ae;t he w&ae;s an h&ae;fod &d;a a&d; to swerene &amp; witnesse to berene &t;&ae;r &d;a eorles sunu of Normandi &amp; &t;es eorles dohter of Angeow w&ae;ron totwemde for sibreden. 
 &T;us earmlice w&ae;s &t;one abbotrice gifen betwix Cristesmesse &amp; Candelmesse at Lundene. 
 &amp; swa he ferde mid &t;e cyng to Wincestre &amp; &t;anon he com to Burch. &amp; &t;&ae;r he wunede eallriht swa drane do&d; on hiue. 
 Eall &t;&ae;t &t;a beon dragen toward swa frett &t;a drane &amp; draga&d; fraward. 
 Swa dide he eall &t;&ae;t he mihte tacen wi&d;innen &amp; wi&d;uten of l&ae;red &amp; of l&ae;wed swa he sende ouer s&ae; &amp; na god &t;&ae;r ne dide. ne na god &d;&ae;r ne l&ae;uede. 
 Ne &t;ince man na sellice &t;&ae;t we so&d; seggen for hit w&ae;s ful cu&d; ofer eall land &t;&ae;t swa radlice swa he &t;&ae;r com &t;&ae;t w&ae;s &t;es Sunend&ae;ies &t;&ae;t man singa&d; EXURGE QUARE O. D. &t;a son &t;&ae;r &ae;fter &t;a s&ae;gon &amp; herdon fela men feole huntes hunten. 
 &D;a huntes w&ae;ron swarte &amp; micele &amp; ladlice. &amp; here hundes ealle swarte &amp; bradegede &amp; ladlice. &amp; hi ridone on swarte hors &amp; on swarte bucces. 
 &T;is w&ae;s segon on &t;e selue derfald in &t;a tune on Burch &amp; on ealle &t;a wudes &d;a w&ae;ron fram &t;a selua tune to Stanforde. &amp; &t;a muneces herdon &d;a horn blawen &t;&ae;t hi blewen on nihtes. 
 So&d;festemen heom kepten on nihtes. s&ae;idon &t;es &t;e heom &t;uhte &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;r mihte wel ben abuton twenti o&d;er &t;ritti hornblaweres. 
 &T;is w&ae;s s&ae;gon &amp; herd fram &t;&ae;t he &t;ider com eall &t;&ae;t lentedtid on an to Eastren. 
 &T;is was his ingang. of his utgang ne cunne we iett noht seggon. 
 God scawe fore. 
 Eall &t;is geare weas se kyng Heanri on Normandi for &t;one unfri&d; &t;&ae;t w&ae;s betwenen him &amp; his nefe &d;one eorl of Flandres. 
 Oc se eorl wear&d; gewunded at an gefiht fram anne swein. 
 &amp; swa gewundod he for to Sancte Berhtines minstre. &amp; sone &t;ear wear&d; munec &amp; liuode si&d;&d;on fif dagas. &amp; he wear&d; &t;a d&ae;d &amp; &t;&ae;r bebyriged. 
 God geare his sawle. 
 &T;&ae;t w&ae;s &d;es daies vi kalend&ae; Augusti. 
 &D;es ilces geares for&d;ferde se biscop Randulf Passeflambard of Dunholme. &amp; &t;&ae;re bebyriged on Non&ae; Septembris. 
 &amp; &t;es ilces geares ferde se forensprecene abbot Henri ham to his agen minstre to Peitou be &t;es kynges leue. 
 He dide &d;one king to understanden &t;&ae;t he wolde mid alle forl&ae;ten &t;one minstre &amp; &t;&ae;t land &amp; &t;&ae;r wunien mid him on Englalande. &amp; on &d;one mynstre of Burh. 
 Oc hit ne was na&d;ema swa. he hit dide for&d;i &t;&ae;t he wolde &t;urh his micele wiles &d;&ae;r beon w&ae;r it tweolf mon&d; o&d;&d;e mare. &amp; si&d;&d;on ongeon cumen. 
 God &ae;lmihtig haue his milce ofer &t;&ae;t wrecce stede. 
 &D;es ilces geares com fram Ierusalem Hugo of &t;e temple to &d;one kyng on Normandig. &amp; se kyng him underfeng mid micel wur&d;scipe. 
 &amp; micele gersumes him geaf on gold &amp; on silure. &amp; si&d;&d;on he sende him to Englalande. 
 &amp; &t;&ae;r he w&ae;s underfangen of ealle gode men. &amp; ealle him geauen gersume &amp; on Scotlande ealswa. &amp; be him senden to Ierusalem micel eahte mid ealle on gold &amp; on silure. 
 &amp; he bebead folc vt to Ierusalem. &amp; &t;a for mid him &amp; &ae;fter him swa micel folc swa n&ae;fre &ae;r ne dide si&d;&d;on &t;&ae;t se firste fare was on Vrbanes d&ae;i pape &t;eah hit litel behelde. 
 He seide &t;&ae;t fulle feoht was sett betwenen &d;a Cristene &amp; &t;a he&d;ene. 
 &T;a hi &t;ider comon &d;a ne was hit noht buton l&ae;sunge. &t;us earmlice wear&d; eall &t;&ae;t folc swengt. 
 On &d;is gear sende se kyng to Englaland &ae;fter &t;one eorl Waleram. &amp; &ae;fter Hugo Gerueises sunu. &amp; &t;&ae;r hi gisleden hem. 
 &amp; Hugo ferde ham to his agen land to France. &amp; Waleram belaf mid &t;one kyng. &amp; se kyng him geaf eall his land buton his castel ane. 
 Si&d;&d;on &t;a com se kyng to Englaland innon heruest. &amp; se eorl com mid him. &amp; wur&d;on &t;a alswa gode freond swa hi w&ae;ron &ae;ror feond. 
 &D;a sone be &t;es kynges r&ae;d &amp; be his leue sende se &ae;rcebiscop Willelm of Cantwarbyrig ofer eall Englaland. &amp; bead biscopes &amp; abbotes &amp; &ae;rced&ae;cnes. &amp; ealle &t;a priores muneces &amp; canonias &t;a w&ae;ron on ealle &t;a cellas on Englaland. &amp; &ae;fter ealle &t;a &t;et Cristendome h&ae;fdon to begemen &amp; to locen. &amp; &t;&ae;t hi scolden ealle cumen to Lundene at Michaeles messe. &amp; &t;&ae;r scolden sprecon of ealle Godes rihtes. 
 &T;a hi &d;ider comen &t;a began &t;&ae;t mot on Monend&ae;ig &amp; heold on an to &d;e Frid&ae;ig. 
 &T;a hit eall com for&d;  &t;a weor&d; hit eall of earced&ae;cnes wifes &amp; of preostes wifes &t;&ae;t hi scolden hi forl&ae;ten be sanctus Andreas messe. &amp; se &t;e &t;&ae;t ne wolden done forgede his circe &amp; his hus &amp; his ham &amp; nefra ma nan clepunge &t;&ae;rto na hafde mare. 
 &T;is beb&ae;d se &ae;rcebiscop Willelm of Cantwarabyrig &amp; ealle &t;a leodbiscopes &d;a &t;a w&ae;ron on Englalande. 
 &amp; se kyng hem geaf ealle leue ham to farene. &amp; swa hi ferdon ham. 
 &amp; ne forstod noht ealle &t;a bodlaces. ealle heoldon here wifes be &t;es kynges leue swa swa hi ear didon. 
 &D;is ilces geares for&d;ferde se biscop Willelm Giffard of Winceastre &amp; &t;ear bebyriged on viii kalend&ae; Februarii. 
 &amp; se kyng Henri geaf &t;one biscoprice &ae;fter Micheles messe &t;one abbot Henri his nefe of Glastingbyri. 
 &amp; he w&ae;s gehalgod to biscop fram &t;one &ae;rcebiscop Willelm of Cantwarabyri &t;es d&ae;ies xv kalend&ae; Decembris. 
 &T;es ilces geares for&d;ferde Honorius papa. 
 &AE;r he w&ae;re wel ded. &t;a w&ae;re &t;&ae;r coren twa papes. 
 Se an w&ae;s gehaten Petrus. he w&ae;s munec of Clunni. &amp; weas boren of &t;a ricceste men of Rome. 
 Mid him helden &d;a of Rome. &amp; se duc of Sicilie. 
 Se o&d;er het Gregorius. he w&ae;s clerc &amp; w&ae;rd flemd ut of Rome fram &t;on o&d;er pape &amp; fram his cinnesmen. 
 Mid him held se Kasere of Sexlande &amp; se kyng of France &amp; se kyng Heanri of Engleland. &amp; ealle &t;a be &t;is half &t;a muntes. 
 Nu w&ae;r&d; swa mycel dwyld on Cristendom swa it n&ae;fre &ae;r ne w&ae;s. 
 Crist sette red for his wrecce folc. 
 &D;is ilces geares on Sancti Nicholaes messeniht litel &ae;r d&ae;i w&ae;s micel eor&d;dine. 
 &D;is geares w&ae;s se mynstre of Cantwarabyri halgod fram &t;one &ae;rcebiscop Willelm &t;es d&ae;ies iiii Non&ae; MAI. 
 &D;&ae;r w&ae;ron &t;as biscopes. Iohan of Roueceastre. Gilbert Uniuersal of Lundene. Heanri of Winceastre. Alexander of Lincolne. Roger of S&ae;resbyri. Simon of Wigorceastre. Roger of Couentre. Godefreith of Bathe. Eourard of Noruuic. Sigefrid of Cicaestre. Bernard of Sancti Dauid. Audoenus of Euereus of Normandige Iohan of S&ae;is. 
 &D;es feor&d;e d&ae;ges &t;&ae;r&ae;fter w&ae;s se king Heanri on Roueceastre. &amp; se burch forbernde &ae;lm&ae;st. 
 &amp; se &ae;rcebiscop Willelm halgede Sancti Andreas mynstre &amp; &d;a forsprecon biscop mid him. 
 &amp; se kyng Heanri ferde ouer s&ae; into Normandi on heruest. 
 &D;es ilces geares com se abbot Heanri of Angeli &ae;fter &ae;sterne to Burch. &amp; seide &t;&ae;t he h&ae;fde forl&ae;ten &t;one mynstre mid ealle. 
 &AE;fter him com se abbot of Clunni Petrus gehaten to Englelande bi &t;es kynges leue &amp; w&ae;s underfangen ouer eall swa hwar swa he com mid mycel wur&d;scipe. 
 To Burch he com &amp; &t;&ae;r behet se abbot Heanri him &t;&ae;t he scolde beieton him &t;one mynstre of Burch &t;&ae;t hit scolde beon under&d;ed into Clunni. 
 Oc man sei&d; to biworde. h&ae;ge sitte&d; &t;a aceres d&ae;leth. 
 God &ae;lmihtig adylege iuele r&ae;de. 
 &amp; sone &t;&ae;r&ae;fter ferde se abbot of Clunni ham to his &ae;rde. 
 &D;is gear &ae;fter Cristesmesse on an Moneniht &ae;t &t;e forme sl&ae;p w&ae;s se heouene o &d;e nor&d; half eallswilc hit w&ae;re b&ae;rnende fir. swa &t;&ae;t ealle &d;e hit s&ae;gon w&ae;ron swa off&ae;red swa hi n&ae;fre &ae;r ne w&ae;ron. &t;&ae;t w&ae;s on iii IDus Ianuarii. 
 &D;es ilces geares w&ae;s swa micel orfcwalm swa hit n&ae;fre &ae;r ne w&ae;s on manne gemynd ofer eall Engleland. 
 &T;&ae;t w&ae;s on n&ae;t &amp; on swin. swa &t;&ae;t on &t;a tun &t;a w&ae;s tenn ploges o&d;er twelfe gangende ne bel&ae;f &t;&ae;r noht an. &amp; se man &t;a heafde twa hundred o&d;&t;e &d;re hundred swin ne beleaf him noht an. 
 &T;&ae;r&ae;fter swulten &t;a henne fugeles. &t;a scyrte &d;a flescmete &amp; se ceose &amp; se butere . 
 God hit bete &t;a his wille be&d;. 
 &amp; se kyng Heanri com ham to Engleland toforen heruest &ae;fter Sancti Petres messe &t;e firrer. 
 &D;es ilces geares for se abbot Heanri toforen Eastren fram Burch ofer s&ae; to Normandi &amp; &t;&ae;r spreac mid &t;one kyng. 
 &amp; s&ae;ide him &t;et se abbot of Clunni heafde him beboden &t;&ae;t he scolde cumen to him &amp; bet&ae;cen him &t;one abbotrice of Angeli. &amp; si&d;&t;en he wolde cumen ham be his l&ae;fe. 
 &amp; swa he ferde ham to his agen mynstre &amp; &t;&ae;r wunode eall to midsumerd&ae;i. 
 &amp; &d;es o&d;er d&ae;ies &ae;fter Sancti Iohannes messed&ae;i. cusen &t;a muneces abbot of hem self and brohten him into cyrce mid processionem. sungen Te Deum Laudamus. ringden &t;a belle. setten him on &t;es abbotes settle. diden him ealle hersumnesse swa swa hi scolden don here abbot. 
 &amp; se eorl &amp; ealle &t;a heafedmenn &amp; &t;a muneces of &t;a mynstre flemden se o&t;er abbot Heanri ut of &t;a mynstre. 
 Hi scolden nedes. on fif &amp; twenti wintre ne biden hi n&ae;fre an god d&ae;i. 
 Her him trucode ealle his mycele cr&ae;ftes. nu him behofed &t;&ae;t he crape in his mycele codde in &ae;lc hyrne gif &t;&ae;r w&ae;re hure an unwreste wrenc &t;&ae;t he mihte get beswicen anes Crist &amp; eall Cristene folc. 
 &T;a ferde he into Clunni &amp; &t;&ae;r man him held &t;&ae;t he ne mihte na east na west. 
 S&ae;ide se abbot of Clunni &t;&ae;t hi heafdon forloron Sancti Iohannes mynstre &t;urh him &amp; &t;urh his mycele sotscipe. 
 &T;a ne cu&t;e he him na betre bote bute behet hem &amp; a&d;es swor on halidom &t;&ae;t gif he moste Engleland secen &t;et he scolde begeton hem &d;one mynstre of Burch. swa &t;&ae;t he scolde setten &t;&ae;r prior of Clunni &amp; circeweard &amp; hordere &amp; reil&t;ein &amp; ealle &t;a &d;ing &t;a w&ae;ron wi&d;inne mynstre &amp; wi&d;uten eall he scolde hem bet&ae;cen. 
 &T;us he ferde into France &amp; &t;&ae;r wunode eall &t;&ae;t gear. 
 Crist r&ae;de for &t;a wrecce muneces of Burch &amp; for &t;&ae;t wrecee stede. 
 Nu hem behofe&d; Cristes helpe &amp; eall Cristenes folces. 
 &D;is gear com Henri king to &t;is land. 
 &T;a com Henri abbot &amp; uureide &t;e muneces of Burch to &t;e king for&t;i &d;&ae;t he uuolde under&t;eden &d;&ae;t mynstre to Clunie. sua &d;&ae;t te king was welneh bepaht. &amp; sende efter &t;e muneces. 
 &amp; &t;urh Godes milce &amp; &t;urh &t;e biscop of Seresberi &amp; te biscop of Lincol &amp; te o&t;re ricemen &t;e &t;er w&ae;ron &t;a wiste &t;e king &d;&ae;t he feorde mid suicdom. 
 &T;a he nanmor ne mihte. &t;a uuolde he &d;&ae;t his nefe sculde ben abbod in Burch. oc Crist it ne uuolde. 
 Was it noht suithe lang &t;er efter &t;atte king sende efter him. &amp; dide him gyuen up &d;&ae;t abbodrice of Burch &amp; faren ut of lande. 
 &amp; te king iaf &d;&ae;t abbodrice an prior of Sancti Neod Martin was gehaten. 
 He com on Sancti PETRES messedei mid micel wurscipe into the minstre. 
 On &t;is g&ae;re for se king Henri ouer s&ae; &ae;t te Lammasse. 
 &amp; &d;&ae;t o&t;er dei &t;a he lai an slep in scip. &t;a &t;estrede &t;e d&ae;i ouer al landes  &amp; uuard &t;e sunne suilc als it uuare threniht ald mone. an sterres abuten him at midd&ae;i. 
 Wur&t;en men sui&d;e ofuundred &amp; ofdred  &amp; s&ae;den &d;&ae;t micel &t;ing sculde cumen herefter. sua dide. for &t;at ilc g&ae;r warth &t;e king ded. &d;&ae;t o&t;er d&ae;i efter Sancti Andreas massed&ae;i on Normandi. 
 &T;a &t;estreden sona &t;as landes. for &ae;uric man sone r&ae;uede o&t;er &t;e mihte. 
 &T;a namen his sune &amp; his frend &amp; brohten his lic to Englelande &amp; bebiriend in Redinge. 
 God man he wes &amp; micel &ae;ie wes of him. 
 Durste nan man misdon wi&d; o&d;er on his time. 
 Pais he makede men &amp; d&ae;r. 
 Wua sua bare his byrthen gold &amp; sylure. durste nan man sei to him naht bute god. 
 Enmang &t;is was his nefe cumen to Englelande Stephne de Blais. &amp; com to Lundene. 
 &amp; te Lundenisce folc him underfeng. &amp; senden &ae;fter &t;e &ae;rcebiscop Willelm Curbuil  &amp; halechede him to kinge on midewintred&ae;i. 
 On &t;is kinges time wes al unfri&d; &amp; yfel &amp; r&ae;flac. for agenes him risen sona &t;a rice men &t;e w&ae;ron swikes. 
 Alre fyrst Balduin de Reduers &amp; held Execestre agenes him. &amp; te king it bes&ae;t. &amp; si&d;&d;an Balduin acordede. 
 &T;a tocan &t;a o&d;re &amp; helden her castles agenes him. 
 &amp; Dauid king of Scotland toc to uuerrien him. 
 &T;a &t;ohuuethere &t;at here sandes feorden betwyx heom. &amp; hi tog&ae;dere comen &amp; wur&d;e s&ae;hte. &t;o&t; it litel forstode. 
 &D;is g&ae;re for &t;e king Stephne ofer s&ae; to Normandi &amp; ther wes underfangen for&t;i &d;&ae;t hi uuenden &d;&ae;t he sculde ben alsuic alse the eom wes. &amp; for he hadde get his tresor. ac he todeld it &amp; scatered sotlice. 
 Micel hadde Henri king gadered gold &amp; syluer. &amp; na god ne dide me for his saule thar of. 
 &T;a &t;e king Stephne to Englalande com &t;a macod he his gadering &ae;t Oxeneford. 
 &amp; &t;ar he nam &t;e biscop Roger of Sereberi &amp; Alexander biscop of Lincol &amp; te Canceler Roger hise neues. &amp; dide &ae;lle in prisun. til hi iafen up here castles. 
 &T;a the suikes underg&ae;ton &d;&ae;t he milde man was &amp; softe &amp; god. &amp; na iustise ne dide. &t;a diden hi alle wunder. 
 Hi hadden him manred maked &amp; athes suoren. ac hi nan treuthe ne heolden. 
 Alle he w&ae;ron forsworen &amp; here treothes forloren. for &ae;uric rice man his castles makede &amp; ag&ae;nes him heolden. &amp; fylden &t;e land ful of castles. 
 Hi suencten suy&d;e &t;e uurecce men of &t;e land mid castelweorces &t;a &t;e castles uuaren maked &t;a fylden hi mid deoules &amp; yuele men. 
 &T;a namen hi &t;a men &t;e hi wenden &d;&ae;t ani god hefden. bathe be nihtes &amp; be d&ae;ies. carlmen &amp; wimmen. &amp; diden heom in prisun efter gold &amp; syluer. &amp; pined heom. untellendlice pining. for ne uu&ae;ren n&ae;ure nan martyrs swa pined alse hi w&ae;ron. 
 Me henged up bi the fet &amp; smoked heom. mid ful smoke. 
 Me henged bi the &t;umbes. other bi the hefed. &amp; hengen bryniges on her fet. 
 Me dide cnotted strenges abuton here h&ae;ued. &amp; uurythen to &d;&ae;t it g&ae;de to &t;e h&ae;rnes. 
 Hi dyden heom in quarterne &t;ar nadres &amp; snakes &amp; pades w&ae;ron inne. &amp; drapen heom swa. 
 Sume hi diden in crucethus &d;&ae;t is in an c&ae;ste &t;at was scort &amp; nareu. &amp; un dep. &amp; dide sc&ae;rpe stanes &t;erinne. &amp; &t;rengde &t;e man &t;&ae;rinne. &d;&ae;t him br&ae;con alle &t;e limes. 
 In mani of &t;e castles w&ae;ron lof &amp; grin. &d;&ae;t w&ae;ron rachenteges &d;&ae;t twa o&t;er thre men hadden onoh to b&ae;ron onne. 
 &T;at was sua maced. &d;&ae;t is f&ae;stned to an beom. &amp; diden an sc&ae;rp iren abuton &t;a mannes throte &amp; his hals. &d;&ae;t he ne myhte nowiderwardes. ne sitten ne lien ne slepen. oc b&ae;ron al &d;&ae;t iren. 
 Mani &t;usen hi drapen mid hung&ae;r. 
 I ne can ne i ne mai tellen alle &t;e wunder ne alle &t;e pines &d;&ae;t hi diden wreccemen on &t;is land. &amp; &d;&ae;t lastede &t;a xix wintre wile Stephne was king &amp; &ae;ure it was uuerse &amp; uuerse. 
 Hi l&ae;iden g&ae;ildes on the tunes &ae;ure um wile &amp; clepeden it tenserie. 
 &T;a &t;e uurecce men ne hadden nan more to gyuen. &t;a r&ae;ueden hi &amp; brendon alle the tunes. &d;&ae;t wel &t;u myhtes faren all ad&ae;is fare sculdest thu neure finden man in tune sittende. ne land tiled. 
 &T;a was corn d&ae;re. &amp; flec &amp; c&ae;se &amp; butere. for nan ne w&ae;s o &t;e land. 
 Wreccemen sturuen of hung&ae;r. sume ieden on &ae;lmes &t;e waren sum wile ricemen. sume flugen ut of lande. 
 Wes n&ae;ure g&ae;t mare wreccehed on land. ne n&ae;ure hethen men werse ne diden &t;an hi diden. 
 For ouersithon ne forbaren hi nouther circe ne cyrcei&ae;rd. oc namen al &t;e god &d;&ae;t &t;arinne was. &amp; brenden sythen &t;e cyrce &amp; alteg&ae;dere. 
 Ne hi ne forbaren biscop land ne abbod ne preostes. ac r&ae;ueden munekes &amp; clerekes. &amp; &ae;uric man other &t;e ouermyhte. 
 Gif twa men o&t;er iii coman ridend to an tun. al &t;e tunscipe flug&ae;n for heom. wenden &d;&ae;t hi w&ae;ron r&ae;ueres. 
 &T;e biscopes &amp; lered men heom cursede &ae;ure. oc was heom naht &t;ar of. for hi uueron al forcurs&ae;d &amp; forsuoren &amp; forloren. 
 Wars&ae; me tilede. &t;e erthe ne bar nan corn. for &t;e land was al fordon. mid suilce d&ae;des. &amp; hi s&ae;den openlice &d;&ae;t Crist slep. &amp; his halechen. 
 Suilc &amp; mare &t;anne we cunnen s&ae;in. we &t;olenden xix wintre for ure sinnes. 
 On al &t;is yuele time heold Martin abbot his abbotrice xx wintre &amp; half g&ae;r &amp; viii d&ae;is. mid micel suinc. 
 &amp; fand &t;e munekes &amp; te gestes al &t;at heom be houed &amp; heold mycel carited in the hus. 
 &amp; &t;o&t;wethere wrohte on &t;e circe &amp; sette &t;arto landes &amp; rentes. &amp; goded it suythe. 
 &amp; l&ae;t it refen &amp; brohte heom into &t;e neuu&ae; mynstre on Sancti PETRES m&ae;ssed&ae;i mid micel wurtscipe. &d;&ae;t was anno ab incarnatione Domini Mcxl. a combustione loci xxiii. 
 &amp; he for to Rome. &amp; &t;&ae;r w&ae;s w&ae;l underfangen fram &t;e pape Eugenie. 
 &amp; beg&ae;t thare priuilegies. an of alle &t;e landes of &t;abbotrice. &amp; an o&t;er of &t;e landes &t;e lien to &t;e circewican. &amp; gif he leng moste liuen  alse he mint to don of &t;e horderwycan. 
 &amp; he beg&ae;t in landes &t;at ricemen hefden mid strengthe. 
 Of Willelm Malduit &t;e heold Rogingham &t;&ae; castel. he wan Cotingham &amp; Estun. &amp; of Hugo of Walteuile he uuan Hyrtlingberi. &amp; Stanewig. &amp; lx  soluti of Aldewingle &ae;lc g&ae;r. 
 &amp; he makede manie munekes &amp; plantede wini&ae;rd. &amp; makede mani weorkes. &amp; wende &t;e tun betere &t;an it &ae;r w&ae;s. &amp; w&ae;s god munec &amp; god man. &amp; for&t;i ham luueden God &amp; gode men. 
 Nu we willen s&ae;gen sumdel wat belamp on Stephnes kinges time. 
 On his time &t;e Iudeus of Noruuic bohton an christen cild beforen Estren  &amp; pineden him alle &t;e ilce pining &d;&ae;t ure Drihten was pined. 
 &amp; on lang frid&ae;i him on rode hengen for ure Drihtines luue. &amp; sythen byrieden him. 
 Wenden &d;&ae;t it sculde ben forholen. oc ure Dryhtin atywede &d;&ae;t he was hali martyr. 
 &amp; to munekes him namen. &amp; bebyried him heglice in &t;e minstre. 
 &amp; he maket &t;ur ure Drihtin wunderlice &amp; manif&ae;ldlice miracles &amp; hatte he Sancti Willelm. 
 On &t;is g&ae;r com Dauid king of Scotlande mid ormete f&ae;rd to &t;is land. wolde winnan &t;is land. 
 &amp; him com tog&ae;nes Willelm eorl of Albamar &t;e &t;e king adde beteht Euorwic &amp; to other &ae;uez men mid f&ae;u men &amp; fuhten wid heom. &amp; flemden &t;e king &ae;t te Standard. &amp; sloghen suithe micel of his genge. 
 On &t;is g&ae;r wolde &t;e king Stephne t&ae;cen Rodbert eorl of Gloucestre &t;e kinges sune Henries. ac he ne myhte for he wart it war. 
 &T;erefter in &t;e lengten &t;estrede &t;e sunne &amp; te d&ae;i. abuton nontid d&ae;ies. &t;a men eten. &d;&ae;t me lihtede candles to &ae;ten bi. 
 &amp; &t;at was xiii kalend&ae; Aprilis. w&ae;ron men suythe ofwundred. 
 &T;erefter fordfeorde Willelm &ae;rcebiscop of Cantwarberi. &amp; te king makede Teodbald &ae;rcebiscop &t;e was abbot in the Bec. 
 &T;erefter w&ae;x suythe micel uuerre betuyx &t;e king &amp; Randolf eorl of C&ae;stre noht for&t;i &d;&ae;t he ne iaf him al &d;&ae;t he cuthe axen him. alse he dide alle othre. oc &ae;fre &t;e mare he iaf heom. &t;e w&ae;rse hi w&ae;ron him. 
 &T;e eorl heold Lincol ag&ae;nes &t;e king. &amp; benam him al &d;&ae;t he ahte to hauen. 
 &amp; te king for &t;ider. &amp; bes&ae;tte him &amp; his brother Willelm de Romare in &t;e castel. 
 &amp; te &ae;orl st&ae;l ut &amp; ferde efter Rodbert eorl of Gloucestre. &amp; brohte him &t;ider mid micel ferd. 
 &amp; fuhten suythe on Candelmassed&ae;i agenes heore lauerd. &amp; namen him  for his men him suyken &amp; flug&ae;n. &amp; l&ae;d him to Bristowe &amp; diden &t;ar in prisun. &amp; feteres. 
 &T;a was al Engleland styred mar &t;an &ae;r w&ae;s. &amp; al uyel w&ae;s in lande. 
 &T;erefter com &t;e kynges dohter Henries &t;e hefde ben Emperice in Alamanie. &amp; nu w&ae;s cuntesse in Angou. 
 &amp; com to Lundene &amp; te Lundenissce folc hire wolde t&ae;cen. &amp; sc&ae; fleh &amp; forles &t;ar micel. 
 &T;erefter &t;e biscop of Wincestre Henri &t;e kinges brother Stephnes spac wid Rodbert eorl &amp; wyd &t;emperice &amp; suor heom athas &d;&ae;t he neure ma mid te king his brother wolde halden. &amp; cursede alle &t;e men &t;e mid him heoldon. 
 &amp; s&ae;de heom &d;&ae;t he uuolde iiuen heom up Wincestre. &amp; dide heom cumen &t;ider. 
 &T;a hi &t;&ae;r inne w&ae;ren. &t;a com &t;e kinges cuen mid al hire strengthe. &amp; bes&ae;t heom. &d;&ae;t &t;er w&ae;s inne micel hung&ae;r. 
 &T;a hi ne leng ne muhten &t;olen &t;a stali hi ut &amp; flugen. &amp; hi wurthen war widuten &amp; folecheden heom. 
 &amp; namen Rodbert eorl of Gloucestre. &amp; ledden him to Rouecestre. &amp; diden him &t;are in prisun. &amp; te emperice fleh into an minstre. 
 &T;a feorden &t;e wise men betwyx &t;e kinges freond &amp; te eorles freond. &amp; sahtlede sua &d;&ae;t me sculde leten ut &t;e king of prisun for &t;e eorl. &amp; te eorl for &t;e king. &amp; sua diden. 
 Sithen &t;erefter sahtleden &t;e king &amp; Randolf eorl at Stanford. &amp; athes suoren &amp; treuthes f&ae;ston &d;&ae;t her nou&t;er sculde besuiken other. 
 &amp; it ne forstod naht. for &t;e king him sithen nam in Hamtun. &t;urhc wicci r&ae;d. &amp; dide him in prisun. 
 &amp; efsones he let him ut &t;urhc w&ae;rse red. to &d;&ae;t forewarde &d;&ae;t he suor on halidom &amp; gysles fand. &t;at he alle his castles sculde iiuen up. 
 Sume he iaf up  &amp; sume ne iaf he noht. &amp; dide &t;anne w&ae;rse &t;anne he h&ae;r sculde. 
 &T;a was Engleland suythe todeled. sume helden mid te king. &amp; sume mid &t;emperice. 
 For &t;a &t;e king was in prisun &t;a wenden &t;e eorles &amp; te rice men &t;at he neure mare sculde cumen ut. &amp; s&ae;htleden wyd &t;emperice. &amp; brohten hire into Oxenford. 
 &amp; iauen hire &t;e burch. 
 &T;a &t;e king was ute &t;a herde &d;&ae;t s&ae;gen. &amp; toc his feord &amp; bes&ae;t hire in &t;e tur. 
 &amp; me l&ae;t hire dun on niht of &t;e tur mid rapes. &amp; stal ut. &amp; sc&ae; fleh &amp; i&ae;de on fote to Walingford. 
 &T;&ae;refter sc&ae; ferde ouer s&ae;. 
 &amp; hi of Normandi wenden alle fra &t;e king. to &t;e eorl of Ang&ae;u. sume here &t;ankes &amp; sume here un&t;ankes. for he bes&ae;t heom til hi aiauen up here castles. &amp; hi nan helpe ne h&ae;fden of &t;e kinge. 
 &T;a ferde Eustace &t;e kinges sune to France &amp; nam &t;e kinges suster of France to wife. 
 Wende to big&ae;ton Normandi &t;&ae;r &t;urh. oc he spedde litel. &amp; be gode rihte for he was an yuel man. 
 For ware se he com he dide mare yuel &t;anne god. he reuede &t;e landes &amp; l&ae;ide micele gildes on. 
 He brohte his wif to Engleland. &amp; dide hire in &t;e castel on Canteberi. 
 God wimman sc&ae; w&ae;s. oc sc&ae; hedde litel blisse mid him. 
 &amp; Crist ne wolde &d;&ae;t he sculde lange rixan. &amp; w&ae;rd ded &amp; his moder beien. 
 &amp; te eorl of Ang&ae;u w&ae;rd ded. &amp; his sune Henri toc to &t;e rice. 
 &amp; te cuen of France tod&ae;lde fra &t;e king. &amp; sc&ae; com to &t;e iunge eorl Henr&e;. &amp; he toc hire to wiue. &amp; al Peitou mid hire. 
 &T;a ferde he mid micel f&ae;rd into Engleland. &amp; wan castles. 
 &amp; te king ferde agenes him mid micel mare ferd. &amp; &t;o&t;w&ae;there fuhtten hi noht. oc ferden &t;e &ae;rcebiscop &amp; te wise men betwux heom. &amp; makede &d;&ae;t sahte &d;&ae;t te king sculde ben lauerd &amp; king wile he liuede. &amp; &ae;fter his d&ae;i ware Henri king. &amp; he helde him for fader &amp; he him for sune. &amp; sib &amp; s&ae;hte sculde ben betwyx heom. &amp; on al Engleland. 
 &T;is &amp; te othre foruuardes &t;et hi makeden. suoren to halden &t;e king &amp; te eorl &amp; te biscop &amp; te eorles &amp; rice men alle. 
 &T;a was &t;e eorl underfangen &ae;t Wincestre &amp; &ae;t Lundene mid micel wurtscipe. 
 &amp; alle diden him manred. &amp; suoren &t;e pais to halden. 
 &amp; hit ward sone suythe god pais. sua &d;&ae;t neure was here. 
 &T;a was &t;e king strengere &t;anne he &ae;uert her was. &amp; te eorl ferde ouer s&ae;. &amp; al folc him luuede for he dide god iustise &amp; makede pais. 
 On &t;is g&ae;r w&ae;rd &t;e king Stephne ded &amp; bebyried &t;er. his wif &amp; his sune w&ae;ron bebyried &ae;t Fauresfeld. &t;&ae;t minster hi makeden. 
 &T;a &t;e king was ded. &t;a was &t;e eorl beionde s&ae;. &amp; ne durste nan man don o&t;er bute god for &t;e micel eie of him. 
 &T;a he to Engleland com. &t;a was he underfangen mid micel wurtscipe. &amp; to king bletc&ae;d in Lundene on &t;e sunnen d&ae;i beforen midwinter d&ae;i. &amp; held &t;&ae;r micel curt. 
 &T;at ilce d&ae;i &t;at Martin abbod of Burch sculde &t;ider faren. &t;a s&ae;clede he &amp; ward ded iiii Non&ae; Ianuarii. 
 &amp; te munekes innen d&ae;is cusen o&t;er of heom s&ae;lf. Willelm de Walteuile is gehaten. god clerc &amp; god man. &amp; w&ae;l luued of &t;e kinge &amp; of alle gode men. 
 &amp; on cyricen byrieden &t;abbot hehlice; &amp; sone &t;e cosan abbod ferde &amp; te muneces mid him to Oxenforde to &t;e king &amp; he iaf him &t;at abbodrice. 
 &amp; he ferde him sone to Lincol &amp; was &t;&ae;r bletc&ae;d to abbot &ae;r he ham come. 
 &amp; sithen was underfangen mid micel wurtscipe at Burch. mid micel processiun. 
 &amp; sua he was alsua at Rames&ae;ie. &amp; at Torn. &amp; at &amp; Spall &amp; at Sancte I. beres. 
 &amp; nu is abbot. &amp; fair haued begunnon. Cristes him unne.
